Welcome!

Hello and welcome to The Unofficial Neopian FAQ! This is a semi-comprehensive list of significant Frequently Asked Questions covering numerous topics of Neopia, including, but not limited to, ticket support, event information, and more!

Before May 15th, 2018, the official FAQ and ticket system were hosted on Parature which subsequently closed down leaving those resources to their support address. Back then, you could have searched up the FAQ questions, but all the answers were unavailable and possibly outdated with the ongoing editorial.

As of November 17, 2020, the official FAQ has returned! However, there are parts of the official FAQ that is not current with the Editorials, social media Q&As, and other places of where official discussion was made. I am still working and wishing to complete this guide, but I will need your support on creating this community-sourced quick reference guide, SO WE CAN FIGURE OUT HOW TO PLAY THIS GAME. :D

The FAQs are divided into a general section, an other section, and the NeoBoard Topics to fit their closest related specification. The navigation can be found on the right-hand side of this petpage and as a tip, you can search terms using CTRL-F for quick convenience. We are unable to provide a concise answer to every query, but we hope this might lead you to the right direction.

If you have any questions, suggestions, or other comments, please contact Chips!

██████████████████████████████████████ Last Updated: Jan 17th, 2022


General FAQs

▸ Will my Neopets die if I don't feed them?
Your Neopets can't die so no worries if it's been a few years. They're just starving and sobbing uncontrollably is all.

▸ I just came back to the site. What changed over the years?
Tons of things have changed! We would refer you to check out these resources:

Hiatus Rescue Kits
/~Kaps (2014 - Present)
/~WhatWentOn (2014 - May 2020)
/~ArentIPretty (2005 - 2015)

Jellyneo's Book of Ages
bookofages.jellyneo.net/history/


▸ When are the New Features released?
The New Features are usually updated around 3 PM to 8 PM throughout the weekdays. The update date will usually be marked as the next day.

Basics Related

▸ How many pets can I own?
You can own six (6) pets on each account (One Main + Four Sides). Premium members are allowed to have ten (10) pets on their main account. Extra Pet Slots can be purchased to add a maximum of ten (+10) pet slots per account. The theoretical max is eighty-four (84) pets.


▸ What is the best way on how to make Neopoints?
The best way to earn Neopoints is by playing the game persistently as it's going to be a long journey. You can do any or all of the following:
- Site Dailies (and Trudy)
- Playing Games
- Battledome
- Restocking (and Reselling)
- Stock Market
- Food Club

▸ Where and how do I get Paint Brushes?
Here's a quick list of where Paint Brushes can be obtained:

- Alien Aisha Vending Machine (r150 and lower rarity Paint Brushes)
- Anchor Management (Pirate Paint Brush, Pirate Petpet Paint Brush, & Maraquan Paint Brush)
- Creative Contest (Various Paint Brushes)
- The Faerie Caverns (Faerie Paint Brush)
- Fruit Machine (All Paint Brushes)
- Grave Danger (Maraquan Paint Brush + Maraquan Petpet Paint Brush, & Zombie Paint Brush)
- Lost Desert Scratchcard Kiosk (Lost Desert Paint Brush)
- Random Events (r101s from Jacko the Phantom painter + Christmas Paint Brush when visiting Terror Mountain)
- Referral Programme (Various Paint Brushes)
- RIC Redemption (Various Paint Brushes)
- Rubbish Dump (Blue Paint Brush and Silver Paint Brush)
- Test Your Strength (Halloween Paint Brush)
- Tarla's Toolbar (Speckled Paint Brush, Cloud Paint Brush, Sketch Paint Brush, and Baby Paint Brush)
- Wheel of Extravagance (All Paint Brushes)
- Wheel of Monotony (Tyrannian Paint Brush + Tyrannian Petpet Paint Brush)
- Ye Olde Fishing Vortex (All Paint Brushes)

- Discovered Treasure Chest (Pirate Paint Brush + Pirate Petpet Paint Brush)
- Legendary Chests (No-Trade) (Pirate Paint Brush)
- Trick-or-Treat Bag (Halloween Petpet Paint Brush)

- Gift Shop of 1,000 Rewards (Lost Desert Paint Brush)
- Sophie's Shack and, grudgingly, Prize Shop (Ghost Paint Brush)
- Jorax's Discount Space Prize Emporium (One-Use Robotification Zappermajig)
- The Faeries' Ruin - Prize Shop (Faerie Paint Brush)
- Mysterious Obelisk - Prize Shop (Tyrannian, Relic, and Shadow Paint Brush)
- Altador Cup Prize Shop (Themed after whoever won 1st place last year)

- The Shop Wizard (All if there are any)
- The Trading Post (All if there are any)
- The Auction House (All if there are any)
- The Hidden Tower (Baby Paint Brush, Darigan Paint Brush, Maractite Paint Brush, & Royal Paint Brush + Royal Petpet Paint Brush)


▸ Is the Lab Ray worth it?
This depends on what you want from the Lab Ray. Do you want to spend ~2m for:
- Lab Ray Only Exclusive Colors (Burlap, Ice, Mosaic, MSP, Robot, and Sponge)
- Fluctuating Battledome Stats
- The ability to change the gender of your pets on demand without additional costs
- The Lab Ray Avatar
- Random Species/Color changes

If you answered yes to most of these questions, then yes, the Lab Ray might be worth it to you!


▸ What are the risks of the Lab Ray?
As a disclaimer, do know that there are certain risks such as:
- You are not guaranteed a specific color/species zap within a short time or even a year.
- There is a chance of your pet being zapped down to Level 1 with any given zap (the odds sharply decrease around Level 25+).
- "Fluctuating Battledome Stats", means your pet's Defense and Level will be demolished, but your HP will skyrocket as that stat cannot be lowered by the Lab Ray.
- Lab Ray zaps are practically irreversible. If you happen to zap an unconverted pet (which you honestly shouldn't), then there is a chance for TNT Support to reverse it for you, but don't make it a habit.


▸ Where can I get Petpet and Regular Lab Ray Map Pieces?
You can obtain Lab Ray Map Pieces from the following:
- Buying them from other players through the Shop Wizard, Trading Post, or Auction House
- Random Events
- Tarla's Non-Toolbar Treasures
- The Wheel of Extravagance


▸ Is the Petpet Lab Ray worth it?
The Petpet Lab Ray is just an additional component to the Lab Ray Map. It's not too expensive and there's an avatar from it. There are some exclusive Petpet species and colors from the Petpet Lab Ray, but do take notice of the risks of this activity.


▸ What are the consequences and risks of Petpet Lab Ray?
This is a quick list of the consequences and risks of the Petpet Lab Ray:
- Zapped Petpets are not eligible for the Petpet Protection League award.
- Zapped Petpets cannot be painted.
- Zapped Petpet Krawks cannot be turned into Pet Krawks.
- There is a chance your Zapped Petpet (and Petpetpet) will permanently disappear.


▸ Where do I redeem the Secret Lab Maps?
You can redeem your maps over at the Neopets Treasure Hunt page.


▸ Why can't I redeem the Petpet Lab Ray Map?
You need to redeem the main Lab Map first.


▸ Can I attach a petpetpet to a zapped petpet? What happens if I zap a Petpet with a petpetpet?
Yes, you can attach a Petpetpet to a zapped Petpet although be warned if your Petpet gets a permanently disappearing zap, then the Petpetpet will also disappear with it.


▸ Does my Petpet matter if I want an exclusive Lab Ray color?
No, it does not, because the Petpet Lab Ray does not take into consideration of what species your currently Petpet is.


▸ If my petpet gets zapped into an avatar petpet, will it qualify for said avatar?
If it meets the right requirements, such as age or matching pet, then yes it will qualify for said avatar.


▸ Can I remove a zapped Petpet, but keep it's zapped form?
No, you cannot remove a zapped petpet and have it retain its zapped form. It will revert to its original colored species when removed from your pet.


▸ My pet just zapped into a Pile of Soot. Is this permanent?
No, it is not permanent and you can revert your Petpet to its original form by removing it from your Pet.


▸ Are Petpet Levels good for anything?
Petpet Levels are only really used for Petpet Battles. There's nothing else.


▸ Where can I get Transmogrification Potions?
You can obtain Transmogrification Potions from the following:
- Buying them from other players through the Shop Wizard, Trading Post, or Auction House
- Random Events
- Neocola Machine
- Battledome (Moehog, Harry the Mutant Moehog on Mighty)
- Halloween Neopian Times (Poogle)


▸ What's The Neolodge good for?
The NeoLodge is used to keep your pets at Bloated status for the duration of their stay. You will be unable to feed them for the time they are there, so no need to worry about accidentally feeding your Grarrl, Jetsam, or Skeith! The NeoLodge can also be used to reset your pet's hunger satiety back down to Bloated status if you happened to eat a bit too much over at Kelp or the Golden Dubloon.

There's no shame leaving your pets at Cockroach Towers with no Extras as there is no difference in those additional features other than a higher cost.


▸ How do I change the language of the site?
You can change the language of the site by going to the bottom of any page to Select Language and adjust your language preferences there. By changing the language of the site, you might notice some differences such as follows:
- The site being translated to the selected language.
- Being able to use/read/eat certain items you wouldn't normally be able to (only effective with various items prior 2013-2015).
- Changing the rewards of the Qasalan Expellibox.
- Access to different Language NeoBoards (Italian, Japanese, Simplified Chinese, Traditional Chinese, Dutch, and Korean NeoBoards are retired).
- NC Mall not being available (Italian, Simplified Chinese, Traditional Chinese, Japanese, or Korean).

Note: In 2008 and 2015, TNT has stopped translating all their content. A number of newer items (2015-Present) might not exist for Non-English languages and exchanging/gifting items to another player might make those items disappear. You would have to ticket in to have the items returned.


▸ How do you win at Neopets?
Quoting from Jellyneo:

Like in real life, the world of Neopets isn't linear, doesn't have a single overarching story, and hasn't got a single "ending" point that everyone is working towards. Instead, there are many different activities to try, and you're free to choose whichever you want, and as many or few as you want. (By extension, you're also free not to participate in the ones that don't interest you. Nobody is going to penalise you for having no interest in building a gallery or designing a web page.) My advice to you as a newbie is to try out as many of them as possible and see which ones suit you. Most players find a few activities that they really enjoy and focus on those things. If you manage to achieve the goals you set yourself in your favourite areas, then you can probably claim to be "winning" at Neopets, even if there's no congratulatory message and ending credits. ;)

You can strive to be the richest, create pet dreamies, collect avatars, win trophies and contests, etc. There are an abundance of activities to do on this site and picking out your goals is how you can start to aim for that sense of pride and accomplishment.


▸ What happens when my pet's mood is low/high?
It just changes the facial appearance of your pets and the occasional flavor text your pet gives off. Back then, if your pet's mood was extremely low, a certain Random Event (all color changing Random Events are now retired) would change that pet's color to Blue or Red.


▸ How do I make my pets happy / increase their mood?
You can do any (or all) of the following:
- Feed your Neopets (Happy Negg , Smiley Negg, NC Food are boosters)
- Play with Toys
- Use Grooming items
- Play with Instruments
- Ride the Roo Island Merry-Go-Round
- Visit the Tiki Tours
- See a Concert
- Play Kacheek Seek
- Play with a Chia Plushie (sharply increases happiness and rips Chia Plushie with Lupe)


▸ Why are my pets unhappy?
The cause of your pet's unhappiness could be for any of the following:
- Nothing, mood decreases overtime
- Playing with Broken Toys
- Random Events
- TDMBGPOP / Apple Bobbing
- Being Sick / Hungry / Having No HP


▸ Does Neopets do anything special for my Birthday?
On your Birthday, you will receive a special Birthday themed Site Theme for the day! TNT has said that this Site Theme will increase the frequency of Random Events.

Neopets Editorial - Issue 653 | Question 8 [link]

Hi, TNT! *waves* I'm sure this is something that you thought you were done explaining, but unfortunately quite a few users (including myself) would like some clarification with regard to getting Random Events on your birthday. I've seen some users say that it was just an old joke on your behalf, but one gets an increased amount of RE's on their birthday, yes? Please remove my UN. Thank you. :3 ~UN removed

The fact that you get an increased chance for Random Events on your birthday is completely true. :) It's even been carried over to the new system. So, enjoy your special day!


▸ How do I make NeoFriends?
Making NeoFriends is a pretty difficult task! You can go around the NeoBoards, join Guilds, and whatnot to see if there's anyone that would like to be your NeoFriend.


▸ What does this acronym/phrase mean in Neopets?
I would check out the following general guides for that:

Jellyneo's Neopian Dictionary
jellyneo.net/?go=neopian_dictionary

TDN's The Neopian Acronyms And Terms Page
thedailyneopets.com/articles/tnaatp

As these are general guides, they might not cover specific terms in relation to the topic in mind. I would either check out if there is a acronym/phrase guide for that specific topic or ask the closest related NeoBoard for that.


▸ Why did my message get blocked?
It's because your message tripped the filters so you gotta reword it (but only do so when the context is appropriate).


▸ Am I finally allowed to mention LGBTQIA+ related topics on Neopets?
As of December 18th 2020, you are allowed to discuss LGBTQIA+ related topics on Neopets.

We suggest you read the full editorial here and keep in mind the numerous caveats that this change entails:

Neopets Editorial - Issue 923 | Second Special Announcement [link]

We wanted to give you a heads up about some changes coming soon to the filters on the Neoboards. As many of you are aware, certain discussions that extend to real-life topics are not permitted on the boards, in order to ensure the safety and privacy of our users.

However, Neopets should always be a safe place to express yourself, regardless of your identity or orientation, and many of the filters we had in place in the past did not allow for that expr.ession. Above all else, it's important to us on TNT that Neopia and the Neoboards are a safe and welcoming place for everyone, including Neopians in the LGBTQIA+ community. We've realized that some of the filters or restrictions placed on the Neoboards did not always account for that, so we'll be making changes to filters surrounding LGBTQIA+ filters and topics on the Neoboards.

It's always been a priority for TNT to support our userbase in expressing themselves openly and safely, and we are excited to roll out these long overdue changes! In doing so, we'd like to be very clear about what we can and cannot allow to keep Neopia safe, supportive and inclusive for all our users. Please look over our new rules below, which will be added to the Chat Rules page as well. (cont.)


▸ Someone sent me a Foal in Box for some reason. Why is that?
It's because your NeoMail inbox is full. Foal in Box is play-on-words for "Full Inbox".


▸ Is there anything else I need to know about the basics of Neopets?
Don't be afraid to ask questions. Everybody starts somewhere and the game has a lot of content to discover. The most important thing is to have fun along the way.

Site Dailies Related

▸ What is the Anchor Management and is it worth doing this?
Anchor Management is a simple single button click daily for a free pirate-themed item per day. This daily started after the events of the Krawk Island Disappearance.

Anchor Management is 100% worth visiting daily as you have the chance to get some Morphing Potions, Dubloons, Paint Brushes, and other great rewards!


▸ What is Apple Bobbing and is it worth doing this?
Apple Bobbing is a simple single button click daily for a free apple/Haunted Woods/Neovia themed item or an unfortunate event per day. This daily started at the start of the Haunted Faire 2010 and is run by Vandebart Biggsby (or Bart)!

These are the unfortunate events that could happen from Apple Bobbing:
- You can lose Neopoints (it is also possible to have your Neopoints on hand go negative)
- You lose a random item from your inventory
- Your active Neopet's mood is lowered
- Your active Neopet gets hurt and loses health
- Your active Neopet contracts Blurred Vision
- Nothing happens

Apple Bobbing varies for some people, but we all do it at some point for the Imposter Apple Avatar. Some people quit this daily right immediately obtaining the avatar because the unlucky outcomes can be annoying, but others might continue to visit here for the free items. You decide if you're hungry for apples!


▸ I heard that Apple Bobbing can reward any item with the word "Apple" in it. Is that true?
This was true, but not anymore. In early 2018, TNT updated the Apple Bobbing prize pool and accidentally made the daily give apples that were rare item codes, r99s, and even Everlasting Apple for a short time!


▸ What is the Bank Interest?
At the National Neopian Bank, Bank interest is a daily dose of free NP with the click of a button. The more NP you have in the bank and higher Interest Rate you are, the more interest you'll get.

It is basically free Neopoints per day, so it is always beneficial to you. Some people would want to get about 15k+ in Bank Interest (Ultimate Riches! + 43,797,080 NP) to set aside for buying Stock Shares at the Neopets Stock Market.

Jellyneo's Guide + Calculator
jellyneo.net/?go=bank


▸ What is the Coltzan's Shrine and is it worth doing this?
Coltzan's Shrine is a simple single button click daily for a chance of a free desert-themed item, stat boosts, or Neopoints every 13 hours. This shrine is a tribute to King Coltzan III and started being a daily in 2001 after the events of Usurper and Search for the Crown.

You are not always guaranteed a reward, but there are no harm in visiting. Notable rewards include Dubloons, rare Battledome weapons, and more! Free healing, Neopoints, and stat boost are nice extras.


▸ What is this Sparky Random Event I got from visiting the Coltzan's Shrine?
Sparky is a tribute to a former Neopets artist's dog (named Sparky) who passed away on August 27, 2013. Their dog was the inspiration of the Spardel petpet.


▸ Is it true that you can get a million Neopoints for visiting the Coltzan's Shrine?
TNT has said this was possible in the past, but it is believed this discontinued at some point or never happened where it now lives as a Neopets meme of members staying up until Midnight NST to do Coltzan's Shrine.

Is it true that Coltzans Shrine gives out 1 million Neopoints?
Yes, there is a small chance that Coltzan will feel really generous and give out 1 million Neopoints. This is extremely rare though, so don't count on it. (The odds are approximately 6 million to 1.)


▸ What is Council Chamber and is it worth doing this?
The Council Chamber is a simple two-button click daily for a free Altador themed item or Neopoints. This Daily can be accessed after completing the Altador Mini-Plot.

The Council Chamber does not have any spectacular rewards, but you are always guaranteed a cheap item reward or 200-1,000 Neopoints.


▸ What is the Daily Puzzle and is it worth doing this?
Located under the Community Hub, The Daily Puzzle is once per day trivia game of Neopian subjects that rewards Neopoints and even items sometimes.

The game rewards about 200-400 (average around 300) Neopoints upon answering correctly. Items are usually rewarded on Neopian holidays such as pet days. If you are unable to find or just want to find the answer quickly, you can find the answer at the Games NeoBoards Chat, Help NeoBoards Chat, or fansites such as Jellyneo, The Daily Neopets, and Sunnyneo.


▸ Why am I getting the same Daily Puzzle?
Sometimes TNT will forget to update the Daily Puzzle. Same question, same answer, and same rewards. No harm.


▸ What is Deadly Dice and is it worth doing this?
The Deadly Dice is a game where you can gamble your active pet's Level against Count Von Roo. You can only challenge with him once per day and at anywhere 12:00am to 1:00am NST (except on Halloween when he is awake to play all day that day).

Most people quit after getting the Count von Roo's Deadly Dice Avatar. Some people might only do it when they want to decrease their pet's Level for training. In reality, this game is not recommended for training Levels.


▸ Why didn't I get more Levels from this massive tie streak win I just got from the Deadly Dice?
To quote Jellyneo, "You can never wager an amount of levels that would put you in the negatives if you lost.

This is to say if your active pet is currently Level 3 and after two ties, you cannot wager to get +4 Levels as losing would drop you down to Level -1. You would get +3 Levels instead.


▸ Is there a way how to guarantee a win from the Deadly Dice?
There is no guaranteed win method from the Deadly Dice.


▸ What is the Deserted Tomb and is it worth doing this?
The Deserted Tomb of Geraptiku is a simple two-button click daily for a free Geraptiku/Mystery Island themed item, codestones, fading faeries, and/or Neopoints. There is the possibility of getting hurt or getting nothing at all though.

The Deserted Tomb varies for some people, but we all do it at some point for the Geraptiku - Deserted Tomb Avatar. Some people quit this daily right immediately obtaining the avatar because the unlucky outcomes can be annoying, but others might continue to visit here for the free items.


▸ What is the Faerie Crossword and is it worth doing this?
The Faerie Crossword is a simple Neopian themed word puzzle game that can be played once a day. You can earn 200-600 Neopoints (depending on how fast you complete it) and your active Neopet might receive +1-3 Intelligence.

Most people just do this for the avatar and then forget it exists. There is no harm whatsoever in the Faerie Crossword. If you are unable to find or just want to find the answers quickly, you can find the answers at the Games NeoBoards Chat or fansites such as Jellyneo, The Daily Neopets, and Sunnyneo.


▸ The Faerie Crossword is under maintenance. When is it coming back?
The Faerie Crossword is known to go under maintenance and it's all random on when it'll come back. It can be a few days or weeks. TNT usually don't give out an ETA on its fixes.


▸ What is the Forgotten Shore and is it worth doing this?
Quite similar to Anchor Management, The Forgotten Shore is a simple single button click daily for the chance of a free pirate-themed item, Neopoints, or a Treasure Chest containing other goodies. You can only access this daily once you have completed the Forgotten Shore Map (which is pretty cheap under 200 NP).

There are days where you will receive nothing from this daily, but there is no harm in checking in each day. The price of the map is worth the unlimited access to the daily. You can also obtain the Forgotten Shore avatar which is randomly awarded.


▸ What is the Fruit Machine and is it worth doing this?
The Fruit Machine is a simple click daily for the chance of a Desert Fruit, Neopoints, and if you're lucky, Paint Brushes! You can also win a random Neopian Petpet (≤ r70), Fading Bottled Faeries, random Battle Muffins, and Strength/Level stat boosts to your active pet.

You are not always guaranteed a reward, but there are no harm in visiting. The rewards are nice to try each day.


▸ I got two matches in the Fruit Machine, why didn't I win anything?
You are only given the two-match rewards if they the same fruit from the left side and center.


▸ Didn't there used to be a trophy with the Fruit Machine?
Indeed, there used to be a trophy for the Fruit Machine that was based on the amount of Neopoints won. It is believed that the High Score Table stopped updating during the daily's makeover in 2012.


▸ What is the Giant Jelly / Giant Omelette and is it worth doing this?
The Giant Jelly and Giant Omelette are single click dailies for free food being Jelly or an Omelette. Both can be visited once per day and share quite the same similarities with no harm for visiting either.

The Giant Jelly (if such a thing existed) does not have any major rewards. Poisonous Jelly and Glowing Jelly (with a very small chance of coloring your pet Glowing) can disease your pets.

The Giant Omelette does have r101+ which are worthwhile to hoard (or sell) towards Charity Corner. There is also Honey Blossom Omelette which is really just a rare item at a high price. Rotten Omelette can disease your pets.


▸ The Giant Jelly / Giant Omelette has been eaten! When will another appear? MY PETS ARE DYING
Randomly throughout the day, both places will run out of food and will be replenished later. The time of the replacement for both are unkown to this day.


▸ What is Grave Danger and is it worth doing this?
Grave Danger is a 3-10 hour daily that can reward a miscellaneous vartiety of items with highlights being Morphing Potions, Paint Brushes, Petpetpets, and the elusive Grave Danger Stamp. You must have a petpet attached to one of your pets and they will be temporarily absent from your pet upon entering.

You are always guaranteed a reward (albeit it might not be a spectacular one) and there is no harm in participating in this daily despite the "chance of being cursed" description.

Neopets Editorial - Issue 620 | Question 2 [link]

So, we have a new daily and it's one aimed at Petpets! That's totally awesome, but I have a question. The news for it seemed to imply that Petpets might not come back, which we've seen before (like the Petpet Lab Ray and Turmy). This is obviously a bit of a concern for Neopians who either have expensive Petpets or, like me, super old ones with no intention of ever detaching them. Is that really the case? Can you lose your Petpet going in the catacombs? Thanks for answering. ~kristykimmy

You can rest assured that your Petpets will eventually wander back, once they've danced with Ghost Meepits, chewed on cultists' robes, or any other crazy adventure they experienced down there. :)


▸ What kinds of things happen when my petpet is at Grave Danger?
When your petpet is adventuring in Grave Danger, the following events will be in effect:

- The petpet will temporarily poof in a cloud of smoke in its owner's userlookup.
- You will be unable to remove the petpet.
- You will be unable to zap the petpet.
- You will be unable to transfer or abandon the petpet's owner.


▸ What is Grumpy Old King / Wise Old King and is it worth doing this?
The Grumpy Old King / Wise Old King are both dropdown submission-based dailies of telling wisdom or a making a good joke to impress the directed king. If you are able to impress the kings, they will reward items related to their kingdom, Neopoints (with a possible x10 multiplier), and possibly an avatar.

The Grumpy Old King, King Skarl, can reward Meridellian foods, Neopoints, and most notably his collection of King Skarl related paraphernalia that's worth hundreds to millions of NP (although most people believe those rewards are not obtainable anymore nowadays or were actually released properly at all). You can try twice per day.

The Wise Old King, King Hagan, can reward Brightvale Books and Scrolls with the addition of Neopoints. None of the rewards exceed over the 25k, but most of them are in the r90+ for Charity Corner. You can try once per day.

Most people just visit each king for their avatars and then quit immediately, because of its long and monotonous effort of going through all the dropdown options just to get a cheap item and/or few NP at most times. There is a trophy for this daily to mention that is based off your given score from the kings.


▸ Did TNT ever release Skarl Collectable Charm?
Apparently TNT released it four times, but we have never seen this item outside aside from a Staff Member's Stamp Album. It is believed sometime before July 2019 that TNT took out most of the new King Skarl prizes.

- Neopets Editorial - Issue 867 | Question 3 [link] (May 31st, 2019)
- Neopets Editorial - Issue 856 | Question 3 [link] (February 15th, 2019)
- New Features (January 24th, 2019)
- Neopets Editorial - Issue 632 | Question 5 [link] (February 14th, 2014)


▸ Does my response to the Grumpy Old King / Wise Old King matter?
No, but nothing happens when you leave the whole response blank. There is a random avatar when using a specific response to King Skarl.


▸ What do you do if fierce Peophins has eaten too much tin of olives?
This line actually came from the description of Blumaroo Court Jester (TCG).


▸ What is the Healing Springs and is it worth doing this?
The Healing Springs is a place where you can get your pets healed, fed, or be given some goodies for free. You can also purchase those goodies from her shop. Both healing and shop purchases are limited once every 30 minutes.

There is no harm, only heal. Well, your pets are either going to be healed, fed to Bloated status, or be given a free item. Either outcome is cool and it beats purchasing for a cure. Some people really just visit to purchase a Sticky Snowball (r100) or Icy Snowball (r95) for their high rarity in preparations for Charity Corner.

In 2020's Charity Corner, TNT purposely reduced the point value of Sticky Snowball to 1 CC Point.


▸ What is Kiko Pop and is it worth doing this?
Kiko Pop is a carnival game of throwing a dart at a spinning board with balloons. It has three difficulties and the harder the difficulty the rarer the prize, but the harder chance to get a prize. You can only play once per day.

You are not always guaranteed a reward, but there is no harm in doing this daily (don't forget to lower/mute your volume upon entering). There is also an avatar that can be randomly won from the Standard and Hard difficulty only.


▸ What is Lunar Temple and is it worth doing this?
The Shenkuu Lunar Temple is a once per day daily where you are examining the position of Kreludor and Neopia on an astrological map to guess the phase of the Kreludor. This daily rewards a variety of Shenkuu-related rewards and high valued goodies being the Lunar Cape and Pygui if the correct phase is chosen. If you did not choose the correct phase, then you will be rewarded a consolation prize which is mostly, if not all, junk.

You are always guaranteed a reward (albeit it might not be a spectacular one) and there is no harm in participating. Some people don't bother to find the correct phase now and then due to its tedious process but the free junk item is appreciated. Most of the correct item rewards are in the r90s range in case you want to stockpile for Charity Corner.


▸ Okay so for Lunar Temple, how do I find the correct moon phase?
The correct moon phase is based on a specific number that can be found when you left click and select View Page Source. You then use CTRL + F or CMD + F the text "&angleKreludor" and compare to the following chart:

▸ What is Meteor and is it worth doing this?
Meteor Crash Site 725-XZ is a daily where you poke a giant meteor with a stick in hopes that it might drop a kreludan-themed reward. You can try once per hour just until you get a reward.

The Meteor does not have any spectacular (nor worthwhile) rewards and you are not always guaranteed a reward. There is no harm in doing this daily, but do remember to select the correct dropdown option to prevent the Meteor from poofing out of existence for that hour.


▸ What is the Money Tree / Second-Hand Shoppe and is it worth doing this?
The Money Tree / Second-Hand Shoppe are donation outlets from both Neopets players and famous Neopian characters. You are only allowed to pick up 10 total items per day from these outlets and the Rubbish Dump (example: picking up 4 items from the Money Tree, 4 items from the Second-Hand Shoppe, and 2 from the Rubbish Dump will count as 10 total).

You'll mostly find daily junk in both outlets (from both Neopets players and famous Neopian characters), but there is no harm in picking up the junk. You might possibly find some cool items from generous Neopians.


▸ What kind of goodies are donated by famous Neopian characters?
In the Money Tree, there are many different famous Neopian donors that donate a variety of items, Neopoints, or Neocash items. Wishing Well donations are directly from the Wishing Well and donations from Ghost are from that NP stealing Random Event.

In the Second-Hand Shoppe, you'll find them donate r40-r70 wearables. Those famous donors being:
- Hubrid
- Jerdana
- Koya
- Lucie
- Lucy
- Prince Jazan
- Princess Amira
- Vanity


▸ Are the Money Tree events from the World Events still happening?
It is believed that they still are, but the timing might have been delayed. Generous NC Mall Shopper (NC Upcycle Fortune Cookie donations) and The Scamander-in-Chief event were confirmed to still be active.

▸ Why can't I collect any Neopoints from the Money Tree?
You are only allowed to collect Neopoints from the Money Tree if you have less than 20,000 NP.


▸ Is there some sort of indicator that I collected the max amount of donations from the Money Tree / Second-Hand Shoppe?
If the text description of the donation being taken is centered then that's your indicator that you have reached your max for the day.


▸ Is there a limit on how many items/NP I can donate to the Money Tree / Second-Hand Shoppe? Can I donate anything?
In terms of items, there is no limit and you're allowed to donate anything (some items such as Hidden Tower items and Pile of Dung, you'll need to donate through its item page directly) that isn't No-Trade! For Neopoints, you are only allowed to donate 6 NP to 5,000 NP per donation with the total amount of 50,000 NP per day.

There are no perks to donating aside from having your UN appear in the Money Tree with your donation.


▸ What are Monthly Freebies and is it worth doing this?
Monthly Freebies is a daily where you can receive 2,000 NP and a free food item for each pet you own. The food items are low rarity and you can only visit this daily once per month.

Monthly Freebies does not have any spectacular rewards, but there is no harm in doing this once per month daily.


▸ What is the Mysterious Negg Cave and is it worth doing this?
The Mysterious Negg Cave is a grid-based puzzle game where you can win Shenkuu and Negg-related rewards from solving its mystery. You can only solve the puzzle once per day and you are give a different puzzle each day.

There is no harm in doing this daily and there are a few decent, although not extraordinary, goodies such as Ultimate Icy Negg and Red Poogle Morphing Potion. There is also an avatar that can be randomly won and also an assortment of r90 items if you are hoarding for Charity Corner to mention. If you get stuck on puzzle, I'd check out TDN's guide:

TDN's Mysterious Negg Daily Guide
thedailyneopets.com/articles/mysterious-negg/


▸ What is the Qasalan Expellibox and is it worth doing this?
The Qasalan Expellibox is a Plinko-styled daily that is most notable for its possibility of rewarding free Neocash! There is also the chance of receiving some junky NP item reward, Neopoints, a disease to your active pet, or nothing at all. You can try every once every 7 hours and 7 minutes.

Despite the risk of disease, most players would still continue to visit this daily for the chance of free Neocash.


▸ If I land on the Neocash slot in Qasalan Expellibox, am I guaranteed the 150 NC?
If your language is set to English, Dutch, Portuguese, German, French, or Spanish: You will be given 150 NC for landing on the Neocash slot.

If your language is set to Italian, Simplified Chinese, Traditional Chinese, Japanese, or Korean: You will be given 5,000 NP for landing on the Neocash slot.

Non-Flash Qasalan Expellibox Link
One-Click


▸ What is the Rubbish Dump and is it worth doing this?
The Meridell Rubbish Dump is a donation outlet similar to the Money Tree / Second-Hand Shoppe although it works a bit differently. You are still tied to the 10 total item limit with the Money Tree and Second-Hand Shoppe although the items are generated from the Rubbish Dump itself. Members can refresh at the Rubbish Dump to make items appear there with their name attached that will indicate they have visited/refreshed there. For notable items that can appear, rare r101 exclusive items such as Apple Core and Old Paper, and also r99 Medieval Petpets being Mortog and Turmac that can be found here.

There is no harm in doing obtaining items from the Rubbish Dump although it is very, very unlikely you will ever see an item that is worthwhile. There is an avatar that can be obtained from the Rubbish Dump although it is very, very rare to get.


▸ Is the That's Not Rubbish avatar active?
The avatar is active, but the refreshing requirements and absurd rarity of an avatar rewarding item makes it extremely difficult to obtain.


▸ What is the Symol Hole and is it worth doing this?
The Mysterious Symol Hole is an activity where players can get their active pet's petpets to go jump a Symol Hole in hopes of goodies. You can visit the Symol Hole repeatedly (not refreshing) until you are rewarded a prize (one prize per day).

Most people stop visiting this activity once they get the Symol avatar. In general, it is very, very tedious to get a reward from it. There are a few items that are worth hundreds to millions of Neopoints to mention if you do wish to do this monotonous daily.


▸ I thought the Symol Hole was once per hour?
It was assumed to be once per hour back then, but there's no actual time limit to try for a reward.


▸ Why wouldn't refreshing the Symol Hole work for a reward?
You'll need to create a new URL string with each page entry. So, I'd go back to the previous page and submit any action again.


▸ Does my action matter in the Symol Hole?
No, you can visit the Symol hole with any action.


▸ What is Tarla's Non-Toolbar Treasures?
Tarla's Non-Toolbar Treasures is a bit an old freebie link where on certain days and certain times, Tarla will appear in that link to give a way a free item. If it a Tarla day, there will be four different opportunities with each in different time intervals. You can only claim one prize per day. There are two different types of rewards she can give where we call them the Main and the Not-Main where sometimes the Main rewards can be Paint Brushes, Neggs, Map Pieces, and other fun goodies! The Not-Main is a random prize from a specified pool with a variety of goodies that are in the r80s, r90s, and r180s.

You are always guaranteed a reward (albeit it might not be a spectacular one) if you happen to catch her.


▸ How do I catch and/or track Tarla's Non-Toolbar Treasures?
/~Greegs has a detailed explanation on how to track down Tarla's Non-Toolbar Treasures.

Also, usually there are a couple people that track her in Site Events Chat, Games Chat, Newbies Chat, and Charter Chat (Premium Only).


▸ How would I know if it's not going to be a Tarla Day?
She will not be available for the day if you get the description: "Tarla is busy with her other chores today. Check back tomorrow to see if she's back.

She will be available for the day if you get the description: "Tarla is at the prize warehouse right now. Check back later to see if she's here!


▸ Can I still download the Neopets Toolbar? Is it still updated?
No and also no.


▸ What is The Discarded Magical Blue Grundo Plushie of Prosperity and is it worth doing this?
The Discarded Magical Blue Grundo Plushie of Prosperity (or TDMBGPOP) is a simple single button click daily for a various events. You can visit once per day.

The following outcomes are:
- Nothing happens.
- Your active pet's hunger decreases by one stage.
- Your active pet's hunger increases by one stage.
- Your active pet is fully healed.
- Your active pet's mood decreases by one stage.
- Your active pet gains intelligence.
- You are given 50 to 5,000 NP.
- You are given a random toy, rarity 89 and below.
- You are given an exclusive plushie.

You are not always guaranteed a reward and the daily might negatively affect your pet (albeit the effects are easily recoverable if it happened). Aside from the randomly awarded Grundo - Discarded Plushie avatar, Most people would still continue to visit TDMBGPOP for its possible rewards of Trick-or-Treat Bags, Birthday Bags, Usukicon Bags, and, indirectly, other Toys that might be requested by Dark Faerie Quests.


▸ What is Tombola and is it worth doing this?
Tiki Tack Tombola is a simple single button click daily for the possibility of free Codestones, Gross Food, and Mystery Island-themed prizes. How the game works is that you pull a ticket ending with a 0, 2, or 5 then you win 1-2 items with some Neopoints! There are 21 different cards and you have about a 20% chance to win! Occasionally if you get a losing ticket, the Tiki Tack Man will give out a consolation prize and sometimes Neopoints along with or without that prize.

You are not always guaranteed a reward, but there are no harm in visiting. The most notable prizes are the Codestones, items commonly requested for Aboard The Coincidence, and the few consolation rewards are worth quite a bit.


▸ Um, Tiki Tack Tombola is asking me for donations to reopen... Do I get anything for donating?
Occasionally, the Tiki Tack Man will run out of funds and will need donations to bring the daily back up. The daily will be back up once the funds have been raised. Other than that, there are no personal perks to donating so you can check back later once other players have donated their NP.


▸ What is Tombola's hours of operation?

TOMBOLA IS ALWAYS CLOSED DURING
3 AM - 4 AM NST
1 PM - 2 PM NST
9 PM - 12 AM (Midnight) NST

▸ What are Tombola Coins for? How do I get them?
A long time ago, Tombola Coins were used to play Tiki Tack Tombola but with the game being free, they are really just collector's items nowadays. They are retired and only obtainable by purchasing from other players.


▸ What is Trudy's Surprise and is it worth doing this?
Trudy's Surprise Slot Machine (or just Trudy) is a simple single button click daily for free Neopoints, exclusive items, and sometimes Basic Gift Boxes just for coming to Neopets. The amount of Neopoints rewarded increases with every consecutive visit and on your 25th consecutive visit, you will get 100,000 NP and reset back as if it was your first day of spinning. Exclusive items are rewarded every 7th consecutive visit. The Basic Gift Boxes are randomly rewarded.

There is no harm in doing this daily and it is really considered one of the best dailies on the site in terms of making Neopoints and getting Basic Gift Boxes for free. Basic Gift Boxes are used for gifting and trading Neocash items (the basic gift boxes themselves cannot be sent away). There is also an avatar that can be rewarded when you have redeemed your 25th consecutive spin.


▸ I just got another notification to spin Trudy's Surprise when I already did, why is that?
Sometimes when Neopets lags a whole bunch, it'll send out multiple notifications again. Nothing bad is going on and you can just simply delete the notification.


▸ Is there a certain time frame where Trudy's Surprise's weekly rewards changes prize pools? Will we ever see old prize pools return?
There is no set time when Trudy's Surprise's weekly rewards update. TNT has never rereleased any of the older prize pool items, although there is a possibility for their return.

Neopets Editorial - Issue 841 | Question 4 [link]

Are the new Trudy's Surprise weekly prizes retired now? They seem to have been replaced with Terror Mountain and Snowman-themed items. If so, can we expect more new prizes to be added in the future?~~ummagine3284

You can expect the Trudy's Surprise prize pool to be updated on a regular basis. Whether you will ever see the first set of prizes again is something we can't say for sure yet - perhaps if they become rare and valuable at some point, the slot machine may begin awarding them once more.


▸ The notification of Trudy's Surprise is annoying. Is there a way I can disable it?
You can go to Site Preferences and disable/reactivate the notification there. At this moment, we are unsure if this will still allow you to spin or reset your spin streak.


▸ What is the Turmaculus and is it worth doing this?
The Turmaculus is a daily where your active pet's petpet can try to wake up this LORGE Turmac. He is only awake for one hour per day and you can only try once per day. If you succeed in waking up the Turmaculus, you can be rewarded with Meridellian and Turmaculus themed rewards, Neopoints, +1 STR boost to your active Neopet, full heals your active Neopets, or raises your active pet's petpet's Level by 1. Although, do know there is a risk of having your active's petpet eaten when visiting him in his waking hour.

Visiting the Turmaculus varies for some people and always guaranteed a reward. Most of us would visit the daily for the Turmaculus Avatar. Some people quit this daily right immediately obtaining the avatar because of the chance of the Turmaculus eating your petpet while some people still visit for the item rewards and stat boost to your pet.


▸ How will we know when the Turmaculus can be awoken?
/~Brownhownd tracks down the times the Turmaculus can be awoken. NeoBoard threads in Site Events Chat, Avatar Chat, Games Chat, Newbies Chat, and Charter Chat (Premium Only) will also have PSA threads. Fansites such as JN and TDN will also give out reminders on their perspective pages.


▸ Once a petpet is eaten by the Turmaculus, is it permanently gone?
Yup, so choose your petpet wisely upon waking him up.


▸ Does my action matter with the Turmaculus?
No, you can try waking him up with any action.


▸ What is the Ye Olde Fishing Vortex and is it worth doing this?
The Ye Olde Fishing Vortex is a daily where you can go fishing with your pets. Each one of your pets can go fishing every 12 hours and build up their Fishing Level. Your pet's Fishing Level will determine which items your pet can get. There are a variety of exclusive goodies such as Food, Toys, Books, Stat Increasers, Potions that can fiddle with your pet's species/color, and more! There are also non-exclusive rewards such as Transmogrification Potions and Paint Brushes.

Most of the time you'll receive junk, but there is no harm in participating in this daily. Most players don't really bother switching between pets to go fishing, but that's really a personal preference. There is also an avatar when your pet catches a Titanic Giant Squid (Fishing Level 80).


▸ Can I lend/trade a pet with a high Fishing Level?
You can, but Fishing Level is tied to your account and will drop down to Level 0 when abandoned/transferred. It will reinstated back to its original Fishing Level when it is returned to the prior account it leveled up on.


▸ Aside from regularly fishing, is there a way I can raise my Fishing Level? What is the highest Fishing Level?
You can read the book, Fishing Made Easy, to raise your pet's Fishing Level. The highest Fishing Level is 500.

Side Accounts Related

▸ How many accounts can I have in total?
Five (5) in total. You are allowed one (1) main account and four (4) side accounts.

- Neopets Editorial - Issue 700 | Question 6 [link]


▸ What's the difference between a main account and a side account?
A main account is where you do all your main account business per se:
- Earn Neopoints/Neopoint Items through Games, Restocking/Selling, Dailies, Battledome, etc.
- Participate in Events and most Contests/Spotlights
- Obtain all the avatars
- Purchase Premium

A side account is where you can hold more pets, make more galleries/Neohomes, casually chat on the NeoBoards with, and tons of other fun things to do. There are quite a ton of limitations to what you can do on your side account, but it's an optional decision if you feel like you want to have one or not.


▸ Why should I create a side account and what can I do on side accounts?
The main reason why people create side accounts is to store and have more pets, but here's a quick list:
- More pets and petpages
- More Galleries/Neohomes
- Purchase Neocash and participate in most NC events (and collecting NC Mall Freebies)
- Join a Guild or make a Guild Account
- Use as a main when your actual main account is silenced/frozen (this does NOT mean that you can use your side to continue to discuss what got your main account the silence or suspension in the first place)

It is completely optional to have a side account, but do keep in mind of the rules if you plan on making one.


▸ Am I allowed to make sales off my side accounts?
You are NOT allowed to bid on auctions or trades on your side account for any purpose if those auctions or trades are not your own. That includes creating sales transactions through the trading post, auctions, and official (and user) shops. Also, do make sure to take out all the items from the side's shop if you're moving accounts.

Guild Account Shops are OK as long as the shop is owned bt the Guild Leader (no account sharing), properly labeled as a Guild Account, and all funds go to Guild purposes.

- Neopets Editorial - Issue 844 | Question 4 [link] (Guild Shops Are OK with more clarification)
- Neopets Editorial - Issue 828 | Question 4 [link] (General Everything Most Recent)
- Neopets Editorial - Issue 338 | Question 9 [link] (Using Auctions to puposely bump prices of items is NOT allowed)
- Neopets Editorial - Issue 282 | Question 2 [link] (Using Auctions to puposely bump prices of items is NOT allowed)
- Neopets Editorial - Issue 229 | Question 11 [link] (General Basics Covered + Guild Shops Are OK)


▸ Am I allowed to collect avatars on my side accounts?
You are allowed to collect avatars on side accounts as long as you do NOT gain Neopoints or items for doing so. From a specific inquiry, you are allowed to get the Lever of Doom avatar on your side accounts as well.

A visual listing of avatars that are allowed on side accounts can be found here:
/~Mustala

- Neopets Editorial - Issue 310 | Question 1 [link] (General Info)
- Neopets Editorial - Issue 444 | Question 12 [link] (Lever of Doom Is OK)


▸ Am I allowed to create a Bank Account on my side accounts?
You are allowed to create a Bank Account on your side account, but you are NOT allowed to collect interest.

- Neopets Editorial - Issue 389 | Question 2 [link] (Reconfirmation That Having A Bank Account On Side Is OK)
- Neopets Editorial - Issue 313 | Question 9 [link] (General Info + Collecting Interest NOT allowed)


▸ Am I allowed to use the Battledome on my side accounts?
You are NOT allowed to use the Battledome on your side accounts for the rewards. You are however allowed to use the Battledome on your side accounts for 2-Player fights because you do not gain any rewards for doing so.

- Neopets Editorial - Issue 888 | Question 2 [link] (2P battling is OK)
- Neopets Editorial - Issue 570 | Question 8 [link] (General Info That 1P NOT allowed)


▸ Am I allowed to Train my pets on my side accounts?
You are allowed to train your pets on your side accounts (Swashbuckling, Mystery Island, and Secret Ninja). You are also allowed to use the free Swashbuckling Academy training from pet days and Neopets's Anniversary (Nov 15th).

Methods of training that could give your Neopoints/Neopoint items are NOT allowed (Kitchen Quests, Scratchcards, etc.). Training and Faerie Quest Fortune Cookies are NOT allowed as well.

- Neopets Editorial - Issue 254 | Question 7 [link] (General Info and special day training is OK)
- Neopets Editorial - Issue 783 | Question 2 [link] (Kitchen Quest is NOT allowed)
- Neopets Editorial - Issue 716 | Question 6 [link] (Faerie Quest Cookies are NOT allowed to be used)


▸ Am I allowed to read Books to my pets on my side accounts?
You are allowed to read books (and obtain the Neopian and Booktastic Book Award) to your pets on your side accounts as they do not reward any Neopoints or Neopoint items.

You are also allowed to purchase the Hidden Tower books, Grimoire of the First Order, Grimoire of Prosperity, and Grimoire of Affluence on your side accounts as long as you abide by the one Hidden Tower purchase rule (aka not buying multiple Hidden Tower items on your main and sides on the same day).

- Neopets Editorial - Issue 494 | Question 10 [link] (Hidden Tower Books are OK)


▸ Am I allowed to participate in Creative Contests on my side accounts?
You are NOT to participate in most Creative Contests on your side accounts. You are allowed to participate in Creative Contests that do not award Neopoints nor Neopoint Items.

ALLOWED

You were allowed to enter in the Neohome Spotlight, Pet & Petpet Spotlight, Site Spotlight, Faerie Caves II Spotlight, Hannah and the Pirate Caves/Kreludor Spotlight, and Tyrannian Mini Golf Spotlight on your side accounts, but these have been discontinued.

You were NOT allowed to enter in the Adventure Generator Spotlight, Lenny Conundrum, and Random Contest (very rarely pops up again) on your side accounts prior to their retirement.

- Neopets Editorial - Issue 554 | Question 5 [link] (Site Spotlight is OK)


▸ Am I allowed to do Dailies on my side accounts?
You are NOT allowed to do Dailies on your side account. Visiting the Healing Springs is allowed though.

- Neopets Editorial - Issue 223 | Question 9 [link] (General Information and Healing Springs is OK)

Just think of it this way: before you do anything in your alternate accounts, just ask yourself, "Will I receive any Neopoints/items from this activity?" If the answer is yes, then don't play. Activities such as the Soup Kitchen, and the Roo Island Merry Go Round are fine to play in alts, because no matter what, you will not receive anything from it (except maybe happier Neopets). The ONLY exception to this is the Healing Springs. We wouldn't want your pets to suffer if you couldn't afford their medication.


▸ Am I allowed to purchase items from the Almost Abandoned Attic/Hidden Tower on my side accounts?
In most cases, you are NOT allowed to purchase items from the Almost Abandoned Attic/Hidden Tower on your side accounts. The exception is when your side account is older than your main account and that the funds come from your main account. For the Hidden Tower, you must abide by the one item purchase rule (aka not buying multiple Hidden Tower items on your main and sides on the same day). You are only allowed to restock from the Almost Abandoned Attic on one account.

- Neopets Editorial - Issue 494 | Question 2 [link] (General Information)


▸ Am I allowed to complete Faerie Quests on my side accounts?
You are allowed to complete random Faerie Quests (not Faerie Quest Fortune Cookies/Illusen/Jhudora/Snow) on your side accounts. You can use the Shop Wizard to purchase the requested item from user shops (not offical shops).

- Neopets Editorial - Issue 891 | Question 1 [link] (Random Faerie Quests are OK, but FQCs are NOT allowed)
- Neopets Editorial - Issue 268 | Question 5 [link] (Controlled Faerie Quests are NOT allowed)
- Neopets Editorial - Issue 285 | Question 7 [link] (Using and buying Shop Wizard is OK, but buying from official Neopian Shops is NOT allowed)


▸ Am I allowed to redeem the Freebies perks on my side accounts?
You are allowed to redeem the Freebies Pack and the free 150 NC, but you are NOT allowed to redeem your Monthly Freebies on your side accounts.

- Neopets Editorial - Issue 891 | Question 1 [link] (Obtaining the Newbie Pack and free 150 NC are OK)
- Neopets Editorial - Issue 319 | Question 2 [link] (Newbie Pack is OK, but Monthly Freebies is NOT allowed)
- Neopets Editorial - Issue 796 | Question 2 [link] (Creating multiple accounts for the free 150 NC is NOT allowed)

▸ Am I allowed to create/join Guilds on my side accounts?
You are allowed to create/join Guilds on your side accounts. You are NOT allowed to join guild contests that have prizes (UNLESS they are non-tangible prizes like graphics). If you are the leader of that Guild, you are allowed to have a Guild Account (does not count as one of your total accounts unless you want it to be your main account, and also, this account cannot be shared with others).

▸ Am I allowed to use the Lab Ray on my side accounts?
You are allowed to use the Secret Laboratory Map (and Petpet Laboratory Map) on your side accounts. You are also allowed to keep the 10k from redeeming those Maps.

You are NOT allowed to use Lab Ray Fortune Cookies on your side accounts UNLESS that one side account is your only Lab Ray account (even if you have access to the Lab Ray on your main and/or other accounts, you would only be allowed to use the Lab Ray Fortune Cookies on your main account if that was the case).

Similarly, for battling the Lab Ray Scientist to change a pet's Gender, you are NOT allowed to fight him on your side accounts UNLESS that one side account is your only Lab Ray account (same rules as above). Also, you are NOT allowed to win the fight either as you can earn Neopoints and Neopoint items from winning.

▸ So, I got my account got Frozen. Am I allowed to make my side account a temporary main account?
You are allowed to use your side (or a new) account as a temporary main account if you are in the process of recovering your main account. You are NOT allowed to use your side (or new) account to evade a suspension/freeze or continue an offense you committed on your main.

- Neopets Editorial - Issue 906 | Question 2 [link] (Temp Mains are OK)
- Neopets Editorial - Issue 320 | Question 6 [link] (General Info)


▸ I want to make my side account be my new main account. What would I have to do?
There isn't any set procedure on switching accounts, but it's a bit of serious decision. Few questions to ask yourself:
- Do you like the name of the account?
- Do you care about the account age perks (Pet Transfers, Food Club, etc.)?
- Is it worth the time switching over (Neofriends, NC/NP Items, etc.)?

If you do plan to make the switch, here are a couple of things you'd want to do:
- Empty your Usershop (and Shop Till), Trading Post, Auctions, Stocks, and Gallery if they indicate sales
- Avoid doing dailies and anything that could earn you items/NP for like 24 hours
- Cancel Premium if you have it on your old main/now side account
- Add a label to your accounts indicating that this was an old main/now side account of X account (not guaranteed)
- Change the Site Theme of your sides as a safety measurement to know which account you're on

- Neopets Editorial - Issue 270 | Question 14 [link] (General Info that it is OK, but like as one or two time thing)
- Neopets Editorial - Issue 873 | Question 6 [link] (Tips For Swiching Accounts)
- Neopets Editorial - Issue 905 | Question 1 [link] (Using the Trading Post to transfer items is OK, Usershop is NOT)
- Neopets Editorial - Issue 278 | Question 13 [link] (Premium and Premium paraphernalia are NOT transferable)
- Neopets Editorial - Issue 222 | Question 14 [link] (Lookup Labeling)

- Neopets Editorial - Issue 223 | Question 6 [link] (Accidents can happen, don't turn it into a habit)

If you didn't find the answer here about side accounts, then you can always ask the Help Chat or look through the Editorial. The biggest rule on side accounts is that you are NOT earn Neopoints or items, so if the activity awards any of that, don't do that (unless stated allowed so).

Site Events FAQs
