Reoccurring Events Related


▸ What is the Advent Calendar?
It's a month-long Neopets tradition of giving Neopians some prizes along with short themed animations daily. For each day of the Month of Celebration, animations contain characters and events from last year or new, random animations, along with Neopoints and prizes related to the animations. It has been going on since 2000.


▸ Why won't the Advent Calendar load?
If you're trying to watch old animations, all of them from 2000 to 2016 were Flash based, so you might need to use a browser that enables Flash. As for the current animations, you might have already seen today's one, or maybe it's just broken for everybody. If you are unable to access the main Advent Calendar page, you can visit the process page to obtain the prizes for the day.

Jellyneo's Advent Calendar Articles
jellyneo.net/?go=advent
bookofages.jellyneo.net/history/advent-calendar-animations/

TDN's Latest Advent Calendar Article
thedailyneopets.com/articles/advent-calendar-2020

SunnyNeo's Advent Calendar Articles
sunnyneo.com/adventcalendar.php


▸ How do I get the Advent Calendar Site Theme and Avatar?
The Plastic Fir avatar is rewarded to players every 1st day of Celebration when visiting the Advent Calendar for the first time. The Seasonal Attack Pea avatar is rewarded to players on a random day when visiting the Advent Calendar. The date of Seasonal Attack Pea avatar is the same for everyone, but is different each year. Now, the Winter Holiday theme is awarded to those who collect every single daily prize, and will be awarded at the 31st.


▸ Am I allowed to participate in the Advent Calendar on my side accounts?
No, you are not. You're also not allowed to get the avatar or the Winter Holiday theme on your side.


▸ What is with Pant Devil always stealing a Rod of Supernova in the Advent Calendar?
It's one of the running gags in the Advent Calendar. Every year, you will get a Rod of Supernova, but the Pant Devil will swoop in and immediately steal it from you. The Unfortunate Holiday Ogrin is another Advent Calender running gag where on every December 28th (Ogrin Day), this Ogrin undergoes a series of unfortunate events.


▸ Are there any cool things around December?
Every December, the Winter Starlight Celebration begins to celebrate the Winter season! During the celebration, the Advent Calendar will be opened for visitors, the Holiday Dream Neopet Giveaway will appear, and the Snowager will be hibernating. Neopians will be able to steal one item from the Snowager for each day of the month.


▸ Is it true that you cannot to obtain the Snowager avatar during the Winter Starlight Celebration?
As the Snowager will never blast you, it is true that you will not be able to obtain the avatar in December.


▸ What is the Holiday Dream Neopet Giveaway?
The Holiday Dream Neopet Giveaway is a site-wide giveaway where players can enter in hopes of their pet to be changed into any Converted colored species of their liking (including the exclusive Ice Bori). There will 40 winners from a random draw and winners be announced in the New Features on Christmas day.


▸ Am I allowed to participate in the Dream Pet Giveaway on my side account?
You are allowed to participate in the Dream Pet Giveaway on your side account, but you are only allowed to participate on one account.


▸ What is Charity Corner?
Hosted by Granny Hopbobbin, Charity Corner is a semi-chaotic annual/biannual event where players are asked to donate their items for a specified cause in hopes of rewards such as item prizes, an avatar, and more. The event is based off a point system and it lasts for about a week where many players will be scouring the site in order to find as many items to donate as they can. At the end of the event, players can receive a site trophy, Neopoints, Neocash, and sometimes additional item prizes based off the amount of donations they made in the event.

In the past, this event has given out different rewards:
- Item rewards within the same rarity of the items donated (i.e. Five r90-r99 for one random r90-r99 item)
- Exclusive item rewards redeemed with points via a prize shop
- Site perks redeemed with points that can grant increased inventory size, reduced game avatar scores, etc.

Jellyneo's Charity Corner Articles
jellyneo.net/?go=charity_corner

SunnyNeo's Charity Corner Articles
sunnyneo.com/charitycorner/index.php


▸ What are the best items to stock up for Charity Corner?
The best items to donate are cheap higher rarity items in the r90-r97, r98-r100, and r102-r179 range. Items below r80, r80-r89, and r101 are okay to stock up on, but for some players, purchasing those en masse might be extremely monotonous.

Most players would stop at a total CC Point amount of 10,001 (not 10,000) for that is the minimum amount needed for the highest tier Site Trophy.


▸ When is Charity Corner usually held?
Charity Corner is usually done on an annual/biannual seasonal basis. If the last event was in the Autumn season, the next one would be done around the Winter season. This is not always true and TNT sometimes gives a heads up a week or two in advance.


▸ I hear people talking about going for the Rubbish avatar during Charity Corner. What's up with that?
The Rubbish avatar (not Rubbish Dump / That's Not Rubbish avatar) is based off the amount of items discarded throughout an account's lifetime, and since Granny Hopbobbin actually discards all your items, all those donations are counted towards the avatar.


▸ What is the Altador Cup?
The Altador Cup is Neopets's version of the Olympics except it happens once a year in the Summer and lasts about a month. 18 lands across Neopia compete with each other over who's the best in Yooyuball, Slushie Slinger, Make Some Noise, and Shootout Showdown.


▸ When is the Altador Cup usually?
The Altador Cup usually happens around July. A reminder message usually appears a week before sign-ups start as a reminder for players to redeem their remaining points from last year's prize shop. When sign-ups are over, they're over for the year.

Jellyneo's Altador Cup Articles
bookofages.jellyneo.net/events/altador-cup/

TDN's Altador Cup Articles
thedailyneopets.com/altador-cup/index.php

SunnyNeo's Altador Cup Articles
sunnyneo.com/altadorcup/.php


▸ How do Prize Points work in the Altador Cup?
The Prize Points you get at the end are equal to your Altador Cup rank points, which are based on the amount of qualifying game scores you send during the event. Assuming you don't accidentally send any scores below the requirement, you can usually easily calculate the number of points you'll get by looking at the number of each of the 4 games you've played during that Altador Cup season. The most recent absolute minimum required game score is:

Games
Max Plays
AC Points
Yooyuball
46
552 max (12 for win, 4 for draw/loss)
Slushie Slinger
86
516 (6 AC Pts. each, score 270+ required)
Make Some Noise
401
401 (1 AC Pt. each, score 2700+ required)
Shootout Showdown
401
401 (1 AC Pt. each, score 35+ required)


▸ Do I get a new Altador Cup team avatar by joining a different team the next year?
Well yes, but actually no. You do get a new Altador Cup team avatar, but you also lose your previous one if you had one prior. This is to promote fairness to those who remain loyal to a certain team.


▸ Does it matter which Altador Cup team I pick?
No, the only final feature that changes is your trophy appearance, depending on how well that team performed that season.


▸ Does it matter if I submit the absolute minimum required score?
While it has not been concretely proven, it does affect your team's overall score, so you'll see some Neopians give a bit more effort in the games to support their teams.

If you value your sanity, submitting the minimum required score is completely fine if you just want the prize points and cooler trophies.


▸ Am I allowed to play multiple Altador Cup game tabs to save time?
No, you are not allowed to play on multiple game tabs as that is a freezable offense.

- Neopets Editorial - Issue 786 | Question 2 [link] (You are NOT allowed to play multiple Flash Games on multiple tabs/browsers/etc.)


▸ What is All-Star and what is the most efficient way to get it?
All-Star is the final shield rank you can earn in the Altador Cup. This can be achieved by submitting a monumental amount of qualifying game scores throughout the event. You can click the button next in the Your Stats section of the Altador Cup Home page to check your progress to the next rank.


▸ What are Break/Bye Days?
Break/Bye Days are days in the event where players cannot earn points towards their rank and relax for the time being. This is for TNT to organize the next round and you will always face the Practice Team on these days.


▸ What does it mean when people on the NeoBoards say to "Lock the Brackets?"
It's not something you have to worry about if you're just playing for prize points and the trophy, as the controversy surrounding the tournament brackets is only relevant to those who are invested in the results and the inner workings of the tournament. Altador Cup is split into two rounds, the first being held in a Round Robin tournament format. Depending on each team's performance in the first round, they are then sorted into a high, mid, and low-tier bracket for the second round where they subsequently face off against every other team in their bracket.

In past incarnations of this tournament format, TNT allowed teams to rise or fall into a higher or lower bracket depending on their performance in the second round, which many feel invalidates the results of the first round. It also incentivizes stronger teams to purposely place in a lower bracket so they can easily defeat the weaker teams in the second round and rise into the top bracket/onto the podium with their strong showing and without much effort while all of the initial top bracket struggle against each other. Hence, the term "Lock the Brackets" is repeated by many in hopes that TNT will remove the mechanic of teams changing tiers in the second round.

As of the 2020 Altador Cup, TNT has finally acknowledged the issue and locked the brackets, and this change is expected to apply to future tournaments.


▸ What is the TNT Staff Tournament and how does it work?
The TNT Staff Tournament is an optional side activity to the main Altador Cup event. Players can create their dream TNT Altador Cup team and see who will be the best of them all. There are four rounds, another side game of "who will be the Star Player?", and a prize shop at the end.


▸ What is a Star Player?
A Star Player is the most notable TNT Staff member in the round. If you guess the Star Player correctly, then you'll win an item award that may or may not be in the prize shop. It's rigged and TNT can select anyone they want for any arbitrary reason to be the Star Player.


▸ Is it worth investing in the Star Player rewards?
There is a gamble, since the item might or might not be in the prize shop at the end, but the prizes for correctly predicting the Star Player are usually if not all just collectors items with little to no actual usage.


▸ What is Daily Dare?
The Daily Dare is an annual event where sibling rivals, AAA and Abigail, and occasionally some nerd, Chadley, challenge Neopians in some Flash Game fun! Neopians are given a Flash Game score to beat and are awarded with items (and occasionally stat boosts) for winning. AAA and Chadley are the more difficult challengers to face while Abigail has the lower score, and you have to pick either of them to challenge for the day. If you choose the harder score, make sure you are able to beat it as you cannot change your challenger after making your selection, so think carefully.

This event can award avatars, a Site Event trophy, and a site theme, on top of exclusive prizes for beating your chosen challenger every day!


▸ What is the Games Master Challenge?
The Games Master Challenge is kinda like a diet version of the Daily Dare. The event lasts for about a week and the date of the event is sporatic, being either in the Springtime or Autumn. In terms of mechanics, AAA and Abigail have set up a themed showdown between two opposing forces (Brains vs Brawn, Pirates vs Ninja, Fire vs Ice, etc.) where Neopians can choose a side to help claim victory at the end. The item prizes, qualified game listing, and rules are the same for both sides. The sign-up reward, game challenges, and trophy appearance are different.


▸ How do I get the Daily Dare Site Theme?
In order to obtain the Daily Dare Site Theme, you need to participate in the Daily Dare. Just go complete a challenge if we ever have another Daily Dare in the future.

Jellyneo's Daily Dare & Games Master Challenge Articles
bookofages.jellyneo.net/events/daily-dare/

TDN's Daily Dare & Games Master Challenge Articles
thedailyneopets.com/daily-dare/index/

SunnyNeo's Daily Dare & Games Master Articles
sunnyneo.com/dailydare.php
sunnyneo.com/gmc.php


▸ What is the difference between a gold and green checkmark in DD/GMC?
A gold checkmark indicates that you completed the challenge on the day of release while the green checkmark indicates that you completed the challenge after the day of release. It is encouraged that you complete the challenges on the day of release for additional awards, but it is not necessary with regards to your trophy placement.

For the Games Master Challenge, there is also an additional final prize for getting full gold checkmarks throughout the event. The additional final prize is usually a wearable and/or collectible item.


▸ Am I still eligible for the final rewards if I miss a gold checkmark in the Daily Dare/Games Master Challenge?
You will still get some prizes and your trophy even if you miss a gold checkmark, but you will need to complete the challenge(s) on each release day in order to get the best possible prize (it's usually a valuable collectible item).


▸ Would my game score still count if I already submitted the maximum of three scores per day?
Unfortunately, no. If you happen to submit the maximum of three scores per day, but fail to beat the given score, then you will have to try the next day after your score submissions reset (which excludes you from getting a gold checkmark for that day).


▸ What is a Double Dare?
A Double Dare is a feature in the Daily Dare where if you beat AAA/Chadley's score, you'll get Abigail's awards as well.


▸ What is a Team Challenge?
On some days for a limited amount of time, you (and a partner) are given the opprotunity to participate in a Team Challenge! Team Challenges are an optional feature in the Daily Dare where you and another Neopian pair up and see if you can both beat AAA/Chadley or Abigail's score for an additional award! You are not required to participate in the Team Challenge if you do not wish to rely on another Neopian sending in their score (and possibly terminating your checkmark streak if they fail to do so).

Also, it is good etiquette to have the score ready to send before accepting/creating an invite.


▸ Where am I supposed to find a partner for the Team Challenge? I don't have any Neofriends.
You can find a partner for the Team Challenge over at the Games NeoBoard Chat, Site Events NeoBoard Chat, or Help NeoBoard Chat. It is advised that you check the last post to see who still needs a partner for the event.


▸ What is the Festival of Neggs?
The Festival of Neggs is an annual event where Neopians can participate in some Easter Negg Hunting! The event is usually hosted by Kari, the Negg Faerie, or Topsi (and sometimes with additional assistance). They will provide hints for finding a Negg hidden on one of the site pages every day, and players can receive Negg themed prizes such as food, wearables, books, stamps, etc. and a Site Theme! The event is usually live during the Springtime for about two weeks.


▸ Where can I find the locations of the hidden Neggs?
The Site Events NeoBoard Chat and Help NeoBoard Chat will usually have a dedicated thread with the locations. You can also check out official fansites such as Jellyneo, The Daily Neopets, and Sunnyneo for the answer as well.

Jellyneo's Festival of Neggs Articles
jellyneo.net/?go=festival_of_neggs

TDN's Festival of Neggs Articles
thedailyneopets.com/articles/festival-neggs-20

SunnyNeo's Festival of Neggs Articles
sunnyneo.com/neggfestival.php


▸ I'm at the location of the hidden Negg, but the Random Event isn't showing?
Make sure you visit the Festival of Neggs hub first to register in the event, and that you double-checked that the place is correct on a fansites such as Jellyneo, The Daily Neopets, and Sunnyneo. If you are still unable to locate the hidden Negg, then send in a ticket to the official FAQ for technical support. Note that some days have two possible Negg locations, so if you can't find it at the same place someone else did, your Negg is probably at the other location.


▸ How do I get the Festival of Neggs Site Theme?
In order to get the Festival of Neggs Site Theme, you need to find one hidden Negg. It doesn't have to be on the day of release.


▸ Do we get to choose which Neggs/Prizes we want? Is it really just 5 Neggs and 15 prizes total?
Yes, every FoN usually has 5 predetermined Specialty Neggs with 3 themed items per Negg. You'll be prompted with a random set of 3 of those Specialty Neggs and get to choose 1, which determines which themed item pool your prize will be from. The item you receive is random from the themed pool.


▸ What is the difference between a gold and green checkmark in the FoN?
A gold check mark indicates that you found the hidden Negg on the day of release while a green checkmark indicates that you found your Negg after the day of release. If you are able to collect every hidden Negg with a gold checkmark, then you'll get the final reward (it's usually a collectible item).


▸ Do I have to find the hidden Negg on the release day?
If you want the final award, then yes, you have to find every hidden Negg on each release day. The first day of the event usually lasts for a day and a half.


▸ Am I still eligible for the final reward if I miss a gold checkmark in the FoN?
Nope, they're pretty strict with the gold checkmarks for the final reward.


▸ What is the Faerie Festival? Is there anything interesting that happens on this date?
On September 20th, all the Faeries of Neopia gather in Faerieland to party in the Faerie Festival. All offical Faerieland Shops are 50% off (the Hidden Tower is excluded) and the Healing Springs will always fully heal your Neopets. There was a week-long event in 2017 one time with a mini-game, Wing-It, and an NC portion added.


▸ Are there any other holidays similar to the Faerie Festival?
Yes there are other special event days for certain lands and shops.

Usuki Day - Double stocks + 66.6% off all Usukiland items
Tyrannian Victory Day - 50% off all Tyranian items (except Ugga Shinies)
Meridell Day - 450 bonus points are added in Cheeseroller
Feb 12-14 - Gift Shop stocks A Mysterious Valentines Card in bulk

There are possibly more holiday speciatlies out there, so if you know any, please contact Chips.


▸ Will we ever see Wing-It again?
In an old Editorial, TNT has stated that it was a possibility that they will bring the game, Wing-It, back again in the future.

- Neopets Editorial - Issue 803 | Question 4 [link] (General Info)


▸ I though Faerie Quest Fortune Cookies would be discounted during Faerie Festival. Why are they not?
Faerie Quest Fortune Cookies are only discounted during the Faerie Quest Event, and not during the Faerie Festival on September 20th.


▸ What and when is the Faerie Quest Event then?
The Faerie Quest Event is a yearly event where the Faeries gather around and dedicate their efforts to repair Faerieland in some way. You get a one free Faerie Quest per day for visiting the quest homepage. You also get a Faerie themed prize for visiting each day, and there's usually a bonus prize for visiting each day.

The event usually happens around the Springtime.


▸ During the Faerie Quest Event, if I have an active Faerie Quest Fortune Cookie, which quest do I do first?
As of 2019's Faerie Quest Event, it does NOT matter which quest you accept first. Prior to 2019, you'd want to accept the cookie quest first, and then the event quest to prevent the event quest from overriding the cookie quest.

jellyneo.net/?go=faeriequestevents

thedailyneopets.com/articles/quests-2019

Neopian Times Related

▸ How do you submit a story/comic/article to the Neopian Times?
You can enter over here! You will be shown a list of possible submission sections (article, comic, stories) to choose, each with its own set of rules.


▸ Are there any rewards for being published in the Neopian Times?
Yes! You get a trophy for your publication, with a number below it indicating how many times you have been published before (e.g. 3x CHAMPION meaning you got published three times). You can also get an avatar by reaching certain milestones: as of now, you can get one for being published 10 times, and another one for being published in editions ending with 50 or 00, starting from issue 200.

On these special editions, you can also win special, exclusive item prizes! The prize depends on the issue, each one is different.


▸ Am I allowed to collaborate with another member on an Neopian Times entry?
Yes, you are! If you do, state in the comments, when sending your submission, that it has been done in collaboration, and cite the other person's UN. If you're published, you both get the rewards.


▸ Are Editorial questions counted as Neopian Times entries?
Editorial questions are not counted as entries. All other sections count, though.


▸ I didn't get my trophy/rewards from being published in the Neopian Times. What should I do?
Send a ticket to the Neopets Team (and NM tnt_aesop) detailing your publication and the issue of Neopian Times you've been published on. Remember Editorial doesn't count as a publication for avatar and rewards, though.


▸ I heard that referencing some modern technologies is not allowed to be mentioned in the Neopian Times. What might those subjects be?
Any tecnology that does not belong to the world of neopets. Such as cars, planes, videogames, computers (unless from Space Station), etc. As a general rule of thumb, try to use technologies that have already been created on the game by TNT, such as neomail, Virtupets spaceships, and bicycles. For a comprehensive list, click here.


▸ I'm collaborating with a friend, but my friend got frozen. Can I still enter our entries under both of our accounts even under their predicament?
If one of you has been frozen, the entry will not be published until he/she is unfrozen. Be sure that both of you follow the rules to not risk having your entry disqualified for this reason.


▸ Is there anything else I need to know about the Neopian Times?
It is extremely important to submit as early as possible, but the best time is two weeks prior the upcoming Wednesday. Getting into The Neopian Times can be difficult, and on some weeks, TNT may even announce that they will be skipping that week's issue of The Neopian Times.

Caption Contest Related

▸ What is the Caption Contest?
The Caption Contest is a monthly Creative Contest where users will enter their best descriptions for a provided image. These descriptions are usually a witty single sentence or short comedic dialogue between the Neopets/Petpets in the picture, for chance at being awarded a trophy, avatar, Neopoints, and a cool prize from an assortment of items. The first challenge is having your entry chosen and the real challenge is advertising your entry afterwards.


▸ What can I win from the Caption Contest?
The Caption Contest is considered a Creative Contest meaning you can win a random prize from a pool of awesome items! There are also Neopoints, trophies, and avatars for winning under certain conditions such as achieving certain placements and placing in certain rounds. A Ghostkerchief Pen was awarded on the 1,000th, 1,300th, 1,400th, and 1,420th round.

Caption Contest - Hilarious (the Aisha) is being awarded to the top 5 winners in every non-10th round of the Caption Contest starting from Round #1407. On round #1420 and #1430, any winner in the top 25 who already had the "Caption Contest - Funny" avatar was awarded this avatar.

Caption Contest - Funny (the Grundo) is being awarded to the top 25 winners in every 10th round ever since Round #1400. Prior to Round #1400, it was awarded every 100th rounds.

Jellyneo's Creative Contest Rewards
jellyneo.net/?go=contestprizes


▸ Is there a limit on how many entries I can enter?
There is no limit on how many entries you can enter in the Caption Contest.


▸ How many times can I vote for a caption entry? Am I allowed to vote for my own entry?
You can vote every 4 hours and you are allowed to vote for your own Caption. However, you are still limited to one vote every 4 hours.


▸ Am I allowed to vote from side accounts?
You are NOT allowed to vote from side accounts.


▸ Who decides which Caption Contest entry gets in? What's allowed in the Caption Contest?
TNT handpicks the CC entries themselves. Your entry must be family friendly and within Neopets rules. Overused jokes and clichés are discouraged, but they are often chosen in the Caption Contest nowadays. You can find a short list of rejected phrases over at the Caption Contest FAQ here.


▸ What are the rules of advertising my Caption Contest entry?
The rules are simliar to the Beauty Contest, but here's a quick rundown:
- You are allowed to advertise anywhere on the NeoBoards with your CC entry in your signature (NOT the post).
- For NeoBoard advertising, your post has to be on-topic to the NeoBoard and contribute to the thread's discussion.
- For Guild advertising, same rules as two above. You are NOT allowed request votes in your Guilds.
- You are NOT allowed to create a thread/post that is purely for CC entry advertising (aka asking for votes).
- You are NOT allowed to spam short NeoBoard responses like gl, lol, BFA, etc.
- You are NOT allowed to trade/buy votes.
- You are NOT allowed to advertise off-site (including Neopets's own social medias).
- You are NOT allowed to advertise from your shop.
- You are NOT allowed to advertise/ask for votes for another person's entry.
- You are NOT allowed to advertise/vote from your side account.
- You are NOT allowed to advertise on the Notice Boards.
- You are allowed to advertise from your userlookup and pet's userlookup.
- Advertising through petpages and neomails are a gray area and can be reportable as spam varying on the situation.

▸ I placed in the Caption Contest, but I did not get my trophy and rewards. What's up with that?
You'll have to send a ticket for that. Sometimes TNT will forget about that.


▸ I saw that someone was able to get more than one entry in the Caption Contest. What's up with that?
They'll have to send a ticket for that. It's an uncommon error on TNT's end.


▸ When does a new Caption Contest round start and when do they end?
The Caption Contest usually starts a week before the month ends. The contest itself tends to end within the first week of the next month.

TNT Staff Lore Related

▸ So uhh, who are Jumpstart and what was the transition like back then?
JumpStart Games (owned by NetDragon as of July 3, 2017) is an edutainmental game company that has owned Neopets as of March 17, 2014. Neopets was previously owned by Viacom and a multitude of major changes were made to the site during the year of the transition:

- Most of the previous Neopets Team were let go
- Key Quest, Habitarium, and Petpet Park were (forcefully) shut down
- A couple of NeoApocalypses here and there
- The release of the Vandagyre
- Ghoul Catchers was launched


▸ Who are the current TNT Staff members?
In Altador Cup 2020, TNT did a small introduction of a handful of the current TNT Staff members.

TNT's Small Intros
June 8th, 2020
June 1st, 2020


▸ Who on the current TNT has been on staff the longest?
From an Editorial response, DJ Skellington (Y4?) has been the longest serving TNT Staff member, followed by Kikocat (Y4), Binary_supagoo (Y7), and SenorMalo (Y7).

- Neopets Editorial - Issue 905 | Question 2 [link] (General Info)


▸ What was and happened to the NeoCam?
The NeoCam was an office monitor that would take a snapshot of the Neopets Office every fifteen seconds for players to get to know TNT more and to gain a sneak peek of potential future content in store for them. TNT would often showcase upcoming merchandise, Neopets cosplays, and other fun office shenanigans.

On May 16, 2007, the NeoCam stopped updating when Viacom TNT moved their office. Viacom (and at some point JumpStart) TNT contemplated the idea of bringing back the Neocam through the Editorial, but this site feature has yet to be revived. JumpStart TNT informed us that bringing back the NeoCam involved great difficulty due to a number of factors such as legal issues with other brands, requiring consent from all the staff members, and the change in office location, and so bringing the NeoCam back is currently infeasible.

- Neopets Editorial - Issue 897 | Question 2 [link] (General Info)


▸ Does the retired TNT Staff still play Neopets?
We have been told that Dragona and Snarkie occasionally play Neopets on their non-staff accounts.


▸ Is there anything else I need to know about TNT Lore?
If you type Asparagus, Cheat, Jelly, or Treasure in the Search Bar, you'll get a pretty fun Easter Egg!

Special thanks and FAQ contributions here from Gigantera (Advent Calendar) and riparu (Altador Cup).

Art / Creative FAQs

Creative Contest Related

▸ What is the Art Gallery?
The Art Gallery (AG) is an art competition where you submit your own artwork for upcoming scheduled pet days, Neopian holidays, or a miscellaneous topic. User entries are pooled and winners are chosen by TNT Kikocat (tnt_contest_judge) based on one-to-two page space constraints.


▸ How do I win Art Gallery?
Create your art to reflect canon Neopets designs, and submit it 1-2 days before your chosen topic is due to show up in the news. Kikocat posts her schedule in the Art Chat, under Art Gallery Schedules. She replies to questions about the AG/BC on these boards, but the replies will self delete in a few days after posting.

Remember to save your art in all lowercase characters — Kikocat may not be able to see your submission if there are any uppercase characters.


▸ What can I win from Art Gallery?
For all Creative Contest, you can win a random prize from a pool of awesome items! These prizes range from Paint Brushes, Secret Laboratory Map pieces, Petpets, etc. You will get a Neomail notification if you have been chosen.

Jellyneo's Creative Contest Rewards
jellyneo.net/?go=contestprizes


▸ Why did my entry get rejected/errored immediately from the Art Gallery?
Here's a quick list of reasons why your entry might be rejected from the art-related competitions:
- It wasn't your own artwork (stealing another member's artwork if a freezable offence).
- It has copyright or trademark symbols (having your UN is fine, but it cannot be copyrighted)
- It has won another art-related competition.
- It has little to no relation to Neopets at all.
- It exceeds the size limits.


▸ What are the size limits for the Art Gallery?
- Your image must be at most 600 pixels wide and 600 pixels tall.
- Your image must be at most 80 Kilobytes in size.
- Your image must be of file type .gif or .jpg.


▸ Are sketches allowed in the Art Gallery?
Sketch art pieces are usually rejected in the Art Gallery, but some completed pieces with sketch-like characteristics are allowed. TNT has provided a couple of examples of what would be accepted and not here:

Neopets Editorial - Issue 656 | Question 9 [link]

Hello, TNT! In Editorial #653, you said that sketches aren't allowed in the Art Gallery. May I ask what constitutes a sketch? For example, if an entry has tones and shading but is drawn in a sketchy style, would that be acceptable? Thanks! ~dragonair23

This is, of course, a judgement call by our judges, as there is no fine line. Something unlikely to be accepted as possible winners are rough sketches or things like very simple pencil line drawings with no shading. A sketchy style is just fine as long as it comes across as a finished work of art, and not an incomplete one. Here are some compositions to help you get a better visual idea of what we're looking for:


Incomplete. Would not be accepted as an entry.


Acceptable, but feels incomplete.
Highly unlikely to win.


Completed pencil drawing with good chance to win.


Finished line art. Could be a complete composition,
but unlikely to win unless high quality
with good use of line weight.

▸ Does my Art Gallery entry have to be on paper/digitally created?
Art Gallery submissions are not limited to paper/digital drawings! We have seen chalk, clay, and art drawn on rocks!


▸ Are collabs allowed in the Art Gallery?
Collaborative pieces are NOT allowed in the Art Gallery.

- Neopets Editorial - Issue 901 | Question 5 [link] (Collabs are NOT allowed in the Art Gallery)


▸ Am I allowed to enter more than one entry to the Art Gallery?
You are allowed to submit multiple entries (three per day) to the Art Gallery. Do know that only one of your entries will be picked if you happen to be chosen. Submitting multiple entries does not boost your chance of being chosen.


▸ So, I accidently submitted my winning Beauty Contest art piece to the Art Gallery? AM I IN TROUBLE???
You would want to neomail tnt_contest_judge about it. People make mistakes, there will be no punishment for the removal of that accidental Beauty Contest entry. Just don't make it into a habit and you will be fine.


▸ What is the Poetry Contest?
If drawing art isn't your expertise, Neopets has a poem writing competition! This is where you can showcase your poems, rhymes, and poetry talents. You can win 1,000 NP, a prize from the Creative Contest reward pool, and a cool trophy if you get chosen!


▸ So when is the Poetry Contest?
Nowadays, the Poetry Contest is released on Neopian holidays like pet days.


▸ Are collabs allowed in the Poetry Contest?
Collaborative pieces are NOT allowed in the Poetry Contest.


▸ Am I allowed to enter more than one entry to the Poetry Contest?
You are allowed to enter as many entries as you want! Do know that only one of your entries will be picked if you happen to be chosen. Submitting multiple entries does not boost your chance of being chosen.


▸ Will I get a rejection notice if my Poetry Contest entry doesn't make it in?
Yes you will! Sometimes rejection neomails are sent out within a couple of weeks or definitely within 24 hours of the actual release day if it is a Neopian holiday.


▸ What does it mean when my Poem is held over?
This means that your entry will definitely be used for another Poetry Contest round! You do not need to resubmit your entry if you get the Neomail.


▸ What is Pet/Petpet Spotlight?
The Pet/Petpet Spotlight was where members can write and share about their pet or petpet's character, adventures, and other novelties. You were allowed to enter in both spotlights on your side accounts as you were only awarded a trophy on your pet for winning.

Both spotlights have stopped updating since February 2019, but TNT has not declared them as retired/on hiatus.


▸ What is the Random Contest?
The Random Contest is mostly an art and crafts contest, but the randomness comes in what the topic of the theme might be. This could have been real-life food, pillowcases, and other arbitrary creations. The most current ones have been standard art.

There is no set schedule for the Random Contest anymore, it's pretty much when TNT feels like running one (which is probably like once a year).


▸ Is the Random Contest still active? When is the next one?
In a sense, the Random Contest is still alive. TNT would usually update in the Editorial and/or New Features when a new round up.


▸ Are collabs allowed in the Random Contest?
Collaborative pieces are allowed in the Random Contest, but they are judged more harshly than single entries.


▸ What is the User Lookup Spotlight?
The User Lookup Spotlight is where members can show off their Neo-HTML talents on their User Lookup!


▸ What is Gallery Spotlight?
The User Lookup Spotlight is where members can show off their item hoards and Neo-HTML talents on their Gallery.


▸ Are premades allowed in the Gallery/User Lookup Spotlight?
Premades are allowed if the original source was credited and that the layout is not too similar to the original design. Premades that were edited slightly or layouts there are practically claiming stolen art/premade work as your own would not be accepted.

Neopets Editorial - Issue 718 | Question 2 [link]

Dear CQ: I'm so confused! Today's news (4th February), after announcing the User Lookup of the Week winner, notes that a premade lookup is not allowed in the contest, and that submitting one could get us a warning and our trophy removed. I always thought that premades were just fine in the contest, as long as the content was ours and proper credit was given. Well, I looked it up! In the Editorial on issue 570 of the Neopian Times, published on the 9th day of Storing, Y14, there is an answer that seems to contradict today's news. Could you clarify? I've never sent in an entry to the contest, but I'd like to know what's allowed, for when I do. Thanks, CQ! I'll send you all the cookies!! ~ penelopedastardly ​

Hi! Alright, to help clear up your confusion, there are essentially 3 different scenarios of using help, I felt fancy and listed them out nicely below (also we get a lot of entries that don't seem to totally understand the difference, so hopefully this will help!):

Scenario 1: You look at some premades or tutorials for coding help, and use that to help you make your own. Your userlookup gives credit to wherever you received help from, but is not essentially that premade lookup with a couple changes.

Outcome: You're good! Submit that thing and hope for the best! This is what that previous editorial was talking about :)

Scenario 2: Your lookup is completely a premade, you made little or no change to it, and submit. It probably says somewhere "Lookup Coded by XXX", someone who is not you.

Outcome: Nice lookup, and you will not get in trouble, but you will also not win a User Lookup spotlight, because we do not accept premades.

Scenario 3: You use a lovely premade you found somewhere for your User Lookup with little or no changes to it, but somehow that little line of credit got left out *shifty eyes*

Outcome: Not cool man! If that happens, we usually can't tell its a premade, and it could be spotlighted. If so, usually lots of helpful users let us know whats up (sorry we can't always tell guys, we just can't learn them all. Plus sometimes we see it happen where they change the main picture so it's not easily recognizable either. Ugh.). Here is where you find yourself in hot water. We'll replace your entry, remove your trophy and give you a warning (the first time, if we catch you doing something like this again in any spotlight, you won't be so lucky).


▸ Does our Gallery/User Lookup Spotlight entries have to be Neopets related?
User Lookup Spotlight entries do have to relate to Neopets in some way with the addition of the Spotlight Rules. Gallery Spotlight entries can pretty much be anything as long it follows Spotlight Rules.

Neopets Editorial - Issue 560 | Question 4 [link]

I'd really like to make a User Lookup and submit it to the spotlight, but I was wondering if my submission would be accepted if it was not Neopets-themed. For example, if I had a well-coded Star Trek-themed lookup, would I still have a chance at winning the spotlight? Thanks! :D ~mariesg1

Nope. Only Neopets-themed content is considered for any of our creative contests, including the User Lookup Spotlight, no matter how well done the submission is.


▸ Am I allowed to enter in the Gallery/User Lookup Spotlight on a side account?
You are allowed to participate in the Gallery/User Lookup Spotlight on a side account.


▸ Are rejection notices still given out to the Gallery/User Lookup Spotlight?
Rejection notices are still given out for the User Lookup Spotlight, but not the Gallery Spotlight.


▸ Are Neocash items necessary for Gallery Spotlight?
Neocash items are not required nor necessary for the Gallery Spotlight.


▸ Is there anything else I need to know about Creative Contests?
If you didn't find the answer here about your Creative Contest inquiry, then you can always ask the Help NeoBoard Chat or Art NeoBoard Chat for assistance! Here are a couple guides for Creative Contests as well:

Beauty Contest Related

▸ What is the Beauty Contest?
The Beauty Contest (BC) is an art-themed Creative Contest where you draw your Neopet and advertise in hopes of getting them a shiny trophy (+ avatar for yourself). You may draw from scratch or edit an official Neopets image, but if you do the latter, alterations must look like they took at least five minutes to be accepted.


▸ What can I win from the Beauty Contest?
If you win 1st, 2nd, or 3rd in species and/or overall, you will earn a trophy for your pet's lookup! Winning overall will give you a second trophy, along with your species win. Placing top 3 in any of the species will award the avatar.


▸ When does the Beauty Contest start/restart?
The BC starts around 12:10 PM - 12:15 PM NST on every Friday. The time seems to vary some weeks, but that's the general timeline.

NOTE: If you submit a drawing too close to the deadline, your entry may take a while to be visible and voted for (as Kikocat has to approve of entries before they can be made public), so it's best advised to submit either before or on the Wednesday before your desired week.


▸ What are the size limitation for the Beauty Contest?
- Your image must be at most 75 Kilobytes in size.
- Your image must be of file type .gif or .jpg.
- Optional, but you would want your image must be at most 800 pixels wide and 800 pixels tall to avoid screen stretching in your Beauty Contest entry.


▸ How many times can I vote in the Beauty Contest?
You can vote once per species. So be certain that you want to vote for an entry, as you won't get your votes back even if the entry is removed! You may also ONLY vote on your MAIN account. Using multiple accounts to vote is cheating. However, if you do accidentally vote on a side account, be sure to not do it again for that species on your main and to finish voting on your main. TNT understands that we make mistakes, but it's obvious when you're doing it on purpose to either raise your voting amount or the amount of an entry you really like.


▸ Does the color of my pet have to match my Beauty Contest submission?
Nope! It just has to be the same species.


▸ Am I allowed to enter in the Beauty Contest on my side accounts?
Yes, you may enter from a side account, BUT you must advertise your entries from the account(s) your pet(s) are on, and ONLY vote from your main.


▸ What are the easiest/hardest species to compete with in the Beauty Contest?
The popular species, such as Cybunny, Kougra, Lupe, Aisha, and Draik tend to be super hard and only for the brave-of-heart. Unpopular species such as Ruki, Quiggle, Nimmo, Tonu, and Tuskaninny are generally very empty and may also be filled with repeated entries. They may have their rough weeks, but generally, they are rather easy. Medium categories encompass species such as Shoyru, Gelert, and Peophin; they are rather popular. However, an easy category can become hard, and a hard category can become easy, just like that. There's no way to really determine how the categories will turn out until the new contest rolls around.

Beauty Contest Popularity Chart
/~Colress


▸ Where can I advertise my Beauty Contest entry?
As of March 2020, you are now allowed to advertise your Beauty Contest entries in your neoSignature anywhere on the NeoBoards! You used to be limited to the Art Chat, Spotlight Chat, and Premium Chat (Charter).

Not new, but aside from the NeoBoards, you are allowed to advertise your Beauty Contest entry on your Userlookup, Pet's Lookup, and Petpages.

Do remember to practice good posting etiquette, don't just pop into threads and say "GL" for that is considered spam. Neomailing your NeoFriends to ask them to check out your BC entry is fine if they are okay with getting them. If they are not okay with your Beauty Contest advertising Neomails, they are allowed to report it as spam. Very recently, bumping your own thread, outside the Art/Spotlight/Premium Chat, with the context only being your BC entry in that post is now considered spam

Neopets Editorial - Issue 902 | Question 2 [link]

Hi! I hope you are all doing well. Is there any chance you could let us know if advertising Beauty Contest entries on chat boards other than the Art Chat is allowed? Previously, in issue 887's editorial, it seemed like you reconsidered and would allow it so long as players were making real, substantive posts on chat topics and not brief token posts like "GL!" Or did you mean for the advice you gave in NT issue #887 to only apply to players trying to drum up votes in the Caption Contest? Thanks for your time & please remove my UN. ~Name Removed

Hi, That is for the Beauty Contest (Caption Contest also) but you can post your link in your Neosig outside the Art, Spotlight and Premium boards now (ONLY in your Neosig though) as long as you are contributing to the conversation.


▸ Art-wise, what is not allowed in the Beauty Contest?
Here's a quick list of things not allowed, art-wise, in the Beauty Contest:
- Humans are allowed in the BC, but they CANNOT be the main focus; You are allowed to enter anthro (Neopets with human features) drawings, but NO humans with Neopet features (ex. Aisha ears or a Gelert tail). Humans overall are a grey area.
- Suggestive content and nudity are NOT allowed. Topless males are okay.
- Also, NO real life weapons. Neopets weapons are okay.
- NO religious symbols or flags. Neopian and Altador Cup flags are okay.
- NO violence or death scenes. Make sure your entry is G-rated.


▸ Can I reuse a Beauty Contest entry?
Yes and no. You may use an entry more than once (although it's generally frowned upon by the art chat if it's placed before), but there are some conditions.

1. Entries can only be used for ONE pet, even if you transfer or morph the pet later.

2. If the art entry has won gold, it CANNOT be entered again. Draw a new piece, keep those creative juices flowing!

3. An entry CANNOT be used in multiple creative contests. If it has won any trophies from the Beauty Contest, you may not re-use it for the Art Gallery, or vice versa!

4. Reusing the same lineart (for example, an adoptable you made) is NOT allowed if it has won gold for another pet. Again, the pic has to be entirely new and not just re-edited to enter for another pet.
(Note: Rule 4 was stated by Kikocat at one point, during one of her boards.)


▸ Am I allowed to reuse my art for the Art Gallery/Beauty Contest/Pet Spotlight/etc.?
If you did not win a contest or spotlight with that art piece, you are allowed to submit it to a different competition. The only time you are allowed to reuse the same art piece multiple times after winning is for the Beauty Contest, if you adhere to its rules.


▸ Are collabs allowed in the Beauty Contest?
Collaborative pieces are NOT allowed in the Beauty Contest.


▸ What is the difference between Silent Voting, Non-Silent Voting, and Manual Voting?
Silent Voting (SVing) is when you are voting for Beauty Contest entries, but you are not publicly stating whose. Non-Silent Voting (NSVing) is when you are publicly posting who you are voting for. Manual Voting (MVing) is when you are just browsing through the Beauty Contest voting pages and picking which entries you like.

Manual Voting Quicklink Page
/~Snapsdile


▸ Am I allowed to trade/buy votes?
No, you are NOT allowed to exchange/purchase Beauty Contest votes with/from another user.


▸ What is a Gold Ban (or being Goldbanned)?
A Gold Ban is when you win first place and are rewarded with a 30-day ban from the Beauty Contest on your pet because you were amazing! It's nothing bad as this was implemented to prevent repeated wins from the same pet/person. Before August 25, 2017, the ban duration was 4 months long!


▸ Is there anything else I need to know about the Beauty Contest?
If you didn't find the answer here about your Beauty Contest inquiry, then you can always ask the Help NeoBoard Chat or Art NeoBoard Chat for assistance! Also, here are some guides:

▸ What is Board Stretching and is it bad?

(By the way, accounts are limited to 20 characters, but since we don't use fixed-width fonts on Neopets, some letters are much wider than others and two UNs of 20 characters might be quite different in length!)

Avatars FAQs

▸ What are avatars?
They are the tiny (and sometimes animated) GIFs that appear on everyone's userlookup and NeoBoard posts!


▸ What can I do with Avatars?
You can collect them and show them off to your friends. There is also a trophy for collecting avatars. ;)

Collecting Avatars Related

▸ Where do I start collecting avatars?
A solid start is getting the clickable avatars - all you need to get those is a link! JellyNeo has a pretty good page on how to get them:

JN's Avatar Checklist Pet Page Tool
jellyneo.net/avatars/

Viewable Avatar Reference
/~Avatiers


▸ Can I collect avatars on my side account?
Yes and no! Side account rules apply to avatar collecting, which means you can't do any activities that earn you NPs or tradeable items. You can, however, collect:

- All clickable avatars;
- The following annually available avatars: Blumaroo - Chef Bonju, Happy Birthday!, Easter Cybunny, Quiguki April Fools Avatar, Gadgadsbogen!, Valentine Chia, I *heart* Sloth.
- Most item-related avatars (except the ones that require you to buy in Neopian shops), just as long as the item comes from your main account or someone lends it to your side;
- Most pet/petpet-related avatars, except for Good Day at the Bank. If the avatar requires your pet to interact with an item, it must come from your main account.

Scroll Avatar Reference & Allowed Side Account List
/~Mustala

Neopets Editorial - Issue 310 | Question 1 [link]

My friend's MAIN account was recently suspended for around 2 days (48 hrs.). However, she created a side account at the time so she could continue to chat in the guild and such. She then also began to get avatars, though. I read some previous Editorials and learned that playing games were not allowed. So does that also mean earning avatars, even if the avatars were from games? Also, because her account was suspended, there was no way of sending the Neopoints or items to her main in the first place. Mk. Thanks. (: ~omgringo

Earning certain kinds of avatars on side accounts is fine, like clickables or ones where you need a certain type of Neopet or Petpet, etc. Avatars that require you to play games or do dailies that can grant you either NP or an item is off-limits on side accounts, though. You may not use side accounts as mains during suspension periods.


▸ Is there any occasion where a retired avatar is rereleased?
Very rarely TNT deems fit to rerelease a retired avatar, but you definitely shouldn't count on it! It's best to be safe than sorry with avatars, as you never know if or when they'll be gone.


▸ What is Avatar Simon?
It's a game commonly played on the Avatar Chat. It's played in rounds, and in each one OP will randomly pick one of their avatars; the players must quickly change their active avatar to the same OP picked, and a player gets eliminated when OP changes their avatar to one they don't have. It'll go like this for a few rounds until eventually, only one player will stay, and thus win.

Do keep in mind that you can't actually earn anything from this, though, as it isn't an official Neopets game - it's just for fun!


▸ Is there anything else I need to know about collecting avatars?
Don't get yourself down if you're unable to get an avatar as quick compared to others. Collecting some avatars might take time, patience, and/or dedication to achieve!

Avatar Lending Related

▸ What is avatar lending?
Lending is when another player lets you borrow one of their items or pets so you can get a shiny new avatar!



▸ What type of avatar lends are there?
There are item lends and pet lends.

Item lends are usually done using the Trading Post or Give to NeoFriend function. The Trading Post is more used when you are lending multiple items and/or the lender is wanting collateral for their item lend. The Give to Neofriend function is much quicker than the Trading Post, but there is no confirmation when the item is received.

Pet lends are usually done by adopting pets from the Pound or transferring pets from accounts lending avatar pets. Most avatar pets in the pound tend to have a stuck name (cannot be found in the pound normally unless its name is searched directly) which makes adopting and abandoning to the next account quite quick and easy. Transferring avatar pets requires you to use up a "transfer" which is a direct send or swap to your account. The number of transfers you can get is tied to your account age. Some pet lends might require your account to be at least four months old. An explanation on pet transfers can be found here:

JN's Neopian Pound Guide
jellyneo.net/?go=pound#transfer


▸ What is the procedure of getting a lend of an avatar item/pet?
You either create a thread on the Avatar NeoBoard Chat asking for the specific item you want to borrow or you wait until you see someone on the boards lending the item/pet you want.


▸ What is collaterial?
Collateral is a sort of warranty you send for the lender in exchange for the item, just in case something happens to it; it can be either partial or full, and pure or in items. A full collateral is the entire value of the item you're asking a lend, whereas a partial collateral is only a fraction of it; pure means you have the value (be it partial or full) in Neopoints, and in items means you have it in easy-to-sell items such as the Baby Paint Brush.


▸ Where do I find these avatar lenders?
They're usually lurking around the Avatar NeoBoard Chat waiting for a board asking for an item to be created, but sometimes they create boards announcing the items they have to lend themselves.

It's common courtesy not to send Neomails to lenders unless they specifically say their inbox is open to those, and not to disclose the UNs of lenders with more expensive avatar items as to not attract attention from malicious players to their accounts.


▸ How do I make my account worthy of being lent an avatar item?
You can get easy avatars in order to increase your count, paint your pets, get game trophies, be active on the forums, etc. Anything that lets others know you're dedicated to your account will raise your chances of getting a lend! Even a simple user lookup made by you from scratch, instead of opting for a premade, goes - remember that most of the time the people letting you borrow their hard-earned items and pets won't know you at all and vice-versa, so all they'll have to judge if you can get an item or not is your account and how hard you work on it. Don't get discouraged if someone doesn't lend you an item and ask the lender what you could improve on your account instead!


▸ Are you allowed to profit off avatar lends?
Absolutely not! Lending should be done out of the person's own goodwill, and trying to profit from it in any way is against the rules.

Neopets Editorial - Issue 276 | Question 5 [link]

On the Quest Board, users often create posts saying "Quest Help for 250 NP!" Their topic then says that they will look up an item on the Shop Wizard, put the item in their shop, and add an extra 250 NPs to the price so that they can earn a profit. (Of course, they're free to set their own shop prices.) We regular QB helpers believe this is a scam, although a blatantly stated one. By using the FREE Shop Wizard, this person will earn NPs because someone else cannot use the SW. They argue that this is not stated in the rules; therefore, they can do it. We counter that chat rule #6, which doesn't let you perform services for NPs, makes this a scam. We would just like clarification as to whether saying "I am charging you for my help." is against the rules or not. Thanks. ~alatyr13

You are quite correct that this type of activity is not allowed! Those who try to charge others for services, be it art, avatar lending, or using the SSW or normal Shop Wizard will get this lovely little warning in their Neomail inbox:

You may not ask for or offer any services or use Neopets images or materials to earn money, Neopoints, or Neopets' Items. This is a violation of Neopets copyright and trademark rights and the Terms and Conditions, and is strictly forbidden.

There are a remarkable number of ways to make Neopoints that don't resort to breaking the Terms and Conditions of the site. Perhaps those trying to sell services should look into them.


▸ What happens when someone steals an avatar item from the lender?
Unfortunately, TNT doesn't entirely endorse avatar lending; while they let players lend items and pets as they please, they don't encourage it. That doesn't mean that if someone steals an item they'll get away with it, though - stealing is completely against the site rules and the offender will get their account frozen, but it's not always that TNT will be able to get the stolen item back to its original owner.

Neopets Editorial - Issue 308 | Question 16 [link]

Hello TNT, you guys are doing an awesome job! You rock! Anyway, people on the boards are trading items (such as chokatos, to get the avvie) and then giving it back to the owner. People are getting **RARE** items for free, and it's not fair to the Neopians who are working hard to earn NP to buy rare items and get the avvie. Also, some people are complaining that they got their items stolen from item lending. Isn't that against the rules?!? If it IS against the rules, isn't it their own fault for their items getting stolen? Please leave my name out. Thankies! ~ [removed]

Lending items isn't currently against the rules. Item/NP pools for avatars or paying for a lend are, though. As long as those aren't going on it's okay. While, of course, we'd prefer that people earn their own way, we can't really look down upon those who are kind enough to share the wealth. We salute those who continue to show empathy by lending items despite knowing full well that there are a horrid number of dishonest folk who will take advantage of others' kindness and steal. Those are the players we truly frown upon. (Seriously, stealing from someone who's offering you their trust and generally being kind to others? How low can you possibly go? Certainly, nothing on Neopets is worth the loss of personal integrity... it just boggles our minds how anyone could do such a thing.) Anyway, if you've lent and been victimized by a dishonest player, please report him or her immediately with a clear description of what happened so that all their accounts can be frozen.

▸ Someone morphed and removed the Petpet/Petpetpet off an avatar pet? Is this a ticketable offense?
Sadly, no. Since TNT doesn't totally endorse avatar lending, they don't take responsibility for this kind of thing.

Neopets Editorial - Issue 753 | Question 5 [link]

I'd like a clarification of something from two weeks ago's editorial. "I recently created a new side account and adopted several neopets out of the pound. One of these Neopets had a petpet attached. At first, I thought I'd just leave it be, but then I looked the petpet up and found out it was valuable. Can I sell the petpet if I transfer it to my main first, or is this considered using a side account to cheat? P.S. Please remove my UN. ~ UN removed Hi! Hi! So the notice on the Pound page refers to trading Neopets for Neopoints (or neopoint items) via the Pound. You can trade Neopet for other Neopets, but not anything else, and doing so is a freezable offense. However, adopting a pet and realizing it has a petpet is a different issue - that's an item we cannot force you to keep (and we have no interest in doing so).


▸ Is there anything else I need to know about Avatar Lends?
If you plan to find or give out avatar lends, then doing it on the NeoBoards is the safest way.
