Battledome FAQs

▸ What is the Battledome?
The Battledome is a place where your Neopets can fight famous Neopian characters (and friends) for glory and riches! Get those Battledome weapons ready, because those opponents are waiting for ya!


▸ Can I win anything from battling? Is the Battledome worth it?
The Battledome is very well worth it as a daily! You can win Codestones, Dubloons, and other fun goodies! You do not get any NP or items when battling against another Neopian player (2-Player/2P), but it is still fun to try out!

Battledome Basics Related

▸ How do I get started with Battledome?
You just equip some weapons onto your pet and click around to fight around! You also have to train your pets too, but I'd check out these guides for a more detailed explaination on how to start the Battledome:

Battledome FAQ
/~silvercyanide4

JN's Battledome Beginner's Guide
battlepedia.jellyneo.net/?go=beginners

JN's Training Guides
jellyneo.net/?go=training
battlepedia.jellyneo.net/?go=beginners_guide_to_training

▸ Which Battledome opponent has the best daily prizes?
Well that depends on your stats, but overall these opponents yield the most choice rewards:

Beginner: Chia Clown and S750 Kreludan Defender Robot
Chia Clown for his Chocolate Ice Cream drop and Robot for his Neocola Tokens and small chance of Armoured Neggs. I recommend to challenge on Hard.

Intermediate: Koi Warrior //OR// Jetsam Ace (Premium Only)
Koi Warrior's area drops Codestones more frequently than others with the addition of Dubloons as well. Jetsam Ace drops Nerkmids. Challenge on their hardest difficulty if possible.

Advanced: Giant Spectral Mutant Walein //OR// Giant Space Fungus (Premium Only)
Fungus on Hard difficulty as it has a similar Nerkmid rate to Jetsame Ace but also gives out Bubbling Fungus. Non-premium players should challenge the Walein on Medium for the smallest challenger-specific prize pool and therefore higher codestone rate.


IF YOU HAVE PREMIUM, FIGHT THE PREMIUM FIGHTS IF YOU CAN


▸ Is there a limit of how many rewards I can get from the Battledome?
At max, you can win up to 1,500 NP and 15 items once per day. You can check the prize pools for the areana and challengers over at this guide:

JN's Battle Prizes Guide
battlepedia.jellyneo.net/?go=battle_prizes


▸ What weapons should I be using?
It depends on your what your current set is, stats, budget, and species. If you have a relevant goal such whether you aiming to beat any specific challengers, and whether you play 1P or 2P BD, you'd want to read up on what might be the best fit for your pet from the guides listed below. For 2P equipment advice, the Battledome NeoBoard Chat (or those dedicated League weapon petpages) would probably be your best bet.

Basic 1P Battledome Sets
/~Burrlee

JN's In-depth Battlepedia
battlepedia.jellyneo.net/


▸ Does it matter which species I have for the Battledome?
Your choice of species do not matter in the Battledome unless you wish to use certain healers and/or freezers. There used to be a feature called Species Resistances/Weaknesses, but those were all removed in the new Battledome.

Species With Notable Healers: Blumaroo, Elephante, Gelert, Lenny, Nimmo, Shoyru, Uni, and Kacheek.
Species Notable Freezers: Chia, Lenny, and Lupe (Fragile), and Peophin.


▸ Do icon types matter?
Icon typing is secondary in 1-P Battling. The reason being is that a large quantity of icons would be more practical when using abilities such as Lens Flare or Warlocks Rage, or when the opponent is frozen. Using a mass iconage might overcome your opponent's defensive capabilities.

In 2-P Battling icon typing plays a more important role as there are usually restrictions to using stunning abilities and/or freezing. You are going to have to strategize to work against your own and your opponent's dual-duties, shields, reflectors, etc.


▸ Is X Weapon any good?
I'd check out Jellyneo's In-Depth Battlepedia to see the weapon's information and reviews from the JN BD Staffers. You can always ask at the Battledome NeoBoard Chat if you want a response on how that weapon might be doing in this current day of age as well. If I'm gonna be real, like 95% of all weapons are pretty terrible in 1-Player BD.

JN's In-depth Battlepedia
battlepedia.jellyneo.net/


▸ Why can't I enter my pet in the Battledome?
This is a quick list of reasons why you cannot fight with your pet:
- Your pet has no/negative HP.
- Your pet is sick.
- Your pet is already fighting against another opponent.
- Your pet is being being transferred/travelling to another account.

▸ What are Faerie Abilities? What are the best ones?
Faerie Abilites are side skills that can be used when making a move. You can use them offensively, defensively, and even heal from them. The most notable abilities are An Icicle, Lens Flare, Warlock's Rage, Reflect, and Rejuvenate. This guide below goes in-depth on why are they're pretty awesome:

The Faerie Ability Guide
/~_mariokart_


▸ How do I beat X 1P opponent?
Some guides might have a brute force method, a cloak and dagger method, etc. I often just plan out on what my opponent's HP is and see what I can possibly do with my current set is, stats, budget, and species. 1P is all about maxing out your total damage output (or at least reaching the minimum of your opponent's HP).

If I have the NP and I wanna fight like Chia Clown or S750 Kreludan Defender Robot for the BD rewards, then I'll just get a Cursed Elixir and a Downsize!, because that'll allow me to drain all their HP without having me to heal afterwards. If I don't have the NP, then I'll use Scroll of Ultranovas to bash them in and heal myself with a Magical Healing Potion while using a Downsize! mid-battle.

If you need help formulating a strategy for Meuka, Black Pteri, Space Faerie, or even 2P battles, then I'd check out the Battledome NeoBoard Chat!


▸ Where can I unlock X opponent?
Jellyneo has a Checklist Tool for that! It'll provide you with all the instructions on how to unlock those opponents.

JN's Battledome Challenger Checklist Tool
battlepedia.jellyneo.net/?go=challenger_checklist


▸ How do I exit a battle?
Go to the Challenges Tab and click the big red button that says WITHDRAW. This will count as a loss.


▸ Does difficulty affect the Battledome rewards?
Kinda, but not really. Certain difficulties have exclusive rewards and like the amount of Neopoints earned per battle increases the harder the difficulty. There is a common assumption that the smaler the prize pool, the greater chance you will receive the arena rewards (a reason why Dome of the Deep is largely recommended).


▸ Why can't I see the battle log? How do I fix that?
If you have an ad-blocker, you might have to disable that to see your Battle Log again.


▸ How does Freezing status work?
If you successfully freeze your opponent, they won't be able to use any of their weapons or abilities on the next turn. This is most useful when you want to unleash everything you've got with nothing to stop you!


▸ How did Stealing weapons work?
When Stealing Weapons were functional, you used to be able to take your opponent's most top-left equipped item, leaving your opponent unable to use that equipment for the rest of the battle. The stolen item would later be returned to your opponent when the fight was over.

This was most useful when testing Single Use and Fragile weapons, using Chia/Kacheek Flour to easily morph pets, etc. Stealers were disabled from Battledome plots (and all were given a limit of one stealing weapon per set), because long ago someone did find out you could take down a final boss of a certain plot by taking all their weapons! It was an exciting time. ;D

In the new Battledome, Stealers are bugged and do not work anymore. Heavy Robe of Thievery, Rainbow Sticky Hand, and Purple Sticky Hand were the most commonly used Stealing equipment.


▸ Is Punchbag Sid still active?
Nope, although there has been discussion of his return from the Editorial.

Neopets Editorial - Issue 710 | Question 4 [link]

Is there any chance that Punchbag Sid can put in an appearance? TNT, the old team, used to have him show up every year or so. Would be nice to be able to get that rare avatar on this account... Sends the Neopian staff bags of popcorn... to eat or to string for Christmas decorations ~ platdragon

Yay! *starts to string along popcorn for decoration, gets bored and eats the popcorn instead* Hmm, we haven't been in touch with old Sid in a long time. He's not too good at returning phone calls, ya see, with the being a punchbag and all. Maybe the new year will inspire him to come out of hiding.


▸ What is broken with the Battledome?
A lot of things are broken, unfortunately (Defenders of Neopia, Stealing, Lens Flare/Throw Pillow spam from 1P opponents, High Score Table, etc.). A compiled list and their explanations can be found here:

Everything wrong with the Battledome
/~Samuelosaurus
/~_mariokart_


▸ Is there a way how to reset your Battle Record?
Nope, it's all permanent.


▸ What are Featured Challenges?
It's a Battledome feature that was never implemented.


▸ Where can I get advice or other information that wasn't mentioned here?
I'd check out the Battledome NeoBoard Chat to ask around!


▸ Is there anything else I need to know about the Battledome?
Battledome is pretty much stale in terms of TNT producing new/fixed content, but there's still a group of players that still believe that one day TNT will bring back the old features like HP Increase, Battle Stances, old Battle Records, etc.

Neopets Editorial - Issue 855 | Question 7 [link]

Battledome Results:

After nearly a year of delay, the survey results are finally in! We apologise for the lag on our part, our attention has been dragged into a million and one directions in this past year. We want to improve the site in so many ways. And there are so many things to do here in Neopia as you all know and different users have different tastes and interests so we attempt to reach in all directions for change but sometimes we bite off a little too much. So finally we are ready to tackle the fixes that are Battledome. So with that let's get into a brief summary of the results. We had about 10,000 or so users participate last January! We were overwhelmed with great feedback and results that will help us move into the stages of fixes we hope to begin very soon. Scrappy is away at our other HQ for the week, so the second she gets back we hope to dive in head first. So let's just jump into it.

-68% of you have been playing for 11-19 years! Which is insanely awesome!

-50% of you play 21 plus times a week.

-A lot of you want us to focus on fixing the foresight glitch which we also really want to find a solution to.

-In terms of stances 17% of you thought they were super important while 30% were neutral.

-Featured Challengers received 19% neutral yet 26% found it super important.

-Regarding stealing and reflecting 22% thought it was important while 27.6% were neutral and 11% said no altogether.

-Most answers involving high score table & battling difficult opponents were neutral.

-A big percentage voted toward implementing some sort of hit point system as a fourth option in battling.

-73% of you REALLY want to bring back Defenders of Neopia!

In conclusion,

We hear you loud and clear battledomers! We are working with our lead programmer and QA team to hopefully get to the root of each and every issue to bring you all a better dome experience. Just note each fix is an individual issue. No issue can be fixed with one amazing magical blanket…as much as we wish it could. I'd pay millions for that blanket! But anyways just know we will do our best to find a way to the core of the Battledome code to find the best solutions feasible. Thank you for your year long waits of patience and we hope to report some changes soon

Stat Training Related

▸ Where do I train my Neopets? Which place is the best to train my Neopets?
You can train your pets over at these places:
- Cap'n Threelegs' Swashbuckling Academy (Uses One, Two, and Five Dubloons and Trains Up To Level 40)
- Mystery Island Training School (Uses Tan Codestones and Trains Up To Level 250)
- Secret Ninja Training School (Uses Red Codestones and Trains Level 250 and above)

If you want to know which place is the best to train, then that's a matter of how much you're willing to spend. You would want to max out your stats over at the Swashbuckling Academy (Level 40 with 80 HP/STR/DEF), then hit up the Mystery Island Training School unless you don't mind paying more for Codestones and want to train faster (also actually consistent with checking in with every completed course).

JN's Training Guide For Beginners
battlepedia.jellyneo.net/?go=beginners_guide_to_training
It's a Battledome feature that was never implemented.


▸ How do stats work?
It's based on certain "tier ranges" with a given multiplier of icons used for that range. You can check them out here:

TDN's Stat Boost Tiers Guide
thedailyneopets.com/battledome/strength-defense-boosts/


▸ Do I need Speed and Intelligence?
No, because Speed and Intelligence are useless for nearly every weapon out there. Intelligence is really only practical if you want to use Crisp Blue Tunic or Heavy Blue Tunic.


▸ Where do I obtain Codestones and Dubloons?
You can obtain Codestones and Dubloons from dailies, Random Events, etc. Buying from usershops would be the most consistent and reliable way.

Don't visit the Mystery Island Volcano or open Green Gift Pouches/Pouch of Dubloons for Codestones/Dubloons. It'll most likely be a loss compared to buying from usershops.


▸ Where can I break down bigger Dubloons? This guy doesn't give change.
You can break down Dubloons at the Golden Dubloon (~SparklesRoyal) or the Little Nippers Petpet Shop. If you wish to combine your dubloon for a higher denomination, then I'd visit the Dubloon-O-Matic. The Dubloon-O-Matic only takes in full amounts and do not give change.


▸ At what point is it cheaper to Level Rush towards Secret Ninja Training School?
You should be level rushing when you hit 4-5 Tan Codestones (Level 81-100 or Level 101-120).


▸ Should I lab my pets for stats?
That depends on where your stats are at currently and also personal preference.

The Lab Ray will greatly dimish your Level and Defense, but will make your HP skyrocket (as it will never decrease your HP). If you have already maxed out your STR/DEF and only want HP, then I'd give it a go.

The Lab Ray will occasionally change your pet's species and color, so if you are attached to either (or if you're using a species weapon), then don't use the Lab Ray unless you don't mind the cost of changing it back.


▸ I heard there's free training on certain days. When are those days?
You are able to get free training at the Swashbuckling Academy if it's your pet's Species Day, your pet's birthday if you're a Premium Member, and on Neopets's Birthday (November 15th).


▸ Are the stat boosters any good? Which ones are the best?
Some are pretty good while most are pretty terrible. All are pretty pricey, but if you have the NP and/or the cost of regular training is too high, then WHY NOT GIVE IT A GO!

STAT
Considerably Best Stat Boosters
LEVEL
Elixir of Levelling / Irritable Genie-in-a-Bottle
HP
Purple Spotted Shroom / Snegg
STR
Bubbling Fungus
DEF
Armoured Negg / Mano Root Elixir
SPEED
Lag-B-Gone Serum
INT
Reading Books To Your Pet

NOTE: This Q&A did not mention the usage of Fortune Cookies as those are Neocash.


▸ Are Fortune Cookies any good for stat training?
They are definitely good for stat training! Faerie Quest, Lab Ray, and Training cookies are pretty beneficial, but do know that they are Neocash if you're willing to buy Neocash or NC trade for them. I personally don't use Training Cookies, because I'm forgetful and inconsistent when picking up my pets from training.


▸ Is it ideal to train more than one pet?
Not really, unless that other pet is for Pet Trading or 2-Player purposes.


▸ What are there activies and items that can raise and/or lower my stats?
Aside from INT, here's a quick list of places that can raise and/or lower your stats:
- Mystery Island Training School
- Secret Ninja Training School
- Cap'n Threelegs' Swashbuckling Academy
- Kitchen Quests
- The Secret Lab Ray
- Faerie Quests
- Aboard the Coincidence
- Coltzan's Shrine
- Deadly Dice
- Fruit Machine
- Redeeming Space/Underwater Treasure Maps
- Wheel of Extravagance
- Winning certain Deserted Fairground and Terror Mountain Kiosk Scratchcards
- Stat changing items
- Random Events

The best way to decrease a stat varies:
- LEVEL (Deadly Dice, but it's a 50/50 to increase/decrease)
- HP (Vortex Negg, but it can increase/decrease 1 HP, change your pet's color into a Basic color, or give a disease)
- STR (Bullseye Potion, but it's also a chance to increase/decrease)
- DEF (Lab Ray... there are no items that can decrease Defense)
- SPEED (Mummified Scroll, Scroll of Hunger, and Scroll of the Warrior)
- INT (Glamour Negg, Staring Negg, and Scroll Potion)

JN's Stat Increasers Guide
battlepedia.jellyneo.net/?go=stat_increasers

JN's Random Events Guide
jellyneo.net/?go=random_events


▸ What does HSD mean?
HSD (Health/Strength/Defense) is a term that is used for Pet Trading. To calculate HSD, you just add those three stats up together. If your STR/DEF reaches above 750, then the stats are considered at 750 each as that is the maximum stat boost for STR/DEF.

Examples:
3 HP + 5 STR + 2 DEF = 10 HSD
750 HP + 750 STR + 750 DEF = 2,250 HSD
750 HP + 1,000 STR (750) + 750 DEF = 2,250 HSD
750 HP + 1,000 STR (750) + 1,000 DEF (750) = 2,250 HSD


▸ Is there anything else I need to know about Stat Training?
Stat training is all about patience! You can surely train faster if you used stat boosters, but those are pretty costly and the training journey might make the effort feel more rewarding at the end.

The Obelisk Related

▸ What is the Battleground Of The Obelisk?
The Battleground of the Obelisk is a fortnightly series of skirmish battles which award boons and avatars to users who joined the winning team. This part of the site started right after the events of the War for the Obelisk.


▸ Is participating in the Obelisk worth it? Tell me more about these boons. Are they any good?
Yes, you can win 6 avatars, and the boons available include extra bank interest, cheaper stocks and a map through the faerie caverns. You can find more about all of the boon available at Jellyneo.

Jellyneo's Battleground Of The Obelisk Coverage
jellyneo.net/?go=battleground_of_the_obelisk


▸ Where and how do I start participate in the Obelisk? I can't join for some reason.
You can join right at the Battleground of the Obelisk when the time comes. You will be given three different factions to choose from for the round. It's a simple two-click process, but if you do not see the option to join after the first click then I would suggest resetting your screen resolution (aka zoom to 100%).

You can also try on a mobile device if the problem persists.


▸ Do my pets need to be strong to get the boons?
No, the weakest opponents are beatable by anyone. As long as you play 10 total battles (win, lose, or draw), you'll be eligible for a boon if your faction has won that round.


▸ Do you know which side will win?
There is no formally assured way how to determine which side will win although there are some indicators that might lean towards a certain faction of the round.

- 'Who are you joining?' NeoBoard threads in Site Events Chat, Avatar Chat, Battledome Chat, Games Chat, Newbies Chat, and Charter Chat (Premium Only).
- Checking out what Battledome Guilds might be going with (although most Battedome Guilds prefer to keep their faction choice private from the public).
- Are we currently in a Site Event where the boons might be of great use (Faerie Quest Event, a BD Plot, etc.)?
- Does that faction have the best boons out of the rest?
- oxbridge_united's Predicting the winner of the Battleground of the Obelisk
/~oxbridge786


▸ When does X faction come up? I haven't seen them in ages!
Which teams are available is completely random, except that the team that won last time will not re-appear in the next round.


▸ Why didn't I get a trophy and/or any points for the Mysterious Obelisk - Prize Shop?
The trophies and points for the Mysterious Obelisk - Prize Shop were from the War for the Obelisk event. They are retired along with Tyrannia: Mysterious Obelisk Site Theme and the Obelisk War Veteran avatar.


▸ Is there anything else I need to know about the Obelisk?
Guilds, Petpage Predictions, and NeoBoard Predictions might not always choose the winning faction. There is no guarantee on which side will win, but it doesn't hurt to get your ten battles in no matter what happens.

2P Battling Related

▸ What is 2P Battling?
2-Player Battling is when you're battling against another Neopets player. There aren't any prizes for 2P Battling, but it's an experience worth trying out.


▸ Is 2P Battling still a thing?
Kinda, but it's not as big as it used to be. You'll still see a couple of 2P Leagues and Guilds threads over at the Battledome NeoBoard Chat. Some 2P battlers would be glad to help introduce you to the whole 2P scene!


▸ Is there any incentive for 2P Battling?
You won't win any Neopoints or items by battling in 2P leagues, but you may win a user-created trophy, or you may earn a spot on a user-run leaderboard.


▸ What are 2P Leagues?
2P Leagues are 2-Player Battles with extra rules and restrictions in order to make battles fairer and more fun. Most rules involve setting limits on a pet's stats and restrictions on usable equipment. You can find a whole listing of 2P related petpages here:

Two Player Battledome Directory
/~BD2P


▸ Where can I find players to 2P fight?
You can find 2P fights over at the Battledome NeoBoard Chat or in a Battledome Guild.


▸ What is this Foresight Glitch I'm hearing about?
It's a glitch that allows you or your opponent to know what the other side's equipment and ability used next round will be. Most 2P Battlers are aware of this bug and greatly despise it as it ruins the spirit of the battle. A better explanation (but not instructions) about this issue can be read here:

Everything wrong with the Battledome
/~Samuelosaurus#foresight


▸ Is there anything else I need to know about 2P Battling?
2P Battling isn't just about fighting others in leagues. You used to be able to fight a Darigan Tonu for an avatar, but now you just need to own a Darigan Tonu and fight with it. You can also use Scroll Potion to drain your friend's INT, if you really want to do that.

Special thanks and FAQ contributions here from oxbridge_united (Obelisk) and macosten (Everything).

Customisation FAQs

Customisation Basics Related

▸ What is Customization?
Neopets Customization is one of the main creative aspects on the site! Neopians customize their pets to give them character, make them unique and out of the ordinary compared to the other pets, and sometimes just having a bare pet feels kinda empty. There are 55 different species, over 110 colors, and more than 16,500 wearables to explore!


▸ Is Customization worth it? Is there a right way to customize?
Customization is really just for fun! There is no proper way to customize. You can impress your friends, participate in customization related contests, and express your own creativity! Customization is not a necessity to enjoy or play Neopets, but it's something to try out!


▸ How do I customize my Neopets?
You'll first want to obtain some clothing, or Wearables (these are highlighted in blue in your Inventory and also by a hanger icon in the corner of its image), and put them in your Closet. Wearables can be obtained from some Neopian Shops, Usershops, Paint Brushes, etc.

To customize your Neopets, you would want to go to your Quick Reference (this page can be found by clicking your pet's name in the left sidebar) and click "Customise" under the desired pet's dropdown. In the customization application, all you gotta do is select the desired wearables and apply them on your pet, then save afterwards.

If you want to go into your Active Pet's customization application immediately, you could:
- Click on the "Customise" link under your pet's image in the left sidebar.
- Click on the "Customise" button in the upper toolbar.
- Click on the "Customise Neopet" link inside the upper toolbar under "Customise".


▸ Is there a way I can preview certain wearables items before obtaining them?
You can preview wearables and plan future customizations over at any of the following certified fansites:
Dress to Impress (DTI)
impress.openneo.net

Jellyneo's Wardrobe (JN)
wardrobe.jellyneo.net/app/

Sunnyneo's Wearable HQ (SN)
sunnyneo.com/customisation/wearables/


▸ Do I need to convert my Unconverted (UC) Pet in order to customize?
Nope! You will have restrictions on what wearables your Unconverted Pets can wear, but you are not required to convert your pets to customize them!


▸ What are restricted colors?
Restricted colors are uniquely colored species that are unable to wear all the wearables due to the shape or form compared to the normal-body counterparts. The main three are Baby, Maraquan, and Mutant. All the colors include:
- 8-bit (8-bit Chia, Draik, Elephante, Kyrii, and Ruki are fully customizable)
- Baby
- Invisble (Invisble Blumaroo, Elephante, Gelert, Jetsam, Kau, Kougra, Tonu, and Usul are fully customizable)
- Maraquan (Maraquan Mynci is fully customizable)
- Mutant
- Origami (Origami Eyrie, Kacheek, and Moehog are fully customizable)
- Fruit/Vegetable Chias


▸ What are Presets?
Presets are a feature in the Customization application that allows you to save your pet's customization. When you save your pet's customization with presets, the wearables will be occupied in the save file even when they are not in use. Presets are individually linked to the pet that was being customized on, and they reset if the pet is painted/morphed/transferred/abandoned.


▸ What is a Cross-Paint?
A cross-paint is when your pet is wearing Paint Brush clothing that's not the same color of the pet, so you can pull off some pretty awesome customization combos.


▸ Can I layer multiple wearables within the same category?
Generally, you are unable to layer multiple wearables within the same occupation. There are a couple of cases where you would be able to do that though (it's Markings mostly).


▸ Is there a way I can remove a certain part of my pet's features (Ruff, Spiked Toenails, etc.)?
Yep, there is a way to get rid of those extra features! We call these Wearable Restrictions and they are useful when removing certain pet features that might get in the way of our customization idea.

To check out which wearables restrict a certain feature, I'd check out DTI's and JN's Wardrobe Advanced Search.


▸ How do I attach Petpetpets (P3s)? It's taking forever!
To attach Petpetpets to your Active Pet's Petpet, you will need to first obtain the Petpetpet and then refresh your inventory a lot. The Petpetpet attaching is pretty random and it might take a couple hours or longer to do. There are no items nor activities that will boost the chance of attaching the Petpetpet to your Pet's Petpet.


▸ Where do Petpetpets (P3s) even come from?
Petpetpets can be obtained from certain Dailies (Aboard the Coincidence and Grave Danger), Goodie Bags, and directly purchasing from other players through Shop Wizard, Trading Post, and Auctions.

Prior 2014, Petpetpets used to be rewarded from Random Events, and were also available to purchase from the Almost Abandoned Attic. Vernax is the cheapest Petpetpet for that was given out in 2009's Games Master Challenge.


▸ How do I remove my Petpetpet (P3s) from my Pet's Petpet?
You can remove a Petpetpet from your Pet's Petpet, but they will permanently disappear afterward. If you do wish to remove your Petpetpet, then all you have to do is remove your Petpet from your Pet, so think carefully before attaching. Also, if your Petpet is permanently deleted from the Petpet Lab Ray and it did have a Petpetpet, the Petpetpet will also be deleted.


▸ What is Fansite Modeling?
Fansite Modeling is when you are submitting customization data to certified fansites that specialize in previewing wearables such as Dress to Impress and Jellyneo's Wardrobe. It's really just inputting a pet's name that's wearing a new wearable or showing a new colored species, so that everyone can have the chance to play and plan with those customization specialities in the future. DTI and Jellyneo do have a leaderboard of modeling, and Jellyneo's Wardrobe does award their own site trophies for helping out!

Fansite wearable modeling is a vital part of these fansites and those contributions do support the customization community!

Modeling Guide
/~Draconianism


▸ DTI lied to me said that my pet can wear X (or that X wearable looks different on-site)! Why is this?
There are a couple items that might be deceitful on Dress to Impress because of how the occupations are (or something funky going on TNT's end that can be cross-referenced from "Why can't my pet wear X wearable?).

This tends to happen with non-bodily occupying wearables that are for pets with a restricted color (Baby in a Pumpkin, Baby Sleigh with Raindorfs, etc.) and non-bodily occupying wearables with multiple models (Dug up Dirt Foreground, Living in Watermelon Foreground and Background, etc.).

DTI's code doesn't really vibe with that and we discovered that this too was tedious to fix. We'd recommended to check out Jellyneo's Wardrobe for accuracy if you are unsure.


▸ Is there anything else I need to know about customization?
If you ever need advice on how to get started with customization, what wearables might work well with your customization ideas, or something else not mentioned here, then I would try asking the Customization NeoBoard Chat (and also the NC Mall NeoBoard Chat for possibly faster response if customizing with Neocash is okay).

Jellyneo's Customization Articles and Guides

Customisation Errors Related

▸ Why is my pet a cog/gear?
This usually happens when Neopets is lagging pretty hard on their end or some other problem on-site. If the reason is site lag, you could fix this by recustomizing your Neopet by adding or removing a wearable. You could also wait it out until it fixes itself too.

If it happens to be one of the reasons below, those problems cannot be fixed until TNT does something about it:
- It's a 8-bit Wocky (certain image sizes) or Maraquan Wocky (certain image sizes).
- It's an unavailable colored species combination (Grápe Lutari, MSP Hissi, etc.).
- It's wearing a newer wearable (2019-present, fixes itself reasonably quick or when mentioned in the Editorial).


▸ Why can't my pet wear X wearable?
This can be for a variety of reasons!
- You have an item already occupying and/or restricting that wearable zone.
- If the wearable has a shadowed highlight, it means it's currently being worn another pet or in Presets.
- If your pet is a Vandagyre, wearables released prior November 15, 2014 cannot be worn with that species.
- The wearable was designed for a specific species or restricted color (8-bit, Baby, Maraquan, Mutant, Pea, etc.).
- If your pet is a newer restricted color, wearables released prior cannot be worn with that species.
- If the wearable is in the Biology Effects occupation, Unconverted pets cannot wear the item (Static Occupation will make them appear Invisible).
- The wearable is broken (but this only really happens with newer wearables and gets fixed within a week or two unless forgotten or is purposely avoided until hit by the Editorial).
- The wearable is too funky and has been recorded here:

Wearable Woes: Zoning Errors and Glitches
/~Ereza


▸ I just zapped my pet and their wearables are gone! Why is that?
If your pet zapped into a restricted color or different species while wearing clothing that is not compatible with the current colored species, then you are most likely facing an invisible wearable problem. You do still have the items in your Closet as the problem is that you can't remove them regularly as before. You can put the wearables back into your closet by one of these methods:
- Abandoning your pet (and quickly adopting back hopefully)
- Morphing your pet
- Zapping your pet to a compatible color or species
- Sending a Support Ticket


▸ I just transferred my pet and their wearables are gone! Why is that?
The Neopoint wearables and/or Paint Brush clothing are still there, you just have to re-customize your pet. Neocash, No-Trade, and Paint Brush clothing that were not the same color of the pet would all not transfer over.


▸ I didn't get a new set of Paint Brush after morphing my pet. Why is that?
If your pet matches the same color and species of the morphing potion used, you will not receive a new set of Paint Brush clothing if applicable, so might as well use a Turnip Tonic prior to morphing the pet.


▸ I recently did a transfer and it took away the clothing! It wasn't even on, so why did that happen?
Yeah, the Paint Brush clothing of that specified colored species will transfer even if it wasn't used on the pet directly (i.e. on another pet or in your closet). In the event you have multiple sets of the Paint Brush clothing, it will randomly take a set from either location the set resides on.


▸ Sometimes the facial/biological parts of my pet change from-to-time. Do you what's up with that?
Now I call this a dithering model issue (Colored Unis with regular horns, Grey Draks with different Eyes/Mouths, etc.). Some colored species have dithering appearances in which they would often have multiple sets of the same emotion model. This cannot be controlled whatsoever and changes sporadically. TNT have fixed some dithering model issues in the past, but I would assume that this is not their priority anymore.


▸ Is there anything else I need to know about Customization Errors?
Customization errors are really prominent in the Beta application, but most wearable/pet models should fine in the Static preview even if they're not viewable in the Beta application. It doesn't hurt to send in a ticket to try to get a pet and/or item model fixed, but if it's a zone change, then you might want to discuss that on the NeoBoards first for a communal agreement.

Customisation Contest Related

▸ What is the Customization Spotlight?
The Customisation Spotlight is where members can showcase their pets' customizations in hopes of a trophy and personal clout. The contest is divided into two sections being Neopoint items only and Neocash items included.


▸ Is Customization Spotlight rigged?
In a way, yes it is according to their social media 20th Anniversary Q&A:

Q: How are customization spotlight winners chosen?
A: We take your votes & look at the top entries, & we choose what we like based on that. Other times we choose whichever doesn't matter their rank. In essence, there is no method to the madness it's mostly random.


▸ Is there a way how I can view specific Customization Spotlight entries?
There is no way to directly view a specific Customization Spotlight entry. Entries were told to be randomized for everyone per day.


▸ Why can't I enter my pet into Customization Spotlight?
If your pet is not wearing any wearables, was previously Gold Banned prior, or is colored Invisible, it cannot enter in the Customization Spotlight. TNT has said in the past that they'll consider allowing Invisible pets in the future though.

Neopets Editorial - Issue 793 | Question 6 [link]

Hey there, Scrappy! I was wonderin' why Invisible pets are not allowed entry into the Cusomization Spotlight? In my (not so humble) opinion, some of the VERY best customizations are on invisible pets! If it is a bug, would you please whisper in the right someone's ear and get the bug squished? :D Thank you for lookin' into it! Cheers!

Hey! Don't look at me! There is a certain TNTer that has a slight fear of those invisible pets and refuses to include them! We're working on that fear though...


▸ Why does it say another pet submitted the same outfit as mine in the Customization Spotlight?
You probably clicked too fast when entering. Your entries should be fine.


▸ Why are there only two placed winners Customization Spotlight this week?
The owner of the winning pet that week most likely got frozen/suspended. Why doesn't TNT just pick the next top pet, we dunno fam, we just don't know.


▸ What are Gold Bans? Are Gold Bans still a thing in Customization Spotlight?
Gold Bans are when you win first place and you are not allowed to enter that pet for a specified amount of time (just like in the Beauty Contest). They are still a thing in the Customization Spotlight and they last for two months.


▸ Is there anything else I need to know about the Customization Spotlight?
Even though it's clearly rigged, it doesn't hurt to try every now and again if you're wanting the Customization Spotlight trophy. It's more important to be consistent than to not try at all.

Neohomes Related

▸ Do people still make Neohomes? Is it worth it?
Surprisingly, there is a small group of players that still decorate their Neohomes! There is no real benefit or detriment to making a Neohome (well, maybe if you want to get rid of the Newbies sidebar and also get the Robo avatar).


▸ What is the difference between Classic Neohomes and Neohomes 2.0?
Classic Neohome is the original Neohome format. You start out with picking which Neopian land you'd like to be in can then start renovating to your heart's content! Constructing more rooms, gardens, and interior designs do require an extra fee (and wait time), but this version does include the most amount of Neohome items to play around with. You can only unlock the Robo Avatar through the Classic Neohome.

Neohomes 2.0 (or V2) is the newest Neohome format. The navigation is easy to explore and visuals are more appealing. You can choose which Neopian land you would like to create your Neohome in (although choose wisely, as you cannot change locations) and you are given a set amount of both outdoor and living space. While this does mean there is a limited amount of space you can mess around with, this also means there are no additional fees or wait times in terms of renovating your Neohome. Neohomes 2.0 does have fewer Neohome items variety, but as a perk, you can place your Neopets in the homes!


▸ How much do Neohomes cost?
Building a Neohome is free! Expanding and obtaining furniture/gardening supplies are not, so have fun!


▸ How do I make walls?
There are no actual wall furniture items, but the Neohome community has found that Chalkboards and Cylara Posters are affordable and decent substitute for making walls in your Neohome 2.0. Almost everything can be used as a wall in the Classic Neohome.


▸ Do items have to be used just as they are named?
No, items can be used creatively to build all kinds of exciting images, in both versions of Neohomes! Castles, pirate ships, paintings, monsters - the sky isn't even the limit. You can build an outer space image if you want to.


▸ Is there a way I can preview certain Neohome Items?
There is no application to plan a design for your Neohome, but you can preview certain Neohome Items over at Jellyneo's Item Database and also this page:

Secret3191's Museum (Classic Neohome)
/~Korazee


▸ Can I delete my Neohome?
You can delete your Classic Neohome, but you can neither delete nor change the location of your Neohome 2.0.


▸ Are Neohome Spotlight and Notable Neohome still a thing?
Nope x2. They stopped Neohome Spotlight and the Notable Neohome showcases have been there for years.


▸ Why can't I take out my NC Neohome items out of my Storage Shed?
It's a known bug that Neocash Neohome items cannot be removed from the Storage Shed. TNT has not discussed this problem in the Editorial and we assume that this is not a priority fix for them.


▸ What do Neohome Extensions do?
They're nothing, but a flex. You can't show your Neohome Extensions stats off if you have a Neohome 2.0.


▸ Is there a place I can share my Neohome?
You can show off your Classic Neohomes and Neohomes 2.0s over at the Customization NeoBoard Chat!


▸ Is there anything else I need to know about Neohomes?
I'd check out these resources for more information on Neohomes:

jellyneo.net/?go=neohome2 (Neohomes 2.0)

Exploring Neopia FAQs

▸ Why does the Neopia Central Map not load the Movie Central sometimes?
To this day, we don't know why the Movie Central randomly appears and disappears. None of the movie posters will appear, but you can still feed your pets and play the games there if they are available.


▸ What's up with the Keep Out! sign in Krawk Island?
We don't know for sure what its purpose is supposed to be as it is not being used for anything. In terms of lore, there are assumptions that after the events of the Disappearance of Krawk Island, that this is the home of the Krawk Island citizens that did not agree with Governor Gavril McGill's policies.

Timeline of Neopia
/~Chocoladen/


▸ It's been over 8+ years, will Faerieland ever return back to the skies?
Canonically, it does return back to the skies in the future based on the events of the discontinued Legends and Letters game, but for now it it still under repairs.


▸ What's that weird giant island next to Shenkuu?
That is Petpetpet Island from the Journey to the Lost Isle Plot.

JN's Journey to the Lost Isle Plot Recap
bookofages.jellyneo.net/events/journey-to-the-lost-isle/


▸ Is TNT ever bringing back Lutari Island?
It was mentioned in the Editorial that a TNT staff member truly desired to bring back Lutari Island, but stated that they couldn't do the job. In the End of Flash Update video, two TNT staff members stated that bringing back Lutari Island was not entirely impossible to do in the future.


▸ What's the Kreludan Mining Corporation authorisation code?
There is no code anymore. This location was launched in 2004 and was used in the The Lost Desert Plot in 2005.

Altador Mini-Plot Related

▸ Is completing the Altador Mini-Plot worth it?
There are no spectacular item rewards that are given from the Altador Mini-Plot, but completing the activity will reward with the following:
- Royal Astronomer Site Event Trophy
- Lenny - Finneus Avatar
- Altadorian Constellations Site Theme
- 5,000 Neopoints and additional item rewards
- Access to the King Altador daily (he gives away a free Altador themed item or Neopoints once per day)


▸ Alright, where can I find a guide to complete the Altador Mini-Plot then?
Here are a couple guides that can help you complete the Altador Mini-Plot:
jellyneo.net/content/plot/index.php
thedailyneopets.com/altador-plot/index
sunnyneo.com/plots/altador/


▸ Does the Altador Mini-Plot work with the new HTML5 map?
The Altador Mini-Plot does in fact work with the new map! If for whatever reason the map does not work for you, then here are the following links to the unmarked areas on the main map:
- The Old Follies Farm
- The Restive Tomb
- Perfectly Flat Rock Quarry
- Altador Water Distribution Plant
- The Colosseum
- The Altadorian Docks
- The Clouds


▸ Can I participate in the Altador Mini-Plot on my side account?
You are NOT allowed to participate in the Altador Mini-Plot on your side accounts.


▸ Do I really need to click every submit and leave button?
Yes, you really do need to click every submit and leave button in order to progress through the Mini-Plot.


▸ How do you find constellations? Is it the same for everyone?
They are not the same for everyone and you can find your constellation locations from the following resources below:
jellyneo.net/content/plot/index.php?id=constellation_finder
thedailyneopets.com/altador-plot/constellation-finder/
sunnyneo.com/plots/altador/starmapper/starmap.php


▸ How do you heal the Vaeolus? I've been at this for three hours.
Aside from finding your constellations, the Vaeolus activity has to be one of most complicated roadblocks in the Altador Mini-Plot. You are going to have to be consistent with the timing for every minute per action (Bandage, Feed, Medicine, or Wait), then you would immediately check up on the petpet. For example:

12:01:00 → Action
12:02:02 → Check Up
12:02:05 → Action

I would say TDN has the best walkthrough for this activity.

TDN's Vaeolus Guide
thedailyneopets.com/altador-plot/vaeolus/


▸ How do fix the Water Plant? I've been at this for four hours.
The Water Plant's configurations are random for everyone, but TDN and SunnyNeo both have individual guides on how to tackle the 254 possible combinations. There is one combination that you should avoid (don't worry if you hit do it though), and that is turning on all the wheels and levers as that will flood Altador.

TDN and SN's Water Plant Guides
thedailyneopets.com/altador-plot/waterplant/
sunnyneo.com/plots/altador/waterplant.php


▸ How do you configure the gears in the Hall Basement?
The gear positions are random for everyone, but TDN's guide has a strategy on how to solve this:

TDN's Gears Guide
thedailyneopets.com/altador-plot/gears/


▸ How do I find my spellbook location?
Your spellbook location is based off your Sleeper constellation coordinates. I would reference to the following guides for the process:

TDN and SN's Spellbook Finder
thedailyneopets.com/altador-plot/spellbook-finder/

▸ Is there anything else I need to know about the Altador Mini-Plot?
If you ever get lost or in need of clarification with any of the steps, then feel free to head over to the Avatars/NeoSignatures NeoBoard Chat, Games NeoBoard Chat, or Help NeoBoard Chat for assistance. The Altador Mini-Plot can be difficult at times, but it is a fun activity to do on the site!

Atlas of the Ancients Related

▸ Is the Atlas of the Ancients plot still active?
Nah fam, it started and ended in 2009 (Y11). However, you can still get free items from it.


▸ Is collecting all the Moltara Worms worth it? 
If you want the experience and the glory of being able to say you've done it, sure. Otherwise, it can be a pretty significant time investment to wait for all the worms to show up, especially the black and rainbow ones which are known to be particularly elusive, only showing up for a specified 5 minute time interval at a time each day. The times and total amount of worm appearences are different for everyone, so you might want to record the times you find them!


▸ Is it worth the time creating all the petpets at Tangor's Workshop?
 Again, if you want to do it for the experience, go ahead. Ain't nobody stoppin' ya. But honestly it's much more efficient time-wise to just buy them from other users.

Jellyneo's Tangor's Workshop Guide
jellyneo.net/?go=tangorsworkshop


▸ So, where do I get Scrap Metal and Stone and Red Moltite? 
Scrap Metal and Stone used to be available via a random event while in Moltara, but that event seems to have gone MIA. Red Moltite can be found organically by gathering up all ten worms and exploring the Dark Cave. Both can be found in user shops if you really want to craft the petpets yourself, or if you need them for some other reason.


▸ I was feeling nostalgic and got a free item from the Atlas of the Ancients comic! Are there any related freebies left for me to grab? 
Freebies from the comic include Ancient Map of Neopia, Wind Up Pocket Watch, Shiny Mechanical Faerie Fountain, Mysterious Orchid, Steam Horn, and Mechanical Molla Flower. See Jellyneo's guide for specific instructions on how to obtain them. You can also visit the Obsidian Quarry daily for a free Shiny Obsidian.

Jellyneo's Atlas of the Ancients Plot Coverage
jellyneo.net/?go=atlas_of_the_ancients
