▸ What is and how do I acess the Magma Pool?
Guarded by a Magma Tonu, the Magma Pool is a place where you can dip your Neopets into the lava rock color, Magma. There exists two methods of getting Magma Pool access:

- The first method is to visit the Magma Pool Guard when he is asleep. He takes a ten minute nap at the same time every day (it's a different time for everyone). You are allowed to do this method on your side accounts, however do know that you are only permitted to dip your pets once per week.
- The other method is when the Magma Pool Guard deems you worthy to dip in the Magma Pool. This method grants you permanent access and allows you to visit the Magma Pool at any time. It is not entirely known, but we were informed that it requires obtaining NP/NP items, so that one is not allowed to be done on side accounts.

On-Site Related Links
- /~Kuamik (ZYDP - Free Magma Customs)
- Neopets Editorial - Issue 489 | Question 2 [link] (Acknowledgement of the second method)
- Neopets Editorial - Issue 433 | Question 11 [link] (First method is fine to do on sides, but the second is NOT permitted on sides)

JN's Magma Pool Article and Time Checklist
jellyneo.net/?go=magma_pool
jellyneo.net/?go=magma_pool_checklist


▸ Could you tell me more about Permanent Magma Pool Access?
The process is not entirely known right now, but you can find the most recent efforts in the link below:

Permanent Access To The Magma Pool Findings
/~Piercau


▸ Is there anything else I need to know about the Atlas of the Ancients? 
AotA is generally regarded as the worst plot by most players, being little more than a point-and-click exercise combined with a Daily Dare-esque element (achieve x score in y game to receive z prize). It had a Neocash component as well, something that wasn't looked kindly upon at the time. This plot spawned the knockoff games Clara on Ice (Let It Slide), Tunnel Tumble (Darigan Dodgeball), Moltara Run (Volcano Run II), Clockwork Codebreaker (untimed Time Tunnel), as well as the new games Cloud Raider and Cave Glider.

Most importantly, it led to a new land and pet color - Moltara and magma, respectively - being revealed, which was pretty cool.

Special thanks and FAQ contributions here from yzhen_121993 (AotA).

Guilds / Questing FAQs

Guild Basics Related

▸ Where are the guilds and what are they?
Guilds are special interest clubs that you can create/join to meet other players with similar likes and dislikes. You can find new friends and chat about your favorite things. To get to the Guilds page, click on 'Shops' in the yellow toolbar. When the shops page loads, click on the 'Guilds' link in the toolbar.


▸ What is the purpose of guilds?
Guilds are just special interest clubs that anyone can join. There is no real advantage or disadvantage if you decide not to join a guild. You can find new friends with the same interests as you (e.g Skating, Chias, Drawing), and you can normally find a lot of people to practice within the Battledome.


▸ How do I create a guild?
To start your own guild go to the Guilds page and press Create a New. To get to the Guilds page, click on 'Shops' in the yellow toolbar. When the shops page loads, click on the 'Guilds' link in the toolbar. (It is a blue/green castle). Remember you can only create or join one guild so choose wisely.


▸ How do I join a guild?
When you have found the guild you want to join, go to the guild page. You should see a 'Join Guild' link under the 'Options' header along the left. Click that link and you will become a member of that guild.


▸ How do I get to my guild?
To get to your guild, click on 'Shops' then click on the 'Guilds' link. Once the Guild main page loads, click on the 'Teleport' link in the toolbar. This will take you directly to your guild.
NOTE: You have to be a member of a guild for this to work!


▸ How do I leave a guild?
If you don't want to be part of a guild anymore, it is very easy to leave. Just go to the main Guilds Page and enter the guild you belong to. At the very bottom of the options (in the sidebar of the guild) is a 'leave guild' button. Once you click that you are no longer a part of that guild.

If you are the Guild Leader, you will not have the option of leaving. You would have to actually delete the guild. We will be working on a feature that will allow the Guild Leader to resign and appoint someone else into their place.


▸ How do I delete a guild?
If you have accidentally created a guild you can delete it but first you need to remove all your members. To do this go back to your guild page and click on Guild Members. This will display a list of all the members. To remove someone click on their UN and then select delete member. You need to do this for all your members and then the delete guild option will appear.

You are not allowed to delete a guild that has multiple members, so the members must leave or be removed before you will have the option of deleting the guild.


▸ Can I change the location of my guild?
Unfortunately, once you have created a guild you cannot change its location or neighbourhood.


▸ What are private guilds?
Private guilds are guilds that are not listed in the Guild neighbourhoods. The only way to become a member of a private guild is if you receive an official Guild Invitation and you click on the link provided to you.


▸ What options do I have when I create a guild?
When you are creating your new guild, you have quite a few options to choose from.

- Guild Neighbourhood
There are many neighbourhoods that you can choose from, and each neighbourhood has a unique theme. Try to choose a neighbourhood that will best suit your guild's theme.

- Guild Description
This will be the text along the top of your guild. The description is placed along the top of your guild as a brief intro to what your guild is about. The description is also used when searching for guilds, so make sure that it is something catchy.

- Guild Welcome
This is the welcome message that is displayed when a user goes to your guild's front page. Use this area to update members to new events, news, etc.

- Guild Privacy
You have the option of making your guild public or private. If you choose to make your guild private, then it will not show up when users are searching the the guild neighbourhoods. You will have to invite members directly in order for them to get to your guild.

- Guild Colours
You can customise all of the colours used for your guild layout. This includes the text and border colours. Try creating a colour scheme using the drop down boxes and then click on Preview. This will open a new window showing you how your colour scheme would look. If you don't like the colour scheme, simply try changing the colours and clicking on Preview until you are happy with the colour scheme.


▸ How do I change the appearance of my guild?
Once you have created your own guild, you can change its appearance whenever you wish. This includes the colour scheme, welcome message and guild logo. To change the welcome message (the main page people see when they come to your guild) first go to your guild. At the bottom of the sidebar is a section called 'Admin'. Click on 'Guild Layout'. You now have three options. The first will change your guild appearance. The second will let you change the names of the positions in your guild. The last one will let you upload/change your logo.

Click on 'Modify Guild Preferences'. Now you can enter a new description and welcome message. You can also choose to make your guild private or not. If you choose to make your guild private, it can only be seen by invited players and won't appear in the guild search. You can also change the colour scheme by selecting different colours from the drop down menus.

Once you have finished making your changes, click on the 'Submit Changes' button. Your changes should now be saved. You many need to refresh the page to see the changes.


▸ How do I promote/demote guild members?
To promote or demote a guild member, click on the 'Guild Members' link under the 'Admin' header. That will pull up a list of all of the members in the guild. To choose a member, simply click on their name. That will pull up an options page which will allow you to modify their current rank and status. Using the drop down menu, select the rank that wish to give them and then click on 'Update Member'!


▸ Can I suspend a member from my guild?
Yes. To suspend a member, click on the 'Guild Members' link under the 'Admin' header. That will pull up a list of all of the members in the guild. To choose a member, simply click on their name. That will pull up an options page which will allow you to modify their current rank and status. To suspend them, simply place a check in the 'Suspend Member' option and click on 'Update Member'! The member will be placed on suspension, which will stop them using the message board, calendar and photo gallery sections. To remove the suspension, simply follow the same steps again and choose 'Reinstate Member.


▸ Can I remove a member from the guild?
Yes. To delete a member, click on the 'Guild Members' link under the 'Admin' header. That will pull up a list of all of the members in the guild. To choose a member, simply click on their name. That will pull up an options page which will allow you to modify their current rank and status. To delete the member, simply place a check in the 'Delete Member' option and click on 'Update Member'! The member will then be removed from the guild. Please make sure that this action is a last resort, since this cannot be undone.


▸ Can I block a user from rejoining a guild?
Yes. To block a user, click on the Guild Members link under the 'Admin' header. That will pull up a list of all of the members in the guild. To choose a member, simply click on their name. That will pull up an options page which will allow you to modify their current rank and status. To block the member, simply place a check in the Block User option and click on Update Member! The member will then be removed from the guild and they will be prohibited from rejoining.


▸ What is a the guild council?
The guild council, is a list of a few trusted people who are given certain duties to maintain the guild. What these duties are, depends on what the guild leader wants them to do. Each council member can have certain permissions such as the ability to clear message boards, although this is up to the guild leader to give them out.

There are four positions other than the guild leader, the names are up to the guild leader to create. The guild leader is the founder of the guild. He or she always has the final say on how the guild will operate.


▸ How do I apply for a position on the council?
The guild leader can promote members to an open position on the guild council or guild members can place an application for an open guild position by clicking on the 'Apply For Position' link under the Guild Council header. The guild leader can then review the application and accept or reject it accordingly. If you do not see a link to apply for a position, then there are no available council positions at that time.


▸ Who has guild admin capabilities?
By default, only the guild leader (founder) and the person appointed by the guild leader as the guild master will have admin capabilities. Although, the guild founder can also assign (and remove) admin privileges to any member he/she deems fit. The admin powers are organised as follows:

- Layout Control
The ability to change the guild description, welcome message, guild logo and many other layout attributes such as the guild colours and guild hierarchy. This is a very powerful position and should only be appointed to those that you trust completely.

- Member Admin
The ability to change a member's rank and other member status values. This is also a very powerful position, as a person with this admin power can also suspend, delete and permanently block a user from the guild!

- Council Admin
The ability to monitor all of the applications sent in for guild council positions. This power allows the member to accept and reject any applications that have been submitted.

- Board Monitor
The ability to monitor the guild message boards. This admin power allows the user to delete messages from the board, as well as, utilize the admin features for the message boards (multiple deletes).

- Calendar Admin
The ability to monitor the guild calendar events. This admin power allows the user to delete any events from the guild calendar.


▸ How can I customise the guild council position names?
To customize your guild layout, click on the 'Guild Layout' link under the 'Admin' header. From there, you can click on Modify Guild Preferences. This page will allow you to modify the description, welcome message, privacy status and all of the colour choices for your guild. Once you have made all of the desired modifications, simply click on 'Submit Changes.


▸ How do I review applications for the guild council?
To review applications submitted by guild members for council positions, simply click on the 'Guild Council' link under the 'Admin' header. If there are any new applications, they will be listed on this page. To review a specific application, simply click on the member's name that you wish to review. This will pull up the application submitted, which includes their current position in the guild, and the position they are applying for. If you wish to accept their application, simply click on 'Accept' and they will be promoted to their new council position. If you click 'Reject', then it will remove their application and they will not be promoted.


▸ Messages keep disapeering from my guild, yet I am not deleting them, why is this?
If a person posts a particularly bad message, we will send them an official warning and delete all the messages that person has posted, this includes guilds and noticeboard posts.

Also we periodically clear old messages from guild boards. We have to do this now and again to make sure they don't get overloaded.


▸ Why can't we have chats in our shops or guilds?
Unmonitored, live chats are against Neopets terms and conditions. We cannot control what is said in them, or ensure our players safety when using them. As there are some very nasty people out there, we cannot permit them to be used.


▸ How do I organise a guild donation?
If you want to do a guild giveaway, you simply need to decide on a date when as many guild members as possible will be able to help out. Start storing up items and promote your giveaway on the messageboards and noticeboards. When it comes to the big day, just start giving away those items in the Money Tree and grateful Neopians will flock to see what is on offer. While you are doing the giveaway, keep reminding people via the Guild board.


▸ How do I invite members to my guild?
If your guild is private, or if you want to directly invite a member, you can do so by entering the prospective member's UN on the Guild Invite page. This will send the user a Neomail with a link to your guild.

NOTE: The guild invite link will need to be copied and pasted into the invited user's browser. The direct link in the Neomail will give an error.

Under Guild Preferences, there is an option to restrict guild invitations to guild admin only. If this is enabled, members without this privilege will not be able to send guild invites.

Guild invites are only valid for a limited time before they expire and have to be resent. Additionally, only users who have Guild Invites activated in their user preferences can receive an invite.


▸ What is a Guild Mailer and how do I send one to my guild members?
A guild mailer is a message that is sent through Neomail to all members of a guild. You can use this feature to send out guild announcements, updates, or any sort of information to your guild members who have this feature active in their user preferences.

To send a guild mailer, a member needs to have been assigned the admin privilege. If you have this privilege, you'll be able to select "My Guild Members" from the drop-down menu when you create a new Neomail. This will display "@guild_list" in recipient box.

Occasionally, a red message will state that guild mailing is offline. You won't be able to send out a guild message during that time, but make sure to check back at a later time. There is no schedule as to when guild mailing is down.

When guild mailing is ónlíné you may need to refresh the page a couple of times before you see the textbox appear. Remember, this will send a message to all members of your guild who have Guild Mailing activated in their user preferences.


▸ A large amount of messages were deleted from the Guild Stats?
You may notice hundreds--or even thousands--of messages deleted from your Guild's stat count. This is a known occurance. Some guilds choose to list the deleted message count on their website, though, of course, this is only provided as an estimate.

Example:
Guild Stats
Page Views: 104274
Members: 36
Messages: 8186 (~20,000 messages deleted)
Founded: 08/06/2015


▸ What is a "guild account" and is it against the rules?
A guild account is a side account created by a member of a guild--likely a council member--to represent the guild on the boards, open a guild shop or gallery, and more importantly, host extra guild pages. Though, it isn't necessary for a guild to operate a guild account.

If a guild chooses to have a guild account, remember that it is considered a side account and may only be accessed by one person. All rules governing side accounts must be followed by the user operating the guild account.


▸ What is a "guild donation shop" and is it against the rules?
A guild donation shop is just a regular shopfront with a few differences. A guild can utilize a donation shop to acquire NPs from guild members to make purchases on behalf of the guild. An example might be using shop donations in order for the guild account to purchase a Faerie Queen Doll to lend to members.

As of NT Issue 843, guild donation shops are allowed--though it must be operated solely for the benefit of the guild, and not the user hosting the shop. The shop doesn't have to be operated on a guild account, though, many guilds choose that option.

NOTE: A guild may only operate one guild shop. Additionally, it isn't allowed to require or pressure a guild member to make donations. Deciding to donate to the guild shop should be entirely optional.

Neopets Editorial - Issue 843 | Question 1 [link]

The Winds are changing...

So you know that rule where we don't allow tournaments/contests in guilds? Well, let's forget that, shall we? From this point on, guild-based contests and tournaments are permitted.

This of course brings up the question of guild donation shops. These are also allowed with the understanding that ALL donations are given back to their respective guild members and not the person running the shop. The guild donation shop (one per guild, please!) does not have to be on the guild founders account but should be on the Guild Council so it's more official. Requiring donations (?!?) and/or fees to join a contest or tournament are still not allowed. Lastly, the guild shop account should only be accessed by the person who created that account.

Joining different guilds on side accounts is absolutely fine. All we ask is that you only have one account per guild.

Overall, please abide by the spirit of the rules. And if you run a tournament, please see it through!

In the future, we will be working on a tool to make this easily manageable. But we're getting ahead of ourselves ;)


▸ Is my guild allowed to host events and award prizes?
Similar to guild donation shops, the rules regarding guild events and prizes have changed as of NT Issue 843. Guilds are now allowed to host events which award prizes--though only guild members are allowed to receive the prizes, and only on their main accounts.


▸ Is there anything else I need to know about Guilds?
It is completely fine if you do not wish to be in a Guild. Guilds are optional and not necessary to have fun on Neopets.

Quests of Neopia Related

▸ What are Taelia/Snow Faerie Quests? Are they worth it?
Taelia the Snow Faerie is in need of some food items, but due to the harsh weather of Terror Mountain, she will ask you to go fetch the items. In return for helping her, she will award you with an avatar, some moderately low valued items, Neopoints, the ability to fight her in the Battledome, and a chance for an exclusive item themed to her or an Ice Cream Cart coupon.

You can do a total of ten Taelia Quests per day, but do know that Edna and Kitchen Quests are included in the daily ten quests. A failed Taelia Quest does not get counted for your daily ten quests. You cannot start a quest if you have 60+ items in your Inventory.

Most people tend to stop fulfilling her quests once they've received the avatar. Her quests are not really profitable and the chance for an exclusive item is so significantly scarce that it does not make up the cost from continuous questing. If you do happen to receive an Ice Cream Cart coupon, there are a couple of pricey ice cream items to try your luck at.


▸ Does Taelia/Snow Faerie Quests still give out Draik Eggs?
Nope, TNT got rid of that. She also used to give out high rarity Battledome weapons, but that also has been removed from her quests.


▸ What are Brain Tree Quests? Are they worth it?
In the depths of the Haunted Woods, there lies a big spooky nerd tree that will quiz you on the deceased. The Brain Tree will ask you for the answers and you will need to feed the Esophagor twice in order to get those answers. In solving his question, he will award you with an item, Neopoints, and the ability to fight him in the Battledome. There is also a High Score Table for the amount of NP earned and placing in the top 50 for that will reward a different avatar.

You can only do one Brain Tree Quest per day. A failed Brain Tree quest does count for that one quest per day.

Most people do Brain Tree Quests for the avatar and then quit right after, because most of his rewards are pretty terrible. There are two Brain Tree items, Brains a la Tree and Brain Tree Knife, that are worth a quite a bit, but they are extremely rare to get.


▸ What are Esophagor Quests? Are they worth it?
The Esophagor is some sort of monster that's known for his massive appetite and proficiency on Brain Tree trivia. He'll request you for low rarity Spooky Food and in return will reward you with a random item that is r89 or below.

You can do a total of ten Esophagor Quests per day and failing a quest does not count for one of your daily ten quests. Also, completing an Esophagor quest for the Brain Tree answers does not count towards the total, but you wont receive any additional rewards other than the answer for these. You cannot start a quest if you have 60+ items in your Inventory.

Aside from the Brain Tree Quests, you should never do an Esophagor Quest as they will almost always result in a loss of Neopoints. Spooky Food has gotten pretty expensive due to the Brain Tree's High Score Table avatar.


▸ Can't I just guess the answer for the Brain Tree and still get the reward?
Nope! You have to complete two of the Esophagor's quests in order to complete a Brain Tree Quest. If the Esophagor's requested items are too expensive for you, you can fail that quest and do another quest later. A failed Esophagor quest does not count as one your daily 10 Esophagor Quests per day.


▸ Can I check back with the Esophagor if I forgot the answer?
Unfortunately, the Esophagor will not repeat the answers for the Brain Tree's quest even after being fed again. He won't even reward you with his regular rewards until you complete/fail the Brain Tree's quest.

If you happen to forget the answers, SunnyNeo has a compiled list of possible Brain Tree answers here:
sunnyneo.com/braintree.php


▸ How are points rewarded for the Brain Tree High Score Table?
The Brain Tree High Score Table is based off the amount of Neopoints earned from completing his quests. The NP amount earned is completely random and there is nothing you can do to increase it aside from attempting again.


▸ What are Kitchen Quests? Are they worth it?
Some time after the events of the Destruction of Maraqua on August 17th, 2001, the Underwater Chef was washed ashore on Mystery Island and now works for Mumbo Pango as his personal chef. Due to the nature of Mumbo Pango's massive appetite, Underwater Chef needs you help on gathering food items for his fancy dishes. By completing his quests, he will reward you with Neopoints, an item reward, or a stat boost (Level, HP, Strength, Defense, or Speed) to a random pet. The item reward has the chance of being an exclusive Kitchen Quest item.

You can do a total of ten Kitchen Quests per day, but do know that Edna and Taelia Quests are included in the daily ten quests. A failed Kitchen Quest does not get counted for your daily ten quests. You cannot start a quest if you have 60+ items in your Inventory.

You aren't here for the item nor Neopoints rewards, but you are here for the possible stat boosts as they're pretty decent when training one pet. It is not recommended to do Kitchen Quests when you have multiple pets on your main account as the stats rewards are randomly given out to one of your pets. Also, don't do the expensive quests that request items such as Neggs, Bag of Peanuts, etc.


▸ What are Edna Quests? Are they worth it?
Inside the Witch's Tower, there is a spooky Zafara sorceress by the name of Edna and she wants your help on making a new spell. She will request various low rarity items and in return, she will reward you with a small amount of Neopoints (85 - 263 NP), a random low rarity Spooky Food item, and the ability to fight her in the Battledome.

You can do a total of ten Edna Quests per day, but do know that Kitchen and Taelia Quests are included in the daily ten quests. A failed Edna Quest does not get counted for your daily ten quests. You cannot start a quest if you have 60+ items in your Inventory and she is not in the tower during Noon - 1PM NST as she is power napping in that time.

Aside from the avatar, you should never do an Edna Quest as they will almost always result in a loss of Neopoints.


▸ Is the three requested item Edna Avatar theory actually true?
Not exactly, but we have been told that completing a quest with multiple requested items should be done over a quest with fewer items if we wanted the Edna - Cackle! avatar.

Neopets Editorial - Issue 603 | Question 4 [link]

Okay TNT, it's been almost 10 years. 10! And yet, still no one knows how exactly to get the "Edna - Cackle!" avatar. Rumor has it that TNT has said it is not random (I can't seem to find proof of this), so let's hear it. Is the avatar really random? If not, can you please, please, please (See, I'm not above begging!) give us a hint?!? ~lavylovesyoulots

*CACKLE* Well, since it's been "almost 10 years," we suppose we can give you a hint. If you're trying to be thrifty about it, we suggest not bothering to fulfill her requests unless she asks you for a few items.


▸ What are Coincidence quests? Are they worth it?
Orbiting around Neopia, there's a century-year-old Lutari scientist named Dr. Landelbrot maintaining all the Random Events of Neopia, and he needs your help with repairing his Random Event machine. He will ask for some common Daily items (some are restockable) and will reward your efforts by letting you test out the machine. You have the chance of getting Neopoints, stat boosts, TCGs, Petpetpets, and more! You do also have the chance of getting your Neopoints stolen, having your stats decreased, or most commonly, getting nothing at all.

You can do one Coincidence quest per day. A failed Coincidence quest does count for that one quest per day, just do remember to decline the quest to get a new set of requested items the next day as there is no expiration date on the quests.

I would say the Coincidence quests are only worthwhile if you only do the quests that are 10k or less. It is very common to get an event that does nothing and the TCG and Petpetpet events are extremely rare. The stat changes, NP loss/gain, and Lottery ticket events are also rare in a sense.


▸ Are Coincidental Fortune Cookies worth it?
I would personally say that Coincidental Fortune Cookie are not worth the effort to open them. They do guarantee you an extra (rarely two) quests per day but given that the chance of getting a positive event is unusually rare, that makes it feel discouraging to throw real-money at these quests.


▸ What happens if I fail any of the Quests of Neopia above?
Aside from the Brain Tree and Coincidence quests, there are no consequences for failing the Quests of Neopia above. If you fail a Brain Tree or Coincidence quest, you won't be able to receive a quest from them until the next day.


▸ Can I use the Shop Wizard for any of these Quests of Neopia?
You are allowed to use the Shop Wizard for all the Quests of Neopia mentioned above (Taelia, Brain Tree, Esophagor, Kitchen, Edna, and Coincidence Quests).


▸ I heard there was a special prize for doing a Brain Tree, Esophagor, and Edna Quest. Is that true?
For completing a quest each from those guys, you will be rewarded with the book, Tales of the Esophagor.


▸ Is there anything else I need to know about any of these Quests of Neopia?
Most of these are not profitable, but if you've got the NP to drop and want to have some fun, then go for it. Edna's Quests is the only quest that doesn't have a high-end/long-term incentive aside from the avatar.

Faerie Quests Related

▸ What are Faerie Quests?
Not to be mistaken with Snow/Jhudora/Illusen Quests, Faerie Quests are referred to the Faeries that are in need of your help towards rebuilding the fallen ruins that is Faerieland. In return, you will be award Battledome stats (and access to the Rainbow Fountain by the Fountain Faerie) for your service.


▸ Where and how do I get Faerie Quests?
Faerie Quests are given out in Random Events, Faerie Quest Fortune Cookies, and the Faerie Quest Event. Random Events are, well, randomly given out, Faerie Quest Fortune Cookies can be purchased from the NC Mall; and the Faerie Quest Event happens around the springtime.


▸ Where can I find the items for a Faerie Quest?
Usershops, Trading Post, Auctions, Quest Help NeoBoard, etc. You are allowed to use a side account to use the Shop Wizard and buy the item on your main account.


▸ Do I need to complete every Faerie Quest I get?
There are no consequences for declining a Faerie Quest.


▸ Do Fountain Faerie Quests stack?
Fountain Faerie Quests do not stack, so if you happen to have a Fountain Faerie Dip saved up, you might want to use that dip before you complete another Fountain Faerie Quest (or the random Grey Faerie Quest).


▸ Are Kaia/Crafting Faerie Quests worth it?
Well, that is up to you if you like any of the items I would say. Trading wise, people do like new items, but you usually won't see these newer Faerie Quest wearables rise significantly nowadays.

Personally and prior October 8th, 2020, I would say Kaia Quests are not worth it. The items are randomly rewarded and difficult to trade away. If there is an item that you like from her prize pool, I would say it would be easier to find someone willing to trade that item off directly.


▸ How can I avoid getting a Kaia Quest?
Kaia Quests can only be given out if you have any Neocash items (including Basic Gift Boxes) in your inventory. If you do not want her quests, then I'd recommend putting all your NC Items in your Closet, SDB, or Gallery.


▸ Are Faerie Quest Fortune Cookies worth it?
Faerie Quest Fortune Cookies are quite worthwhile if you are training your pets and/or wanting to try your luck at getting a Fountain Faerie Quest. They are not necessary to have for training/or getting a Fountain Faerie Quest, but they are a nice booster for those activities.


▸ I heard Faerie Quest Fortune Cookies are discounted sometimes. If so, when?
Faerie Quest Fortune Cookies do get discounted to 50% off during the Faerie Quest Event. The Faerie Quest Event happens around the springtime.


▸ How does the Faerie Quest Refresh Boon work? How do I get it?
The Faerie Quest Refresh Boon can be obtained from the Battleground Of The Obelisk and Charity Corner. How it works is that when you receive a Faerie Quest, you are allowed to swap it for a different faerie quest (or possibly get the same faerie with the same requested item) once.

You are able to use the boon again for every new Faerie Quest you receive in that boon time. In order to make the most use of the boon, most players would open a Faerie Quest Fortune Cookie to get one Faerie Quest per day.


▸ Is it true that Space Faerie Quests are only available to Premium members?
As of this editorial, that statement is true.

Neopets Editorial - Issue 859 | Question 5 [link]

Hey TNT! Could you clarify something for us? Does the Space Faerie only offer quests to premium users? A number of us were discussing this on the neoboards, since Space Faerie quests seem to be even more rare than FFQs, and the few people who said they got a visit from the Space Faerie were all premium users.~~leo_flores

Good to see our players are as observant as ever. The Space Faerie is pretty pally with the Premium users and prefers to visit them whenever she is in need of an item.


▸ Why can't I complete my Faerie Quest?
If you are unable to complete your Faerie Quest, you either are facing one of the following issues:
- You do not have the item requested.
- Your Active Pet is currently in the Battledome.


▸ Do Faerie Quests expire?
These types of Faerie Quests do not expire although you might want to complete them eventually to regain access to the Shop Wizard.


▸ What is the best time to open Faerie Quest Fortune Cookies?
Midnight NST is the best time to open a Faerie Quest Fortune Cookie as you can have the chance for an extra quest since Faerie Quest Fortune Cookie quests reset at Midnight NST.


▸ Why are the old Crafting Faerie Quest ingredients being sold in the NC Mall?
It's for collectors and the very few members that saved those old Crafting Faerie Quests. As of 2018, they have started to retire the Crafting Faerie Quest materials once the Faerie Quest Event ended for the year.


▸ Is there anything else I need to know about Faerie Quests?
You kinda want to complete them as fast you can since you cannot receive any other of these Faerie Quests until you complete or forfeit the one you've currently got.

There are Faerie Quests that are subjectively not worth doing depending on the item they ask for/type of Faerie it is, in which case, feel free to forfeit their quest:

- Air Faerie Quests are a personal choice, since some people do like seeing their stats grow, but the Movement stat hasn't been significant since 2012.
- Some Faeries such as the Battle Faerie, Faerie Queen, Fountain Faerie, and Space Faerie occasionally request items that cost way more than the value of the rewards received in terms of the actual training cost for the same amount of stats / paint brush or morphing potion cost for the same paint job.

Jhudora / Illusen Questing Related

▸ What is Jhudora / Illusen Questing?
Jhudora and Illusen are in need of various r10-r99 items and want them immediately, because they are impatient. For completing their quests, you are rewarded with fun goodies such as books, food, and strong Battledome weapons.


▸ What is the difference Jhudora and Illusen Questing?
Jhudora's Bluff (formerly Jhudora's Cloud):
- Jhudora lives in Faerieland and will reward you with Dark Faerie themed items for completing her quests.
- Jhudora's quests starts to get more difficult around Level 28+. The items of her first two quests are r10-r25
- Her final reward is Wand of the Dark Faerie.
- She is closed on March 17th (Illusen Day), but she does award an avatar on February 4th (Jhudora Day).

Illusen's Glade:
- Illusen lives in Meridell and will reward you with Earth Faerie themed items for completing her quests.
- Illusen's quests starts to get more difficult around Level 35+. The items of her first two quests are r10-r20.
- Her final reward is Illusens Staff.
- She is closed on February 4th (Jhudora Day), but she does award an avatar on March 17th (Illusen Day).


▸ Is Jhudora / Illusen Questing difficult?
These quests start off easy with requests of cheap lower rarity items. As you progress, the quests get more difficult with higher rarity items (eventually capping at only requesting r99s).


▸ What happens if I am unable to deliever the requested item in time?
If you are unable to complete the quest, your quest level, and score for the High Score Table will be reset. You will have to wait 12 hours to do another quest.


▸ Isn't there an easy way to get the Jhudora / Illusen Questing trophies?
The easiest way to get the Jhudora / Illusen Questing trophy is by attemping on the first day on the month and having all the items that can be requested in your inventory (preferably done on Level 1). You will need to do two quests, so it is advised that you do the first quest before ~9 AM NST as you will have to wait 12 hours to do your next quest.

If you were unsuccessful with that method, then the way to go would be to just continue on with the quests regularly every 12 hour interval without any prior set up.


▸ What is a safe amount of Neopoints to have before Jhudora / Illusen Questing to Level 50?
As of March 23rd, 2021, the safest amount of Neopoints to have for Jhudora Questing would be 20m. The safest amount of Neopoints to have for Illusen Questing would be 15m.

This amount does not mean you will be guaranteed to reach/finish Level 50, but this is the hypothetical amount of a typical Jhudora / Illusen Questing run without redeeming high end items such as r99 stamps.


▸ Where can I find people to sell/lend an unbuyable item quickly for Jhudora / Illusen Questing?
You can find collectors to sell/lend requested unbuyable items over at the following NeoBoard Chats below. You would want to first start off at the Trading / Auctions NeoBoard as that's where it's most popular to request backup.

NeoBoard Chats for Jhudora / Illusen Questing
- Trading / Auctions NeoBoard Chat
- Battledome NeoBoard Chat
- Charter: Main NeoBoard Chat (Premium Only)


▸ Is there some sort of etiquette when requesting Jhudora / Illusen Quest help at the later levels?
Here's a quick list of things to know about getting Jhudora / Illusen Quest help when you're around the r99 range:
- Be kind and remember the human.
- Be ready to accept failure.
- Nobody is entitled to lend an item.
- Nobody is entitled to buy/sell an item at a price that a side might disagree with.
- Not everyone is online at the time you would start questing.
- Avoid spamming multiple threads within the same NeoBoard Chat.
- Do follow ups if you plan to do a backup thread such as item requested, completion/failure, time remaining, etc.
- Try to replace a lent item within a reasonable time frame.
- When creating a NeoBoard Post, make your thread easily identifiable that you are on a timed quest (such as putting Jhudora / Illusen and/or their smilies in the title, or a copied message in post).


▸ Is there anything after Quest 50 for Jhudora / Illusen Quests?
Nope, there is nothing after Quest 50 for Jhudora / Illusen Quests. All the requested items will be r99 until you reset.


▸ Is there anything else I need to know about Jhudora / Illusen Quests?
If you do fail your Jhudora / Illusen Quests, do remember to check back and receive the failure message, so you can try again after 12 hours. The quest reset timer will not be activated until you do so. You don't want to panic when the yearly Illusen's Glade/Jhudora's Bluff avatars come by and you're still on cooldown for either of them.

Special thanks and FAQ contributions here from dolphindancer789 (Guilds) and Neopets Guild FAQ (Guilds).

Games FAQs

▸ Is it worth it to play Neopets Games?
Depending on what you play them for, yes and no. They're a great way to pad out your user lookup with spiffy trophies, but they're not the best for earning fast NP. Not to say they're unviable, they're a great secondary or tertiary NP source for newer accounts saddled with numerous restrictions. However, aged accounts generally have much more efficient means of earning NP.

Flash Games Related

▸ Why can't I see anything? It's all just a grey screen/three dots/blank for me when I try to load any Neopets Flash games.
Most modern browsers disable Flash content by default due to its security flaws and growing obsolescence, you will, therefore, have to re-enable Flash yourself.

Jump to instructions on how to enable Flash


▸ Is it possible to play Flash Games on my mobile device?
You will probably require the use of a third-party browser that specifically supports Flash in order to play Flash games on mobile. The only exception is AAA's Revenge, which is actually made in HTML5 and can, therefore, be run on most default mobile browsers.

TNT has been working on converting their Flash content to HTML5 over the past few years, so it is expected that the converted versions of these Flash games will all be easily accessible on mobile.


▸ What are the best Flash Games to play for Neopoints?
While this is largely subjective, varying depending on your aptitude, luck, and skill, several fan favourites for quick NP include Fashion Fever and Kass Basher.


▸ Why is Kass Basher (and other games) giving out fewer points than usual?
Game NP ratios change on the 25th of each month. While there are a small handful of games with a static NP ratio, most games have a fluctuating ratio that typically alternates between an easy score and a demanding score each month. NP ratios change in order to encourage players to try a variety of games for NP instead of sticking to just their favorite few.


▸ Are Neopoint Flash game boosters worth it?
No. They can be a nice bonus if you happen to have them (Premium Membership, Games Fortune Cookie, Lutari Beads, Charity Corner Perk), but it's not worth investing in these specifically for game NP boosters as the benefit is either too paltry or only occurs randomly and is therefore unreliable. You may wish to try the daily Featured Game for the 2x NP bonus though, it's free after all.


▸ What are Mirror Games?
Mirror games are, as implied, mirrors for the Flash games you can play on Neopets. These mirrors were conceptualized years ago for use in promotional campaigns so that people could try out a copy of some Neopets games on other sites.

Mirror games are usually identical to the base game, and they are perfectly fine for you to play and even submit scores and earn NP in. Mirror games may have a different NP ratio from the base game, so in some cases, the mirror is easier to play for NP if the base game currently has a very demanding NP ratio this month.

NOTE: You are not allowed to play both the original and the mirror on the same day. For example, if you already sent scores in the mirror version of Meerca Chase II today, do not play and send scores on the original Meerca Chase II today and vice versa. Doing so is considered cheating and TNT may take action against you for it.

Additionally, mirror games do not have a high score table. If you wish to earn a trophy in a game, you must play the original.


▸ Is there anything else I need to know about Flash Games?
In a couple of the older games, you'll sometimes spot Oliver, aka The Phantom Orange Shirt Guy. He was an old Neopets programmer that created many Flash Games like Ice Cream Machine and Yooyuball. You can find his appearances over at the following page:

The Phantom Orange Shirt Guy Article
jellyneo.net/?go=oliver

Game Trophies Related


▸ What are Neopets Game Trophies and how do they work? How do I get them?
Game trophies that you earn will appear on your user lookup for all to admire. You get these, of course, by playing Neopets games. This is not restricted only to Flash games, a variety of PHP games such as Cheat!, Snow Wars and Cellblock have trophies to earn too.

Flash game trophies are earned by submitting any scores that are high enough to place within the top 17 of that game's high score table. Placing 1st to 3rd will grant you a Gold trophy, 4th to 8th a Silver, and 9th to 17th a Bronze.

PHP games work a bit differently and tend to have varying conditions that must be met in order to earn a trophy in them. For example, winning a specific number of rounds against the CPU opponent. However, some PHP games still feature a high score table. You should look up guides for any specific game you're interested in to see how trophy distribution works in those games.

Most high score tables are reset monthly, so even if the scores during the current month are too high for you to beat, they might be lower next month.

Once you earn a trophy in a game, you will own it permanently. You do not have to maintain a high score in order to keep your trophy.

Trophies can also be upgraded. For example, if you earned a Bronze trophy in a particular game before, you will be able to upgrade that to a Silver or Gold later on if you send a qualifying score. Trophies do not downgrade, if you have a Gold trophy in a game, you will keep the Gold even if you send in a Silver or Bronze score later on.


▸ I just placed for a trophy, but I don't see it on my userlookup. Why is that?
Trophies are not distributed immediately. At the time of writing, they are awarded daily at approximately 8:50 pm NST. This time slowly gets later as the months go by. The trophy script also runs in ascending order of game ID, so if the game you're waiting for has a really high ID number (maybe 1000+) it might take a few minutes before your trophy is awarded. Don't worry if you don't see your trophy immediately.

However, a nasty glitch occurs sometimes that causes the trophy script to not run for that day. There is no recourse for when this happens, but at the very least it is a somewhat rare occasion. Days where the trophy script fails to run are known as "skips" or "skip days".

Note that because trophies are not awarded immediately, the high score you submit must be on the high score table at the time of awarding. If you sent a qualifying score earlier in the day, but have been pushed off the top 17 by the time trophies are being awarded for that game, you will not receive a trophy.


▸ What is a score review? Am I in trouble?
Some scores that you submit might be subjected to a review. You will know when a red message appears upon pressing Send Score that your score will be reviewed first. This is normal and there is no need to be alarmed. Score reviews typically occur when scores are sent too quickly, or when you exceed a certain score threshold for that game. Each game has its own individual threshold whereby any score that exceeds the threshold is automatically sent for review.

When your score is sent for review, you will not receive the NP for that score or be entered into the high score table until the score is approved, after which they will send you a NeoMail message to inform you that your score was accepted, and you will receive your NP and high score placement then.

Reviews typically take a few days to a week, although there have been occasions where reviews take several weeks. Sometimes your score might even be reviewed that very same day. Typically, very popular games that receive a lot of review scores tend to process reviews faster, but this is not a guarantee.

Do know that if your score was rejected for whatever reason, you will not be informed. Your score will simply disappear into the void, never to be heard from again.

NOTE: TNT is not fond of people discussing or revealing the score thresholds for individual games, do not discuss this on-site.


▸ The game bugged out and didn't enter in my score, what gives?!?
Before submitting a score, you might want to ensure that your internet connection is stable and check to see if Neopets itself is encountering any site issues. A fault on either end and your score may fail to go through. Additionally, you are not able to submit scores from a previous day, so if your game window was open before midnight NST*, trying to send a score after midnight will fail. If midnight passes, make sure you close your game window and open a new one, or simply refresh your current one in order to be able to send scores.

If your score fails to go through, there is, unfortunately, no recourse. It cannot be recovered, you will simply have to try and get another score.

* Technically it happens at 12:02 am NST and not exactly at midnight.

Game Spotlights Related

▸ What is Better Than You?
Better Than You is a weekly game competition where you aim to beat a predetermined game score. You will receive an avatar and an item prize, as well as NP and a trophy depending on how quickly you managed to beat the score.

First 10 winners: Gold Trophy + 20,000 NP
11th to 50th winner: Silver Trophy + 10,000 NP
51st to 500th winner: Bronze Trophy + 3,000 NP

Once 500 people have beaten Better Than You, the competition will be closed until the next round begins.

NOTE: This was written before TNT announced Better Than You would be on hiatus due to Adobe Flash's EOL.


▸ Is there a specific time when Better Than You resets?
New rounds of Better Than You typically come out every week on Wednesday. There is no exact time, TNT has to update BTY manually so it could theoretically be at any time on Wednesday. Rarely, they have even released it a day early or a day late. The most common timeframe for when BTY is released is currently between 11 am ~ 4 pm NST, but this can and has changed before and is not a guarantee.


▸ I matched the Better Than You score exactly, why didn't I get the avatar/trophy?
Unlike the Daily Dare event which allows you to simply match the given score, you must beat the score given for BTY. Simply matching the BTY score exactly does not count, you need to score higher.


▸ How is each week's Better Than You score determined?
The Better Than You score is usually derived from the current high score table for the chosen game. That means BTY rounds at the start of the month are typically easiest while the high scores at at their lowest, and conversely BTY rounds at the end of the month tend to be more difficult.


▸ Is there a way how to predict which game this week's Better Than You is going to be?
There is only one (fairly tedious) way to "predict" the upcoming game, and that is to refresh the image URL of the next round until you notice it has been updated. TNT usually updates the image before putting up the next round, and the image might hold a hint as to what the game might be.


▸ What is the Mystery Picture Competition?
The Mystery Picture Competition is a weekly game competition in which TNT uploads a cropped/blurred/pixelated image and you will have to guess what exactly the image is. The image TNT chooses could technically be from any anywhere on the site.

If you correctly guess what the image is, you will receive the shown item prize, NP, as well as a trophy depending on how quickly you managed to answer.

First 10 winners: Gold Trophy
11th to 50th winner: Silver Trophy
51st to 250th winner: Bronze Trophy

Only the first 250 winners will receive the item and trophy, although anyone who answers correctly afterwards will still receive NP.

The NP prize is a 2,000,000 NP pool that is split evenly amongst all winners. That means if only 10 people guess correctly one week, each winner will receive 200,000 NP.


▸ Is there a specific time when Mystery Picture resets?
New rounds of Mystery Pic typically come out every week on Thursday. There is no exact time, TNT has to update MPic manually so it could theoretically be at any time on Thursday. Rarely, they have even released it a day early or a day late. The most common timeframe for when MPic is released is currently between 11 am ~ 4 pm NST, but this can and has changed before and is not a guarantee.

The current round will be judged on the same day, typically at most a few hours before the new round is posted.


▸ How should I format my answer for Mystery Picture?
Since Mystery Pic is not judged manually, trying to find the best way to format your answer so that their automated judging can accurately parse your answer might seem tricky. The most concrete (but not guaranteed) way is to use the page's actual title, located at the top left of the page's main content in bold.

For example, if you think the answer is the Mystery Island Beach it is best to copy and paste the page title shown here:

As such, submitting "The Beach" should be sufficient and is a pretty safe bet.


▸ Does TNT provide any hints to the Mystery Picture answer?
While you should not count on receiving any hints, occasionally the item prize being offered for the current Mystery Pic will be related to the source of the image. This is not a guarantee, and more often than not the prize is a random and completely unrelated item.


▸ How is each Mystery Picture created? Is it just a small portion of a larger image, or is it always the full image?
While it is always a heavily pixelated mess, TNT is known to do both: pixelating and compressing entire images or simply cropping out a small portion of a larger image and pixelating only that instead. There is no guarantee that the Mystery Pic is really the whole image and not just a cropped portion.


▸ Am I allowed to share Mystery Picture Competition answers?
While you are allowed to discuss the image with other users, you are not allowed to outright share the direct answer with them.


▸ What happened to _____ Spotlight?
These Spotlight competitions were removed from the site due to low submission numbers and decline of members playing these games.

- Adventure Generator Spotlight
- Better Than You
- Faerie Caves Spotlight
- Hannah and the Kreludor Caves Spotlight
- Hannah and the Pirate Caves Spotlight
- Lenny Conundrum
- Tyrannian Mini Golf Spotlight


▸ Am I allowed to enter in any Game Spotlights on my side accounts?
No, Game Spotlights reward you with NP and NP items and as such you are not allowed to participate on your side accounts.


▸ Is there anything else I need to know about Game Spotlights?
If it doesn't work out this week, then there's always next week (unless the spotlight has been cancelled, then RIP). Just keep on trying and you'll get the trophy eventually!

Food Club Related

▸ What is Food Club? Is Food Club worth it?
Food Club (FC) is a betting game which makes you profit in the long run. Older accounts in particular can profit a lot from Food Club, as they can bet (and therefore win) more. You can expect to win roughly 1.7-2.2x what you bet in the long term.


▸ Everything looks so confusing??? How do you even play?
If you can count to ten you have enough maths for food club ;) My advice to all newbies is to follow other people's bets. You can find a listing of FC bettors over at /~Hostia. And if youre just looking for NP, that's all you ever need to do. If you want recommendations on who to follow, let us know your goals for FC and how risky you want to play, and ask over there! :) Just remember that each day you should follow all ten bets from one individual. Don't try mix-n-matching sets blindly, or only following part of a set. If you're not ready to risk that much money, reduce your bet amount instead.
Various Food Club Guides
/~BlazeaBruce (Bon's guide to Really Lazy Food Club)
/~OrvinnTheFirstMate (General Terminology / How to Follow a Bet Page / Collect Winnings Info)
/~Keemif (Visual Food Club Following Guide)
/~myfoodclubbets (Hugo's Food Club page)
/~Jawsnapper0991 (Food Club - A Complete Guide of Definitions and How to Bet)
/~windagame (Sirhatter's guide to gambling in the Food Club)
/~Zanzacharee (Food Club Guides and Bettors Directory (NT Articles included!)


▸ So, how much NP do I need to start with? How often do you lose?
Assuming that you are making bets which are of moderate risk or less, I personally think a enough NP for a week of bets is plenty, but it's really up to you. You can bet less if you want to (though the more you bet, the more profit you are likely to make overall.

FC is luck-based so there will be days (sometimes many days in a row!) when you lose. However, it's definitely worthwhile in the long term. How often you lose depends on how riskily you play. As a guess, even safe bettors can expect to lose ~1/4ish of the time.


▸ How old should my account be to playing Food Club?
I'd personally start playing at around 1yr, though older accounts are greatly advantaged. To judge for yourself: expect to make back roughly 1.6-2.2x what you bet, copying someone else's bets takes less than 5mins, your bet amount is displayed on the main betting page (it's 50np + 2x your account age in days), and you can make 10 bets per day.


▸ When are the Food Club gates closed?
Gates are closed for betting between 1:45pm and 2:15pm NST. When they reopen, you can still place bets for that round until the results are out.

As of March 23rd, 2021, each round ends at about 3:49pm NST and it gets later by a few seconds each day.


▸ I accidently placed the wrong bet. Can I take it back?
You cannot take back your Food Club bets. Placing bets that were from the prior round to the next round will never win, so don't bet really late when results are rolling out.


▸ Where can I find my Food Club bets/results?
You can find your current Food Club bets in this link and you can find the results in the Collecting Winnings link. If the round has ended by seeing that the Current Bets page is empty and you do not see any winnings, that means you busted. Also, do know that Food Club bets do expire after 8 days.


▸ Is Charity Corner's "Oh, Blimey!" (+5 Bets For 1 Week) Food Club Perk any good?
If we considered the NP to point cost from last year's Charity Corner, the cost of points used would exceed the amount of NP gained in return on average (assuming we went with the more painless method of donating Sticky Snowballs instead of a thousand 1 point items). An older account that can bet ~10.6k+ would only slightly benefit from the perk as much in comparison of betting without it.

Trophy-wise, this perk can be handy to cover more scenarios if you are disregarding the profit difference without it.


▸ Do the Food Club odds change? If so, why?
The probability of a pirate winning does not change as the round progresses. However, the return you'd get from a given pirate does change depending on how many people bet on that pirate (or others in an arena). Odds going up means you'd win more if they do win, odds going down means you'd win less.


▸ I saw there was a trophy for Food Club. How would one get that?
Trophies are awarded each day for largest NP collection. You can hold your winnings for 7 days and 8 rounds. Many people try for a trophy run at the end of the month since scores are reset on the 1st (so hold from the 25th - 1st if there are 31 days in the month, from the 24th - 1st if there are 30 days).

For a trophy run, it's recommended that you make more risky bets with higher chance of returns. Also, since trophy runs depend on how much you win from Food Club, older accounts who can bet more per bet, have the advantage.


▸ What are Food Adjustments/Allergies?
Each pirate has food types that they like and ones they are allergic too, and this can influence their performance. Some people use this to inform their bets, but in general food adjustment is already factored into opening odds.


▸ What does this acronym/phrase mean in Food Club?
Here's a quick list of Food Club related terms:

PHRASE
MEANING
FC
Food Club
Bust / Busted
You have no winning bets. You lost everything.
Bust Rate
The probability of busting.
BP
Bustproof or a set that will always win something. These sets are usually small profit or a partial loss.
FA
Food Adjustment
ROI
Return on Investment
Win Total divided by Bet Total in units
Gambit
It's when people make a prediction on which five pirates they think will win.
Due
When a pirate hasn't won in ages, so people might have a suspicion that pirate will win in the near future.
Positive Arena
Where one pirate has a greater than 50% chance of winning.
Safety
Safeties are bets on the non 2:1, non-13:1 pirates in a positive arena. Most of your bets will use the 2:1 pirates in the positive arena, so safeties are your contingencies in case the 2:1 pirate loses.
Partial
This is when you have won less than the cost of bets placed, but it was not a complete bust.
TER
Total Expected Ratio (or return), is a probability-weighted average of the possible results on a set of bets. High TERs theoretically give best outcomes in the long term but have a high bust rate, as TER is skewed by very high but unlikely outcomes.
MER
Max Expected Ratio
Upset
When the pirate with the highest chance to win in that arena loses.
Ten Bet
This is when you are betting on the same pirate for all the ten bets you can place for day.
Max Bet
This is when you're placing the maximum amount of Neopoints per bet (or the amount when the bet reaches the 1m cap).
OOGA
Only One Good Arena
