▸ Is there anything else I need to know about Food Club?
Food Club is game of luck! There will be times where you will encounter some bad days in Food Club, but this game is still a pretty decent way of how to earn tons of Neopoints over time.

NeoQuest I & II Related

▸ Is NeoQuest going to break once Flash has been removed?
Neither of the NeoQuest games are Flash-based, so they will be unaffected.


▸ Is NeoQuest I linked to NeoQuest II?
They both have similar gameplay, but are otherwise not linked and have completely unrelated stories. You do not have to finish NeoQuest I to start NeoQuest II.


▸ My NeoQuest progress is gone?!?
NeoQuest I is linked to your active pet. If you have changed your active pet since you last played, you will have to change back. Additionally, NeoQuest I games reset after approximately several months to a year of inactivity. NeoQuest II games are linked to your account instead of a particular pet, and also will never reset.


▸ If NeoQuest I is linked to a particular pet, what happens if I abandon or trade the pet away?
Your game will be transferred with the pet. Whoever adopts or receives your pet will be able to continue an active NQ game from where you left off with that pet.


▸ What happens if I die in NeoQuest?
You will lose some EXP, and in NeoQuest II, your current Gold will be halved upon dying.
You will also be transported back to Neopia City (NQ I) or your most recent resting point (NQ II).
If you die while playing on Insane mode, you will have to start over from the beginning instead. This applies to both NQ I and II.


▸ How do I access the higher difficulties for NeoQuest?
You can access Evil difficulty by beating Normal, and you can access Insane by beating Evil. This applies to both NeoQuest I and II. Since game progress is tied to your pet for NeoQuest I, receiving someone else's pet that has already cleared Normal or Evil mode will also allow you to skip those and challenge the next difficulty immediately.


▸ What do the different difficulties encompass?
In general, all enemies and bosses have higher health and may gain additional skills they did not have on lower difficulties.

On NeoQuest I's Evil mode, there will be another final boss immediately after the original one.
On NeoQuest I's Insane mode, the EXP required for each level-up is doubled, and there is a third final boss immediately after the initial two.

On NeoQuest II's Evil and Insane mode, regular enemies will start dropping equipment with skill bonuses.

Dying on Insane mode in either game will force you to restart the game from the beginning.


▸ Are there any good guides for NeoQuest?
A guide directory featuring a plethora of NQ I and II guides can be found in the link below. Dedicated skill guides and maps can be found there as well.
/~Tetrakaidecagon


▸ What do I get for finishing NeoQuest?
Finishing NeoQuest I and II will award you their Bronze/Silver/Gold trophy for beating Normal/Evil/Insane mode respectively.

Both games have avatars that can be earned (1 avatar in NQ I and 3 in NQ II) by completing various in-game tasks.

NeoQuest II awards you a random exclusive item for beating the game. Insane mode will only award items once, but lower difficulties will award prizes each time you complete them. Check a dedicated NQ II guide for a breakdown of which item can be obtained from which mode. You will also receive Neopoints for beating bosses.




▸ Can I play NeoQuest on my side accounts?
No. Since you will receive items/Neopoints for playing NeoQuest I and II, you may only play them on your main account.


▸ Is there anything else I need to know about NeoQuest?
In Neoquest II, if you've saved your Fathers Sword, then it might be of great use against the final fight against Terask. Your Fathers Sword does 25% more damage than Sword of Kings in the final battle.

The Kadoatery Related

▸ The Kadoatery? What's it for?
The Kadoatery is a game where you aim to feed hungry Kadoaties before others! You'll get a trophy when you feed your first one.

As you feed more, your trophy will upgrade from Bronze (1 to 9 fed) to Silver (10 to 24 fed) and finally Gold (25+ fed). Once you've fed 75, you'll also obtain the Kadoatery avatar.


▸ How do I feed a Kadoatie?
If there's a Kad that's unfed, the food item it currently desires will be listed below it. Simply obtain the food item and click on the Kad to feed it, but you have to be quick or someone might feed it before you.


▸ I hear Kadoaties are notoriously hard to feed due to the competition. Is this true?
While it might have been true in the past, these days it's really not so bad. The player base has unfortunately dwindled since the site's heyday, but that means less competition in the Kadoatery too. Your timezone may come into play as well, some timezones are more active than others.


▸ Should I hoard lots of food items that Kadoaties might want before trying to feed any?
Buying food beforehand (referred to as having an SDB) is not recommended if you are only playing for the avatar. It is very costly to complete a full SDB of Kad food, this is mostly done only by dedicated feeders who intend to feed past 75. If you're only here for the avatar, you should just search for and buy the item you need on the Shop Wizard quickly.


▸ Is the Super Shop Wizard better for Kadding?
While it's better on your wallet, some players note that SSW takes a bit more time to find an item than the regular SW, probably because SSW tries to search the entire market at once. In the end, it's up to you, it doesn't really make that much of a difference in the short term.


▸ I went to the Kadoatery and the food they're asking for is all so expensive!
Don't get the wrong impression! The unfed Kads you'll usually see upon casually walking in are indeed usually the really expensive ones. That's why they've been unfed for a while. All the other fed Kads are probably reasonably cheap, which is why they've all been fed already. If you want to go for a cheap Kad, you should try to catch them when they've just refreshed and are hungry again.


▸ Are those expensive Kads going to be there forever?
As long as nobody feeds them, yes they will remain there and occupy space. Eventually, someone will come along and feed them though, but it might take a while before anyone volunteers.



▸ Why are all the Kads crying when they've already been fed?
It's just a little detail thrown in by TNT, at 11 pm NST the Kadoatery's lights are turned off and the Kadoaties start to cry since they're afraid of the dark. The lights come back on at 3 am NST, so they'll stop crying then.


▸ When do the Kads refresh?
To find out, you'll want to visit the Kadoatery topic on the Games NeoBoard. Look for a topic featuring Kadoatie emoticons, that should usually be the one you need. Inside you'll find fellow Kadoatie feeders, new and seasoned, who are tracking the next possible refresh times for the Kadoatery. The people who track refresh times are known as timekeepers or TKers.


▸ I don't understand the timekeeping posts. How does a refresh actually work?
For that, you should refer to a dedicated Kadding guide to help you understand the nuances of the Kadoatery's mechanics (one will be linked below). You'll also learn about the various terms used on the Kadoatie boards such as splits, mains, minis, NTO, etc.
/~Shouir


▸ Is it ok to help out with timekeeping?
There's a great guide mentioned below if you'd like to help out with the tking effort. It's recommended to observe the more experienced TKers first, in addition to reading the tking guide thoroughly. Timekeeping is very important and many people depend on accurate tking to feed Kads, so learn the subject well!
/~ohmyaelin


▸ Is there any point to feeding more than 75 Kadoaties?
The number of Kadoaties you fed is displayed on your trophy and will continue to increase. There is no other tangible reward, however, but it can be a lot of fun to feed Kadoaties.


▸ Why do people overfeed?
Many of the overfeeders have been feeding Kadoaties for years, for a variety of reasons. Some enjoy improving their trophy's feed count, some enjoy the rush of trying to feed Kadoaties quickly, some find it relaxing, some enjoy the Kadding community, etc. It is a hobby for many.


▸ Is there anything else I need to know about The Kadoatery?
Some of the Kadoatie names have pop culture references to them. There are names from Mario Bros., Futurama, Naruto, and more!

Stock Market Related

▸ What is the Stock Market?
The Neopets Stock Market is a HTML game that you can find here. The aim is to turn a profit by buying and selling company shares, which are portions of a company's money that you can own, and which change in value over time. However, unlike the real-world stock market, the value of company shares in the Neopets Stock Market are decided by algorithms and not by changes in the economy. There are many other differences as well, but the Neopets Stock market is altogether much less risky and complicated to invest in.


▸ What stocks should I buy, and when?
Firstly, the lowest price that you can normally buy shares for is 15np. You should always buy from companies with shares at this price if possible, but if you only have a short window to buy, share prices of up to 17np will do. Secondly, you can only buy 1,000 shares per day. To make the most profit in the long run you should buy the full amount available daily, if you can. Following this method, you will be spending between 15,000np and 17,000np per day on shares. Make sure to complete the Trudy's Surprise daily every day, as for most of the month this will give you enough np to invest!

To make it easier to find the cheapest stocks, there is a hidden "bargain" page sorting the companies with the lowest current share prices that can be found here. It is also worth noting that some Battleground of the Obelisk and Charity Corner event boons allow you to buy stocks for prices as low as 10np per share, allowing you to profit even more in the long run .


▸ How do I buy stocks?
You can find information about companies by clicking the Buy tab and searching for a ticker symbol (a set of letters representing a company), through the full list of companies, or through the hidden bargain" page. Each of these pages shows you the number of stocks available for that company (Volume), the price that company's shares started out at that day (Open), the current price of the shares (Curr), and the numerical change from the beginning of the day price to the current price (Change). The Curr column is the only column necessary when deciding which stocks to buy. The prices for all companies update approximately every 30 minutes, but it is worth noting that they can stay the same.

Once you have chosen a company to invest in, click on the letters of its ticker symbol. This will take you to the company profile, which will tell you some information about the company (note that this is only useful as trivia and doesn't have any impact on stocks). Then, click the company's full name to get to the Buying Shares page for that company. Type the number of shares you want to buy in the Number of Shares box (up to a maximum of 1,000 per day) and click Buy Shares to complete the purchase.

Your purchased shares will then show up in your portfolio (on the My Portfolio tab). This page shows you the same Open, Current and Change information that was seen on the buying pages, now under the heading "Today". The other columns, with the headings Holdings and Overall, show you the quantity of shares you own in each company (Qty), the total amount you paid for the shares (Paid), the total amount all the shares would currently sell for (Mkt Value) and the percentage change between the amount you spent in total and the total amount the shares would currently sell for (% Change). The Current Price column is again the only column necessary for deciding which stocks to sell.


▸ When should I sell stocks?
That is entirely up to you! The only rule to follow in order not to lose np is to never sell your shares for less than you bought them. Many people decide on a share price to sell at (usually between 60np -100np) and will not sell until one of their stocks hit that price. However, there are multiple selling strategies giving faster turnovers or larger profits that are described by SilverCyanide here.


▸ How do I sell stocks?
When it becomes time to sell your stocks, visit your Portfolio page. Next to the icon for each company, there is a small grey triangle that, when clicked, will drop down with all the sets of shares you own for the company. In the "Sell" box, on the far right, type in the number of shares you want to sell in each row. Then, click Sell Shares at the bottom of the page or hit Enter on your keyboard to open a new window which will tell you how much you sold each share for. Nigel the Chia takes a tiny 20np commission from your on-hand np for every sale you make, and you can't sell without it, so remember to have a few np available.


▸ Is investing in the Stock Market worth it?
The short answer is yes, as there is a lot to gain and little to lose. However, as time is required to turn a profit, patience is a necessity. Shares can take weeks, months or years to gain in value, so whilst you can usually expect a sure profit, it will probably not be a fast turnaround.


▸ Do stocks go bankrupt anymore?
The last recorded bankruptcy was in 2004. With everything that has happened regarding the management and development of Neopets since then, it is difficult to say whether more stock companies will go bankrupt, but it is highly unlikely. Although no bankrupt companies have ever started selling shares again, the chances of losing out on your investments in the Neopets Stock Market currently are so small that they are not worth worrying about, especially if you diversify.


▸ How long does it take for Stocks to be ideally profitable to sell?
No matter what strategy you choose to tackle the Neopets Stock Market, it will usually take at least a few weeks to begin to profit, possibly longer. Most established strategies recommend starting by spending 3 - 4 weeks building up your portfolio by investing in shares from a lot of different companies. Past that, it is mostly a waiting game that could take months or years to reach consistent profit, but profit is almost certainly going to be inevitable. Of course, you do have to remember to sell your stocks when the time is right, otherwise you won't earn anything! It is a good idea to make sure to regularly check your current share prices, which at a minimum you should do every time you invest daily.


▸ Can Neopets Premium help me with the Stock Market?
The Premium toolbar on Neopets offers a Stock Market overview on the Bankroll tab which can show you the overall quantity of stocks you own, the total amount you have invested, the overall current market value of all your stocks, and the % change in the amount invested and the current market value. This does not notify you of individual stock changes and does become less useful the more diverse your portfolio. However, it can be useful to track your progress towards the avatar and to see whether your stock values are positive or negative overall.


▸ What do I do if I just want the avatar?
If you invest in 1,000 stocks at 15np each per day, then you will get the "Sell! SELL!!" avatar in 67 days and will have set yourself up a diverse portfolio in the process. However, if you don't want to wait that long, there is a much faster way to get it. Due to a glitch, you cannot get the avatar by buying shares worth over 1,000np, and as you can only buy 1,000 shares per day, this means that you will need to buy shares on at least 2 different days in order to get the avatar. You can therefore invest just before and just after 12am NST in shares worth between 500np – 999np and then sell them straight away to get the avatar without risking much of your np. For more detailed information on this fast method, read DT's guide here.


▸ Should I only buy stocks in one company, or should I diversify?
It is best to spread your money out by buying shares in many different companies. There are many reasons for this. Firstly, if you only buy from one company, you will probably not always be able to take advantage of buying at the lowest share price of 15np and your profit will be limited. Secondly, it lowers your risk; if you invest in 5,000 shares of one company and the company goes bankrupt, you lose all your investment. However, if you invest in 1,000 shares of five companies and one goes bankrupt, you still have 4,000 shares left. Finally, if you diversify, there is a greater chance that the next stock to reach a profitable share price will be one of yours, and you can sell.


▸ Can I play the Stock Market on a side account?
No – this is against the rules, as the stock market will earn you NP!

Plushie Tycoon Related

▸ What is Plushie Tycoon?
Plushie Tycoon is essentially a "business simulation" game. You will start off in the game with 50,000 NP and in order to "win" you must turn out a profit by the end of the game (50,001 NPs or above).


▸ What do I get for winning?
Any win will net you the Plushie Tycoon avatar and at least a Bronze trophy, but you may receive a better trophy depending on how much NP you managed to obtain.

50,001+ NP = Bronze trophy
250,001+ NP = Silver trophy
1,000,000+ NP = Gold trophy

You will also receive an NP prize depending on how many plushies you managed to sell, the minimum being 1k and maximum being 320k.


▸ Is it worth playing Plushie Tycoon for NP?
No, there are much better alternatives to making NP these days. Receiving several hundred thousand for one game of Plushie Tycoon may sound enticing, but the time and effort needed (requires over 2,000,000 plushies sold for the max prize of 320k NP) far outweighs the potential gain. Play for the avatar or trophy, or for fun, but this is not an efficient way to earn NP.


▸ Is it best to start as early as possible in the month?
Not necessarily. Keep in mind that taxes and rent are due every 7 days after your first-day*, so starting too early might cause your taxes and rent to be due extremely close to the end of the month, which is not ideal. Depending on how many days there are in the current month, you should ideally start on a day that leaves you with only 3 tax/rent days instead of 4.

* e.g. starting on the 4th means your tax and rent are payable on the 11th, 18th and 25th.


▸ I'm trying to make/sell plushies in the factory/store but nothing is happening?
The game doesn't run 24/7, it only runs for 8 hours a day. By default, it runs from 10 am NST to 6 pm NST every day, but you can customize the timezone from the main PT page at the beginning of the game so that the 8 hours are at a more convenient time for you.


▸ Are there any good resources for Plushie Tycoon?
A fairly comprehensive basic start-up guide can be found here:
/~MapleHood

This page is an excellent resource for all kinds of PT information, such as basic loading times, upgrading costs, etc.
/~GrundyTycoon


▸ When is the factory/sales update?
There is an update every hour while your game is running (8 updates a day). Many PT guides still list the update time at :01, but this is no longer accurate due to a glitch that causes it to get later by approximately 1 minute every day. Since it is constantly getting later, an exact answer cannot be provided here, but once you find the current update time you should be able to easily keep your eye on it going forward.


▸ Why did I suddenly go bankrupt?
If you find yourself suddenly losing large amounts of money, ensure that you have fired the workers in your factory. Your workers will continue to take hourly payment even if your factory no longer has any pending jobs. Forgetting to fire factory workers is a common mistake and is the most prominent cause of bankruptcy for newer players.


▸ What happens if I go bankrupt?
You will, unfortunately, have to restart your game. Note that you can restart as many times within the month as necessary, so there is no actual penalty for going bankrupt aside from the time lost from having to start over.


▸ What are the best species of plushies to buy?
There are no single best species of plushie to buy, but in general, you should probably avoid any plushies that:

- Require less than 3 or 4 rolls of cloth.
- Do not require accessories.

Beyond this, feel free to experiment with different species and materials. Since sales prices fluctuate constantly, none of them will be the best all the time.


▸ Should I do a full game if I want the avatar?
If you're only aiming for the avatar, it is possible to pull through in only 1 week. Start 6 days before the last day of the month (e.g 24th if the month has 30 days) and follow the /~MapleHood Guide linked above. Doing so means the game will end before you have to deal with any taxes or rent.

On average, you should be able to make a profit after 4 days, but this is dependent on your luck with raw material prices/sales prices.


▸ I need more help, is there anywhere I can go to ask about Plushie Tycoon?
The Games section of the NeoBoards always has a Plushie Tycoon help topic that is run by experienced PT players who can offer more specific advice for your game.
Games NeoBoard Chat

Special thanks and FAQ contributions here from riparu (Everything), unfreeze_divicool72 (Food Club), squigeons (Food Club), phoenix79 (Food Club), and _snails_pace_ (Stock Market).

Mobile FAQs

Mobile App Related

▸ Is Neopets moving to mobile soon?
Neopets is not creating a mobile app. It was stated by a TNT Staff member that it was the very first thing they looked at, but it was deemed unfeasible at the time (Sep 2020).


▸ Is the site only going to be on mobile in the future? Meaning the site will not exist on desktop?
The site will still exist on desktop. It is not going away to solely function on mobile.

- Neopets Editorial - Issue 862 | Question 9 [link] (Confirmation that the site will still exist on desktop)


▸ Weren't there plans for a mobile app at the end of Viacom's ownership?
Yes, there were plans for a Neopets mobile companion app, and it was called Neopets On-The-Go. From retired TNT Staff Member, Snarkie: The implementation of a mobile-friendly site would have taken monumentally long and the idea was not guaranteed approval, so a companion app was discussed instead! The companion app would have been more of a supportive tool when players would be away from the desktop site, featuring activtites such as checking your NeoMails, training times, and more.

As apps of this nature are often not financially viable, the idea was not fully pursued. The app still saw development by a small team of volunteers (salaried workers that would work overtime without pay) and was essentially a side passion project.

At 97% completion, the mobile app was unfortunately cancelled by JumpStart. All the remaining resources were directed to the creation of Ghoul Catchers, and they never knew why. By the time this information was posted, the companion app's coding would have been too outdated by today's standards to ever be released.

Head over to your Settings/Preferences and there should be a Beta Theme section. Do note that not all of the site themes have been converted, but at least you can change out of the default theme.


▸ I can't find my NC items in the Inventory of Neopets Beta. Help!
In the top right corner of your inventory, there should be a toggle feature to swap NP items and NC items.


▸ My unconverted (UC) pets look odd in the Beta Customization application. What's up with that?
Not all the unconverted pets' artwork have been fully transferred, this issue has been noted by TNT support.


▸ My unconverted (UC) pets aren't saving properly in the Beta Customization application. Why is that?
UC Customization is currently broken on Neopets Beta. You can still save UC customizations through the Classic Customization application though.


▸ Why are some of my closet items missing/blanked out?
This could mean several things:
- The items have not been converted to Beta yet.
- The items are currently being worn on another pet.
- The items are saved in the presets feature.
- The items are not in your Closet, and are actually located in your Safety Deposit Box, Gallery, NC Album, Inventory, Item Transfer Log, etc.


▸ Is it possible to attach Petpetpets (P3s) to my Petpets (P2s) in Neopets Beta?
No, it is not possible to attach Petpetpets to your Petpets in Neopets Beta. You must use the Classic Inventory to attach Petpetpets to your Petpets.


▸ Are Random Events active in Neopets Beta?
Random Events are not active in Neopets Beta. Random Event avatars with interactive requirements are still active, however (i.e. the Sloth! avatar is not available). If you plan on getting certain avatars, Battledome challengers, etc. then we'd suggest visiting its Classic page (add an "/" or "/x" to the end of the URL string) if available.


▸ Why are there only 7 games in Neopets Beta?
Most, but not all, of the Flash games are in the process of being converted into HTML5. The most popular games and avatar games are guaranteed to be converted for the new Games Room eventually.

In addition to this, the following features are currently not available, but will be implemented in the future:
- NC Featured Game Tickets (and presumably Send It Again Game Tickets)
- In-game Cheat Codes
- Clickable The Phantom Orange Shirt Guy appearances
- Item rewards (none of those games have been converted yet)


▸ Why aren't game score submissions working in Neopets Beta?
For most of the converted games, score submission was disabled. For the other games that otherwise allow score submissions but are still experiencing this issue, the reason is possibly one or more of the following:

- Score submissions were submitted too quickly.
- The score was absurdly high (commonly noticed in Igloo Garage Sale, but the Review Score for that is 1,998 pts).
- The day has been reset (Midnight NST, after 12:03:00 AM to be exact).

For Fashion Fever, you will need to wait 10 seconds in order for the score submission to work.


▸ Am I allowed to send scores for both converted games and Flash games on the same day?
Similar to mirror games, no. You are only allowed to submit scores on one or the other within a day.

- Neopets Editorial - Issue 924 | Question 1 [link] (You are NOT allowed to send scores for both converted games and converted/mirror games)


▸ A Neopets Beta game just rewarded me more than the usual 1k Limit of NP per game. Am I in trouble?
No, but you should probably send a ticket stating that you experienced this problem.


▸ Are Neopets Beta games awarding Game Avatars?
Aside from Ice Cream Machine, they are not awarding Game Avatars at the moment, but if the Flash version is still functional on your end, then it is still possible to use that version to earn the Game Avatar in question.

Classic Gamesroom
The Link


▸ I tried spinning the Wheel of Excitement/Mediocrity/Knowledge, but the wheel disappeared! What can I do to fix this?
This is a known and common issue. You will just have to refresh the page until the wheel appears.


▸ What is this NeoHomes 3.0 I'm hearing about?
Due to Classic NeoHomes (1.0) and NeoHomes 2.0 being Flash features, they are being replaced with a new creation. It is recommended that you empty your Shed in the meantime before its launch.


▸ Are there really no ads on Neopets Beta?
As of right now, there are little to no ads on Neopets Beta.


▸ Is TNT bringing back the Premium Toolbar?
The Premium Toolbar is considered retired and has been moved to its own page.


▸ Is there any way I can mute the News in Neopets Beta?
There is no feature for that and it is unknown if there will be one.


▸ What are the known bugs and future plans for Neopets Beta?
That information can be found in the Release Notes page.


▸ Where can I give feedback/comments about Neopets Beta?
The Mobile-Friendly Beta Launch NeoBoard Chat and/or Editorial would be cool for that.

Ghoul Catchers Related

▸ Is downloading Ghoul Catchers worth it?
You will earn 1k NP for finishing level 1 which takes about 10 seconds or less, and you can do this 50 times a day.

The 50k NP per day that it provides for minimal effort is a huge income boost for a majority of players, making Ghoul Catchers totally worth it. The collectables you get as prizes for clearing each land can sell for quite a bit too, although this is optional (and quite difficult) and simply sticking to 50k a day will earn you much more in the long run anyway.

As of July 22, 2020, TNT announced that Ghoul Catchers will be discontinued, and the app was removed from app stores. If you have downloaded the game before its retirement, you can still earn rewards from playing the game until December 31, 2020 (?).


▸ What's my Ghoul Catchers login?
Ghoul Catchers uses your Neopets UN and PW. Some people report issues logging in when their password is too long, so try changing passwords if you are experiencing login problems.


▸ When does Ghoul Catchers' 50k-a-Day reset?
Ghoul Catchers resets at midnight GMT every day, which is 4 pm NST (5 pm NST during Daylight Savings Time).


▸ How long does it take to receive my signup prizes?
The signup prizes should be awarded to you immediately, but this is known to be glitchy and unfortunately can take much longer or not even be awarded at all. This also applies to any item rewards for clearing later levels.


▸ Why does it keep saying I reached my Neopoints limit before 50k?
This is a bug, the message is not accurate. Keep playing and you will notice that NP is still being awarded to you until you have actually played 50 times for the day. The best way to tell when you have actually reached the limit is to note how much NP you had on hand before playing and to stop once you have 50k more.


▸ Are all the ads/videos broken?
Kinda, they are mostly broken. Watching ads would award you with powerups that would be useful in clearing difficult levels, but these ads no are pretty sporadic when they want to load.


▸ Is there anything else I need to know about Ghoul Catchers?
The game is essentially dead (no pun intended) to TNT. As of March 23rd, 2021, the NP rewards are still being given out, but the Amulets and Backgrounds either have major reward delays or not currently being rewarded.

Legends & Letters Related

▸ Is downloading Legends & Letters worth it?
The prizes that can be earned from Legends & Letters are all No-Trade (with the exception of Pirate Paint Brush), so it is largely dependent on whether you personally want any of these items, as you can only obtain them by playing the game yourself. You can also win trophies and an avatar.

As of July 22, 2020, TNT announced that Legends & Letters will be discontinued, and the app was removed from app stores. If you have downloaded the game before its retirement, you can still play the game until December 31, 2020. The Crossover Challenges have been discontinued, but all in-app purchases are now free.


▸ How do I earn prizes from Legends & Letters?
Prizes are not available all the time in Legends & Letters. Rather, a "Crossover Week" is held every 4 weeks, during which completing the daily Challenge of Challenges content will award you chests that can be opened for a random exclusive item. You will also receive the avatar for participating, as well as the trophies depending on how many challenges you completed.

There are no on-site prizes for playing Legends & Letters when it is not Crossover Week.


▸ I'm locked out! Help!
The Legends & Letters servers are plagued by bouts of instability and high latency. If you are unable to log in, it could be the fault of the servers. Check in with other players to see if they are experiencing the same issue. If so, it will eventually pass. If you are unable to log in even when the servers are fine, consider reinstalling the app or sending in a ticket to the official FAQ and remember to provide both your Legends & Letters UN and Neopets UN to the support staff.


▸ I don't see Legends & Letters available for me to download. Do you have any idea?
Before the game's discontinuation, the game was not available for download in Belgium and the Netherlands due to some country specific anti-loot box laws.


▸ Did TNT ever release the 10th Crossover Week trophies?
TNT have not released the trophies nor acknowledged this issue. They have stated that after the game's discontinuation, bug fixes and technical support will no longer be provided for the game.


▸ Is there anything else I need to know about Legends & Letters?
The game is essentially dead and there are no active on-site rewards for the game. If you just want to play the game for fun, then there's no one stopping you from doing so.

Island Builders Related

▸ What is Neopets: Island Builders?
Neopets: Island Builders is Neopets's fourth mobile app game. It is a 3D Construction Simulation game and your job is to rebuild the destroyed island civilization of Dacardia. The game is currently in open beta for Android and closed beta for iOS. For information on how to download and play the game, I would read over Jellyneo's on-going article:

Jellyneo's Neopets: Island Builders Guide
jellyneo.net/?go=island_builders


▸ Is downloading Neopets: Island Builders worth it?
As of it's launch, you cannot earn NP nor obtain any tradable items on-site, so not really unless you want the three No-Trade items. That information can be found in this Jellyneo Article:

Jellyneo's Neopets: Island Account Linking Article
jellyneo.net/?go=island_builders&id=account_linking


▸ Do I expand my island towards the giant jungle waterfall first or the purple space mountain?
It is recommended that you expand your island towards the Mystic Jungle first over the Crystal Plateau. This is because the Mystic Jungle Route has the following:

- An increased amount of Core Buildings for faster Town Leveling.
- Quests and Gathering items are more quickly obtainable.
- An increased pet amount.
- The Crystal Plateau items are generally more difficult to come by.
- Jungle Route has Active Quest sequence that also unlocks an amenity building sooner.


▸ Are pet elements and ideals randomized? Is there any way I can get a specific pet element/ideal combination?
Yes, pet elements and ideals randomized, and no, there is currently no way how to get a specific pet element/ideal combination.


▸ What's the most efficient way to gather Power Neggs?
Here is a quick list of ways you can efficiently gather Power Neggs:

- Turn in items that can gathered quickly en masse such as Rocks, Pirate Daggers, Magnets, and Echo to the Power Plant.
- Complete Quests (namely Pet Quests)


▸ What's the most efficient way to gather Building Materials?
Here is a quick list of way you can efficiently gather Building Materials:

- Turn in items that can gathered quickly en masse such as Bamboo, Straw, Rocks, and Spyder Webs to the Molten Mixer.
- Complete Quests (namely Pet Quests)


▸ What's the most efficient way to increase my Town Level?
The most efficent way how to increase your Town Level is by leveling up your Core Buildings. The higher the level of the core building, the more exp gained, so instead of raising 3 different buildings all to level 4, focus on getting one up to max level.

You can also increase your Town experience by placing decorations on your island (the larger and/or more recipe complex the decorations are, the more EXP you earn), but in addition, do note that removing decorations from your island decreases your Town experience.

Also, completing the Active Quests from the storyline awards Town experience.


▸ What's the giant egg in the Crystal Plateu for?
The giant egg in the Crystal Plateu is just an immovable decoration.


▸ Why isn't the Trading Post working?
The Trading Post is broken on Android and has been temporarily disabled for iOS. When functional, the Trading Post would be a way for players to trade their items for other items within the game. Players were encouraged to use the Trading Post when they needed items from their opposing expansion route (Mystic Jungle/Crystal Plateau).


▸ Does upgrading my Core Buildings do anything?
Upgrading your Core Buildings can give you Town Level experience, but aside from that, it just sits there and look pretty.


▸ Why do I keep getting these constant tutorial/error messages?
The error messages are most occurring when you're crafting/gathering items too quickly, but you shouldn't be in any trouble for that. You'll have a certain amount of items taken away and returned, but you can still create/gather said items afterward. This also appears when you're putting ingredients in the Molten Mixer too quickly. You would want to click one item and do a full slow one-count before clicking anything again.

The constant tutorial pop-ups is a known problem, and it is presumed to be worked on.


▸ Is the Premium Emporium/Crystal Negg Store worth investing money in?
Personally, I would say no, since the game is not exactly functional for In-Game Purchases just yet. It is a personal and financial choice if you do wish to purchase an extra pet (Kacheek, but only available for a limited time at the beginning of your playthrough) and additional decorative items.

You can steadily obtain Crystal Neggs from the Wheel of Offers and Level 3 Daily Goals.


▸ How do I raise happiness?
You can raise your pet's and overall island happiness by doing any of the following:

- Eating Omelettes
- Visiting an Amenity Building
- Painting your Neopet (not recommended)
- Customizing your Neopet (not recommended)

Also if your pet levels up it's Affinity then happiness and hunger restored to 100%.

NOTE: Paint Brushes and wearables are Single Use. Blank Paint Brush, Blank Roller, Basic Hat are not craftable and at the time only obtainable through the Wheel of Offers for iOS. For Android, Blank Paint Brush, Blank Roller, Basic Hat can be obtained in the Premium Emporium.


▸ How do I craft X item in Island Builders?
I would check out Jellyneo's guide for a crowdsourced compiled list of items that can be crafted in the game.

In the crafting buildings, you can mix and match new craftable items through the Discovery Item section with the except for the Omelette Slab and Workshop. For the Workshop, the equipment cannot be unlocked early, and you can only obtain them through Active Quests. For the Omelette Slab, you will have to match ingredients every time you want to create/discover a specific omelette. For all failed attempts at the Omelette Slab, items will not be returned and your creation will always result in a Dubious Omelette.

Jellyneo's Neopets: Island Builders Crafting Guides
jellyneo.net/?go=island_builders&id=crafting


▸ Isn't there an avatar for this game?
An avatar for Neopets: Island Builders has been discovered, but the avatar is not currently active, but will most likely be made available in the future.


▸ Is there anything else I need to know about Neopets: Island Builders?
If you have any questions not mentioned here about Neopets: Island Builders, I would refer to the following resources. If the question was not found/answered there, then I would ask any of the following NeoBoard Chats lists below:

Neopets Community Areas
- /~Melandros (Melandros' Random Info about Island Builders)
- Site Events NeoBoard Chat
- Help NeoBoard Chat

Mobile Other Related

▸ Is KeyQuest returning as a mobile app?
The latest word from TNT (Dec 3, 2019) is that there are no plans to bring back KeyQuest, as they are focusing all resources on conversion of Flash content.


▸ What is this Neopets X?
Neopets X was the codename for Neopets: Island Builders. It was unveiled at Comic-Con 2018, and a demo was made playable for attendees at Comic-Con 2019.

Help / Support FAQs

▸ Where can I get a quick question answered about anything related to Neopets?
You would want to visit the Help NeoBoard Chat for your Neopets query.

Ticket Help Related

▸ Where and how do I make a ticket?
You would want to send a ticket through the official FAQ. It is best to write these tickets in a professional matter.
- Make your subject title short and sweet.
- Always remember to include your UN.
- State what you want right away. If this is an account retrieval, then I'd suggest searching for the account recovery question below.
- Avoid humor and emotions. A bit is fine, but you really don't want to go overboard with them.
- Review for ambiguity and make sure your email is clear and free of any spelling mistakes.

You will be given a ticket number and the response time varies between 2 hours to 2 months on average.


▸ How can I get TNT to reply to my ticket faster?
You would want to do the following if you haven't already:
- Post your ticket number on the Highway to Help thread in the Help NeoBoard Chat.
- Post your ticket number on their Social Media pages.
- Update and promptly respond to your ticket reply (if applicable).

If you haven't received your first reply at all after a month, then I would send in another ticket.


▸ What is the Highway to Help thread?
The Highway to Help thread (or Ticket Waiting Board) is a place where players can post their ticket numbers for a Neopets staff member to assign to the next available representative within a timely matter.

You would always want to read the first post of these threads and also take a look over at the following petpage for posting etiquette.
HIGHWAY TO HELP
/~Kaizsa


▸ I have a content suggestion to make for TNT. Would it be better to ask in the editorial or support?
TNT will take suggestions through both the Editorial and their support address at the official FAQ. You can also try posting your idea on the Ideas / Suggestions NeoBoard Chat.


▸ Can I report a person through tickets?
Yes, you can send a report through a support ticket, although it is preferred that you send a report through the Report Abuse page.


▸ Can I send a bug report through tickets?
Yes, you can send bug reports through a support ticket. You can also send reports through the Editorial.


▸ Can I ask others to post my ticket number on the Highway to Help thread or share my number when they get answered by TNT Support?
You are NOT allowed to share or post someone else's ticket number. Not only is this a safety concern, but you would be held accountable for unintentionally supporting any malicious intent or activity the user might have committed.

If you happen to be unable to access your account to post on the thread, you are allowed to make a temporary side account to post on the thread until you regain your old account.


▸ I've heard people request a specific support staff member over another for better ticket help. Does that work?
I would say this varies on the situation, but this is often brought up when people are wanting to recover their accounts. People would often ask for Alice W. over Rico S., Tony P., or Delilah D. as it is believed she is more responsive than the others. There are occasions where the ticket information of the assigned tickets are already shared with the other support staff members.

Account Related

▸ My account got disabled/frozen? How come?
An account can be frozen for a variety of reasons, the most common being violations of the Terms of Use/site rules and guidelines, or for protection if your account was compromised. You are advised to send a ticket to support staff to inquire about the freeze as well as any possible steps you can take to recover the account. If the account has not been used in a long time, there is also a possibility it has been purged. For more information, I would check out the following page:
Jellyneo's Frozen Accounts Article
jellyneo.net/?go=frozen_accounts


▸ How can I recover my old account?
Send in a ticket to support staff. Remember to provide as much information as you can about the account, from basics such as UN and email to even minute details such as who your Neofriends were. The more information you have, the more likely it is that support will believe you were the original owner of the account. If you are having trouble remembering, you can also request support to give you hints.

Note that if the account has not been used in a long time, there is also a possibility it has been purged and cannot be recovered. You can verify if an account has been purged by visiting its user lookup, purged accounts will state that no such user exists. For more information, check /~Wispalings and /~sarika_ambrielle.


▸ I tried resetting my password, but it didn't work. What happened?
Be sure to check your spam folder and verify you are using the correct email address. You can view your account's associated email address here.

Note that addresses from Hotmail, AOL, or Yahoo have a tendency to be deleted/deactivated due to inactivity. If all else fails, you can always try to send a ticket at the official FAQ for assistance, including for changing your email address if necessary.


▸ I forgot my PIN number. What can I do?
You can retrieve your PIN via email on your PIN preferences page. If this doesn't work or you are encountering problems with your email address (see previous question), you can always send in a ticket to support staff at the official FAQ for assistance.


▸ I'm trying to change my E-Mail, but it looks like a bunch of scrambled nonsense. Why is that?
Due to privacy laws, TNT did not store your email information if you registered your account when you were less than 13 years old. Id est, that information has been lost and you are advised to send in a ticket to support staff for assistance.


▸ Do I need to contact TNT if I transfer mains? Also, do I need to contact them if I close an account?
You do not need to contact TNT if you wish to transfer mains or when you are planning to close an account.


▸ Is there anything else I need to know about Account Related Tickets?
If you are looking for help on how to make a ticket, then feel free to ask for support in the Help NeoBoard Chat. Just remember to not mention any personal identifying information before publicly sharing.

Also, the process of reclaiming an account can be a long and hard experience. You are not guaranteed to get your account back even after providing the necessary information, picking a specific support staff member, etc. but it doesn't hurt to rebuild a new main account.

Special thanks and FAQ contributions here from riparu (Everything).

Premium Membership FAQs

▸ Is Neopets Premium worth it?
This depends on how you regularly play Neopets to determine how your experience would be like. Here's a quick questionnaire on the main Premium Features:
- Are you comfortable with giving Neopets real-money?
- Do you want an additional pet slot?
- Do you want to see the lowest Shop Wizard prices instantly on demand?
- Do you like fighting in the Battledome for daily rewards and want to win Nerkmids?
- Do you have a converted dream pet, that's not a Draik/Krawk, but might be the rare Ice Bori?
- Do you play the Flash Games for Neopoints often?

If you answered yes to most of these questions, then yes, Neopets Premium might be worth it to you!

- Neopets Premium is a paid service.
- Neopets Premium will grant you an additional pet slot.
- Super Shop Wizard (SSW) will allow you to search for the lowest Shop Wizard prices within an instant.
- If you win a battle in the Cosmic Dome, you might be awarded with Nerkmids.
- The Free Species Change perk allows you to morph a pet into any converted colored species (including Ice Bori), except Draik or Krawk, you want every 365 days. Just remember to have a proper set up before using the perk.
- The Space Faerie Charm will sometimes double your NP winnings from Flash Games.


▸ Wait aren't there more Premium features than that?
Yep, there are more Premium features! Here's a list of them:
- No Advertis.ements.
- Premium Toolbar (shows SSW, Premium exclusive Featured Game, custom Dailies, Bankroll, and other perks).
- Premium Neoboards (often referred as Charter).
- Premium Avatar and Site Theme.
- Space Faerie Charm on your userlookup (and also sometimes double your NP winnings from Flash Games).
- Premium Collectible Cards.
- Premium Random Events (common Random Event that gives away 1k-3k NP or a r1-r70 item).
- Space Faerie Scratchcards (and access to the Space Faerie Vending Machine).
- Extra Gallery Categories.
- Customisation Journal (stays after your Premium ends).
- Space Faerie Quests.
- Premium Bonus Neocash Collectibles.
- Additional Premium Battleground of the Obelisk Boons.
- Free Swashbuckling Academy Training on your pet's Birthday.

Premium Basics Related

▸ Where can I purchase Premium Membership?
You can purchase Neopets Premium under the Premium bar marked Become a Member.


▸ Where can I cancel my Premium Membership?
You can cancel Neopets Premium under the Premium bar marked Manage Membership.

You will be able to continue using your Premium features until the time you paid for Premium is over. Once it is time, you will return to being a regular Neopets member and you will no longer be able to access or be given the following:

- Premium Featured Game
- Space Faerie Scratchcards
- The "Space Faerie" avatar
- The 7th Pet Slot
- The Monthly Premium Collectible
- The Premium Boards
- The Premium Cards section of the Neodeck
- The Super Shop Wizard
- Your Space Faerie Charm

The Premium Site Theme will stay if you happen to have it on prior to cancellation, but it will not be an available option if you decide to change the theme. If you quit Premium and then re-subscribe later, any perks that you've previously gained, such as your Premium Neodeck cards, will automatically reappear.

In the event you are unable to access your account and you continue to be charged for Premium, then I'd suggest sending a ticket to TNT at the official FAQ in order to get the problem resolved.


▸ Does Premium Membership ever go on sale?
Neopets Premium does go on sale every year around the Fall season. This sale only applies to the Yearly plan at $20 USD off the original price ($69.95 to $49.95). The discount is only accepted in full payment upon purchase and the sale tends to last about a month.

Before you decide to purchase the discounted price, think to yourself if you can commit to a whole year of playing Neopets in order to make the most out of this deal.


▸ Can I purchase Premium on side accounts?
You are NOT allowed to purchase Premium on your side accounts.


▸ How long does it take for Premium Membership to appear on my account?
Premium Membership usually takes a few minutes to launch. I would send a ticket if it has been over 12 hours.


▸ Are Beauty Contest submissions allowed in Charter?
You are allowed to create a thread about your Beauty Contest submissions on the Premium NeoBoard / Charter Chat. This NeoBoard Chat follows the same rules as the Art NeoBoard Chat.

Premium Perks Related

▸ I heard I can get any colored species with Premium. Is that true?
Premium members are given the Free Species Change perk which does allow you technically obtain nearly every color of converted species (Draiks and Krawks are excluded from this, but the exclusive Ice Bori is possible).

How the perk works is that the pet will change its species while keeping its original color. If the species does not come in said color, then you will be given a drop down of all the colors to choose from for that new species! (Example: Lemon Chia to Lutari, but Lemon Lutari do not exist in the Rainbow Pool, so you can choose any possible Lutari color). This perk is the reason why most Chia Morphing Potions and Magical Chia Pops are pricey.

Do know that Orange Chias will make the impending species into the color Orange if that is a possible combination. You can check what colors a species does not come in from the link below:

SunnyNeo's Rainbow Pool Guide
sunnyneo.com/rainbowpool.php


▸ Does the Free Species Change perk work on Unconverted Pets? Can I get Unconverted Pets from it?
The Free Species Change perk does work on Unconverted Pets, but it will convert the pet. You cannot get Unconverted Pets from the perk.


▸ What is the difference between the Shop Wizard and the Super Shop Wizard?
Regular Shop Wizard:
- Randomly searches through many groups of shops depending on the usershop's UN.
- No definite indicator that the item is not for sale in any usershop.
- The Search Limit is 360 searches per each new hour.
- You can search for any Non-Neocash item.

Super Shop Wizard:
- Will give you the usershops with the lowest prices instantly on demand.
- Will tell you if the item is not for sale in any usershop.
- The Search Limit is about less than 75-100 searches per each new hour.
- You are not allowed to directly search for most of the following: Lab Map Pieces, Nerkmids, Paint Brushes, Petpet Lab Map Pieces, Petpet Paint Brushes, and Transmogrification Potions (newer PBs/PPBs/Transmogs are allowed, however).
- You are given the Price Only (limited) option that will allow you to search for any Non-Neocash item, but it will not tell you which usershop.
- The ability to search with wildcard operators (%) to randomize your searches.

Both:
- Frozen Shops can appear.
- Gallery search functions are the same.
- Petpet Park items can be found.

Jellyneo's Shop Wizard Guide
jellyneo.net/?go=shopwiz


▸ Why can't I SSW search Nerkmids, Paint Brushes, etc.?
This was assumingly implemented to avoid a lot of economical issues back then, because those items were and still are infamously sought out due to their relation to Trophies, avatars, customization, etc.


▸ What is SSW Sniping?
SSW Sniping is when Premium members use the Super Shop Wizard to look out for higher priced items at a (sometimes accidental, sometimes intentionally marked) low price. Most people would use Jellyneo's IDB as a start, but there is a special trick to Super Shop Wizard of using wildcard operators (%) in your search. It'll allow you to easily look around for certain items like specially colored Morphing Potions (Example: COLOR % Morphing Potion). There is usually a thread in the Charter Chat where people share their SSW Snipe findings.


▸ Let's say I'm currently using my extra pet slot and my Premium ends, what happens?
You'll be given a grace period to purchase pet slots (if applicable), or transfer out or abandon a selected pet if you hit your maximum amount (the default is 10 pets without any additional pet slots). If you choose to abandon a pet, it will be stuck in Pound Limbo for 90 days where only you can see it. After 90 days have passed, the pet will be available for anyone to adopt (if you have not made a decision in those 90 days, then a random pet will be selected to be abandoned to the pound).

If you abandon a Lutari, you will not be able to re-adopt the pet back.


▸ So, when do I get my Monthly Premium Bonus Collectibles?
A new Monthly Premium Bonus Collectible is given out on the 15th of every month. If you happen to sign up for Premium prior the 15th, you would be given the latest collectible.


▸ Why didn't I get a new Space Faerie Scratchcard?
Every Friday, Premium members are given one Space Faerie Scratchcard. You have to be subscribed to Premium for at least a week in order to get your first Space Faerie Scratchcard.


▸ When is the best time to scratch Space Faerie Scratchcards?
The best time to scratch Space Faerie Scratchcards is when you have the Full Pockets Obelisk Boon.

The boon gives you a boosted amount of Neopoints with every win. You 1,000 NP with every item reward.


▸ What is the Space Faerie Vending Machine? Am I missing out on anything there?
The Space Faerie Vending Machine is a Premium exclusive feature where users can use their Mysterious Tokens, won from the Faerie Scratchcards, to win items such Codestones, Dubloons, etc. Mysterious Tokens are extremely rare and you're not missing much. You can check out the prizes here:

Jellyneo's Space Faerie Vending Machine Guide
jellyneo.net/?go=space_faerie_vending_machine


▸ How strong do I have to be to beat Jetsam Ace and/or Giant Space Fungus?
Who you want to fight depends on your pet's stats, budget, and your own personal stance on where or if you want to stop at a certain point of fighting a specific opponent.

Jetsam Ace on Easy Difficulty is recommended to be fought at Level 50 and 55 STR in order to OHKO him. You can fight him at a STR and Level lower than that, but you would at least want to be at 35 STR and with a similar Defense and/or high HP to make up for it. If you want to fight him at a higher difficulty, then I would recommend training your STR to 85 for Medium and then 125 (200 STR to always OHKO) for Mighty.

In order to OHKO Giant Space Fungus on Mighty Difficulty (Medium/Hard mode Jetsam Ace has higher rarity rewards than Easy/Medium Giant Space Fungus) for his Bubbling Fungus rewards, then it is reasonably affordable, albeit more tedious, to fight him at Level 200 and 400 STR in order to 3HKO him. You would need to be at 750+ STR and have a weapon budget of ~20m if you wanted to OHKO him.


▸ Is there anything special about Premium Cards?
Premium Cards are really just nice collectibles that you get every month. They disappear once your Premium ends, but they do reappear once you subscribe again.


▸ What's the Customisation Journal good for?
The Customisation Journal is really just a place sharing customizations you have made on-site through a catalog. Viewers can check out what items were put on the pet at the time and give "Likes" on your entries. You may make up to 6 entries per day. Also, you get to keep your journal once your Premium ends although you won't be able to add/edit entries.

As a more practical option for sharing customizations, Dress to Impress and Jellyneo's Wardrobe do have a feature for sharing customizions more easily and quickly than the Customisation Journal. It does not require Premium either.


▸ What's special about the Premium Neoboards?
They are really just an extra side chat where users can talk about pretty much anything like Beauty Contest, Caption Contest, etc. NP Trades, NC Trades, Pet Trades, and more can also be found here.


▸ Is there anything else I need to know about Premium Membership?
If you have any questions about Neopets Premium, don't hesistate to ask the Help NeoBoard Chat or Premium NeoBoard Chat (Premium only) for help with your queries!

NC Mall FAQs

▸ What is Neocash?
Neocash (NC) is a Neopian currency with which you can use to acquire an assortment of wearables, site boons, etc. in exchange for real-money. You can use Neocash to purchase NC items from the NC Mall.


▸ Do I need Neocash to enjoy the game?
Neocash is completely optional and not necessary for average gameplay.

Neocash Basics Related

▸ How does one obtain Neocash?
You can purchase Neocash from the following:
- On-site over here.
- NC Cards over here.

You can obtain Neocash/NC items from the following reoccurring dailies/Events:
- Advent Calendar
- Altador Cup
- Charity Corner
- Daily Dare (prior 2012)
- The Money Tree
- NC Mall Birthday / Neopets Birthday / Valentines / Halloween / Christmas Freebies
- Space Faerie Scratchcards (Premium Only)


▸ How long does it take for Neocash to appear on my account?
If you are purchasing Neocash directly from the site, the estimated time is 2 minutes to 2 months, and longer if done with PP. Neocash Cards are usually instant and they have more incentives, such as additional Neocash and Gift Boxes, than buying on-site.

You might want to submit a ticket to TNT at the official FAQ if you have not received your NC within a week.


▸ Am I allowed to purchase Neocash on my side accounts?
You are allowed to purchase Neocash on your side acconuts.


▸ Is there a certain time when new NC items are released?
New Neocash content tends to be released around 10am - Noon NST on the weekdays and sometimes through Future Fashions. Event NC items are usually released before or around the same time the NC Event is launched.


▸ What is Future Fashions?
Future Fashions is a special NC Mall shop for players that have spent 10,000 NC ($100 USD) in the prior month. Future Fashion items are moved to the public NC Mall after 72 hours (3 days) of their initial release.


▸ What does this acronym/phrase mean in the NC Mall Chat?
I'd check out /~Xheoi for a more current list of NC Mall related acronyms and phrases. For general terminology, you could check out Jellyneo's Dictionary.


▸ What do Noda's Fortune Cookies do?
Noda's Fortune Cookies are special NC consumables that can give you site boons, wearables, and other fun activities to do on the site! All Fortune Cookies have a limited amount of stock, but you only really see Faerie Quest Fortune Cookies getting sold out during the Faerie Quest Event, because they're 50% off during that time.

​ SunnyNeo's Noda's Fortune Cookies Guide
sunnyneo.com/customisation/ncmall/NCfortunecookies.php

Jellyneo's Noda's Fortune Cookies Guide
jellyneo.net/?go=fortunecookies


▸ How do I get rid of Neocash items?
You can do either of the following:
- Gift them out to other members using Gift Boxes
- Donate them with Upcycle Cookies (Upcycled items will turn into a cheap buyable in the Money Tree)
- Do Kaia Quests (requires NC)
- Charity Corner them (requires NC)
- Discard them directly through the item's page


▸ How do I delete Basic Gift Boxes?
You can delete Basic Gift Boxes through any of the following:
- Use them to gift/trade NC items to others.
- Send yourself a random NC item.
- Do Kaia Quests (requires NC).


▸ What is the Elite Boutique?
The Elite Boutique is a special NC Mall shop reserved for member's accounts that are 49 months old (4+ years). This shop can be found in the top right corner of the NC Mall page with the star icon. All the items in this shop are No-Trade. TNT has not released any new items nor retired anything from this shop for about a decade.

NC Trading Related

▸ How does one trade Neocash items?
I would check out /~Helper for how to start out NC Trading! The basics of NC Trading are as follows:
- You are trading with another Neopets player.
- You are only allowed to trade NC Items for other NC Items.
- You are both using Gift Boxes in order to send the NC Items.
- Most, but not all, trades usually reference item values of the NC Items.
- All trades are built on trust from both sides to deliver the items to their destined accounts.


▸ I just did a trade, but who accepts their side first?
There's no rule on who should accept first, but it is courteous to accept when both sides have exchanged their sent item messages. The general etiquette about accepting first:
- You want to make sure the other side got their items (big trades, Neomail error, etc.).
- A side is boxless and has to open the, presumably traded, Gift Box Capsules in order to trade.
- A side might about to log off for a long period of time and won't be able to accept their side of trade immediately.

NOTE: It's generally advisable to copy and paste the confirmation message you get from sending the item (add x2 or x3 if you're sending multiple) as an extra layer of verification that you completed your half of the trade. E.g. Congratulations! Your gift has been delivered to UN. You will receive a Neomail updating you on the status of your gift within 48 hours. Thank you.


▸ What happens when I send the NC item to the wrong account? Will I get my Gift Box back?
You would want to NM the account you sent the item to immediately (if you can recall the UN) and see if they will return the item to you (most people will). When the NC item is rejected, you will get the item and gift box back.

In the past, if you have sent an NC item to the wrong account, it would have been returned back to you in 48 hours if no action was taken. The feature is now broken and you'll need to send in a ticket if you want the item back if the account looks to be inactive.


▸ What is a Gift Box Capsule/Cube?
Gift Box Capsules/Cubes (or GBCs) are the item currency of NC Trading. They are mystery capsules that are commonly opened for the 2 to 5 Gift Boxes inside (the 5th Gift Box being a Limited Edition Gift Box). They cost 200 NC and can also award a random item (or two if the GBC has 5 Gift Boxes) in the NC Mall worth around 150 NC.

Gift Box Capsules are usually sold towards the end of each month and very rarely appear in Future Fashions nowadays. They are discounted to 25%-50% off during Black Friday and the Spring Cleaning Sale.

Prior May 2014, Gift Box Capsules used to have a more cylindrical shape and awarded items differently in comparison to the newer cubic variants. They awarded 1 to 5 Gift Boxes (the 5th Gift Box being a Limited Edition Gift Box) and the random NC Mall item (or two) was worth around 200 NC. The cylinder shaped capsules were the same price of 200 NC.


▸ How does one get more Basic Gift Boxes?
You can get more Gift Boxes by doing any of the following:
- Open Gift Box Capsules
- Redeem NC Cards
- Trudy's Surprise (on your main account only)

Unfortunately, you cannot put a Basic (or special) Gift Box inside a Basic (or special) Gift Box.


▸ What is a Value Check thread?
A Value Check (or VC) thread is a thread on the NC Mall NeoBoard where you are asking people what they have traded recently for a certain item, or have seen an item trade for recently. It is one of the best ways to keep yourself safe and up-to-date while trading.


▸ What does 2:1 mean?
2:1 usually refers to a type of "sale" where someone offers two of their items for one Gift Box capsule, Archive Cookie, or other item. Not all traders would have a 2:1 sale and some might do 3:2 (three items for two GBCs), so as to ensure they will have 1 Basic Gift Box after the trade.


▸ Where would I go to find Neocash Trades?
You can find Neocash Trades mainly at the following:
- NC Mall NeoBoard Chat
- Dress to Impress (via Neomails)
- Jellyneo's Item Database (via Neomails)

If you are new/returning to NC Trading, then the safest place to conduct NC trades is through the NeoBoards.


▸ How do I set up a tradelist/wishlist?
I would check out /~Helper again! Tradelists/Wishlist are not necessary for NC Trading, but it is preferred to have one if you are going to be trading NC items every now and then.


▸ Which place is the best to make a tradelist? DTI, JN, Gallery, Petpage, NC Album, etc.?
DTI and/or JN are a great start to making a tradelist for NC Trading!

Dress to Impress (DTI):
- Most preferred place to start an NC Tradelist/Wishlist.
- Simplistic user interface.
- Fluid List Comparison Tool.
- Items can be easily removed from Tradelist.
- You can import items from your Closet/SDB.
- You can export items from your petpages.
- You can add a description to each DTI section.
- Tradelist/Wishlist are shared with a DTI URL.
- Up For Trade/Seeking sections are only indicated by those who have set their sections to "Trading" status.
- Up For Trade/Seeking placing is based on when you added the item to your list.
- Non-Wearables cannot be listed.
- You cannot assign values to the NC items, unlike Jellyneo.

Jellyneo (JN):
- Find Trade feature to instantly compare user's list.
- Top Priority Feature above regular items.
- You can assign values to the NC items.
- Non-Wearables can be listed.
- Has an automatic Last Updated text.
- Up For Trade/Seeking placing is based on when you last updated the section (added/removed an item).
- You can import items from your Closet/SDB.
- You can export items from your petpages.
- Tradelist/Wishlist are shared with a JN URL.
- The List Comparison Tool is clunky.
- No description space.
- Keeping tradelists/wishlists updated is more difficult than DTI.
- Unfavorable user interface for a number of NC traders.

Petpages:
- No linking offsite.
- You can personalize with your own layouts and whatnot.
- Constant multi-page updating.
- Image/Name Filters.
- No special DTI/JN features.
- Longer Loading Times.
- Possible account security issues with shady Neopians.

Galleries:
- No linking offsite.
- Easy to maintain.
- You can personalize with your own layouts and whatnot.
- No special DTI/JN features.
- Constant multi-page updating.
- Image/Name Filters
- Longer Loading Times.
- Possible account security issues with shady Neopians.
- Gallery Size can be expensive.

NC Albums:
- No, just don't.


▸ Why can't I link my DTI/JN URL?
You might want to remove some parts of the URL:
- The starting https://www. part needs to be taken out.
- Long DTI UNs might need to be removed or be broken into parts.
- JN TL URLs might sometimes be weird for NM trades if you end with the URL. Just link it in the top or middle of your post (just put any text after the JN TL URL).


▸ How long does one usually wait for the other person to respond back?
You would usually want to wait 24-48 hours for them to respond back to an NC trade or Dyework Lend. We all can't be on Neopets 24/7 and sudden events in real life might need our priority at the moment.


▸ Are Neomail Neocash trades safe?
Neomail Neocash trades are generally safe if you are an experienced NC trader. They are useful for making possible quick trades, finding trades over from DTI/Jellyneo, and for general convenience!

For new or returning NC traders, it is recommended that you trade through the NeoBoards as it is easy to be scammed through Neomail trading. You should always create a Value Check thread if you are unsure of the fairness of a trade.


▸ What are these Neocash Shuffle threads?
A Neocash/NC Mall Shuffle is NC Mall Chat game in where members list their NC Items/Custom for random offers by anyone for fun! Just do know that there's a risk to the listers on the inevitable aspect of accepting trades and those trades won't always go well.

As this is a Neopets Trading game, Neocash items will be traded for other Neocash items. Pets/Neopoints/NP Items are NOT to be involved in these trades. More information can be found in the following petpage:

NC Shuffle Rules and Guidelines
/~Puvs


▸ What is a Popular?
Populars (or Pops) are highly sought out NC wearables due to their well-liked appearance. These NC wearables can be difficult to trade for, have fluctuating values, and/or are generally known by seasoned NC traders. Trade carefully if you do have these items and as a quick reference, the following petpage should entail most notable wearables:

Popular/Notable NC Wearable Petpages
/~Sovenn (Retired Popular Wearable Trade Database)
/~Pythonics (Retired Notable Wearable Visual Guide)

NC Rules Related

▸ Am I allowed to open Neocash Cookies on side accounts?
You are allowed to open certain Fortune Cookies, but NOT all on your side accounts.

ALLOWED
NOT ALLOWED
Archives
Coincidental
Lab Ray*
Faerie Quest
Specialty Wearable
Games
Training
Upcycle
Wild Card

*You are NOT allowed to use Lab Ray Fortune Cookies on your side accounts UNLESS that one side account is your only Lab Ray account (even if you have access to the Lab Ray on your main and/or other accounts, you would only be allowed to use the Lab Ray Fortune Cookies on your main account if that was the case).

For further information, CTRL-F the following phrase:
Am I allowed to open Fortune Cookies on side accounts?


▸ Am I allowed to trade Neocash items from my side accounts?
You are allowed to trade Neocash items from your side accounts although do be careful and make sure that you are actually trading with the same person. Shell accounts have been found to steal NC items from poofy NC traders.


▸ Am I allowed to trade Neocash items for things other than Neocash items?
You are NOT allowed to trade NC items for things other than NC items. Only NC items for NC items is allowed.

Neopets Editorial - Issue 438 | Question 4 [link]

First of all, I would like to thank you guys for letting us trade Neocash items. That said, I was wondering if we could trade Neocash items for Neopoint items as long as both parties agreed? For example, say someone wants one of my Neocash items that I have up for trade, but they don't have a Neocash item to exchange for it. They do have a Neopoint item to trade, though. As long as that person agrees and doesn't feel scammed in any way, could we do this? ~chuppacabrashelper

No. Even if both parties agree, trading Neocash items for Neopoint ones (and vice versa) is not allowed. These are two separate economies and they are not allowed to intermingle as it would terribly unbalance both economies and become greatly unfair to players who choose not to use the NC Mall.


▸ Am I allowed to participate in NC events on my side accounts?
Nowadays, you are allowed to participate in pretty much all NC events on your side accounts. Always double check with the FAQ of the aforementioned event if you're really unsure.


▸ Am I allowed to gift/giveaway/contest off Neocash items?
You are allowed to gift NC items, but TNT have stated that giveaway threads varies on the degree of subjectivity.

Neopets Editorial - Issue 779 | Question 4 [link]

I recently put up a gifting board for NC items I no longer use. I've done this several times before. This time though, I suppose someone reported it and when I got up the next day I found a "gentle reminder" from TNT telling me such boards were not permitted. The board was gone. I was simply trying to help fellow Neopians. I looked up some old editorials and it did say they are NOT permitted because it encourages begging. OK. So yesterday, someone else did the same thing and nothing happens to them. Board is still and I know a few people reported it.

I'm so sorry that happened! However, it's definitely not a black and white issue, it is pretty much up to the monitors discretion whether a board is crossing the line. Advice for the future, try to keep everything as much within the rules as you can.

-----

Neopets Editorial - Issue 752 | Question 3 [link]

Just wondering if we are allowed to do NC/NP item giveaways. It's our choice and our (real life) money. Can TNT tell us what we can do with it? ~ psychoan.alysis

You're right - your items and money, you can do what you want with them and give them to whomever you'd like. What you can't do is openly advertise that you're giving away items, as it invites begging, which is not allowed :)

You are allowed and only permitted to host contest off NC items through Guilds activities and within your guildmates.

- Neopets Editorial - Issue 897 | Question 1 [link] (You are NOT allowed to participate in Guild Contests that can award you with NP/items)
- Neopets Editorial - Issue 843 | Announcement 1 [link] (Guild Contest are now OK)


▸ Is there anything else I need to know about the rules of Neocash?
If you are ever unsure if something is allowed/disallowed in terms of Neocash related topics, then it doesn't hurt to ask the NC Mall NeoBoard Chat, Help NeoBoard Chat, or Charter NeoBoard Chat (Premium Only). Neocash is real money, so you will definitely find someone that is knowledgable about the rules and regulations of Neocash.

jellyneo.net/?go=nc_mall&page=events
