▸ Are there any NC events that are NOT optional to the main event?
Nope! All NC events are optional and have no impact on any progress in any main Neopets event.


▸ What and when is the Super Sale?
The NC Mall Super Sale is an annual NC Mall event that occurs during the weekends of January. The NC Mall will discount all the wearables of a specified category (usually Backgrounds, Clothes, and Trinkets) by 50% off and release three new wearables in that same category. These sales only last the weekend.


▸ Didn't Super Sale use to be something completely different?
That is correct! Super Sales used to be large NC events where TNT would retire tons of previously "permanent" NC Mall buyables at a discounted price. This was to make room for new "permanent" NC Mall buyables and the discounted ones would soon be retired for good. It wasn't just limited to separate wearables, but these sales contained Superpacks, Specialty Capsules, Neohome items, and more! This style of Super Sales ended somewhere around 2013 along with its mass introduction and discounted retirement of NC wearables. You can read more about old Super Sales here:

Super Saled: The Super Sale FAQ
/~Fibbyck


▸ What are NC Grams?
NC Grams are gift-giving items with NC wearables inside. These grams contain 4-7 (usually 5) wearables with a chance of a Limited Edition item inside. As these are gift-giving items, you do not need to use a Gift Box to send these away! These are usually sold around Valentine's Day (with some seasonal releases) and they each cost 200 NC.

Jellyneo's and SunnyNeo's NC Grams Articles
jellyneo.net/?go=sweetheart_gram
sunnyneo.com/customisation/NCgrams.php


▸ Would I have to buy an NC Gram on a side account or trade with someone if I want the NC Gram item on my main account?
Luckily, you can send NC Grams to yourself.


▸ How do I check if my NC Gram has the Limited Edition item?
You'll have to manually check each gram to see if there's another wearable in the item's dropdown. Also, while this is an extremely rare occurrence with older grams, it is recommended that you seperate any grams that have the Limited Edition item from the others that do not. Since old LE and LE-less grams have the same ID, putting them together will merge them and they will all become LE-less, so put the LE grams in your Gallery in order to keep them apart just in case.


▸ Isn't there an NC portion to the main Festival of Neggs event?
Yes, there is in fact an NC portion to the main Festival of Neggs event! The style of the NC portion has changed a couple of times throughout the years, but we are now following a more consistent style of having three free NC Mystery Negg items and using specialty items (125 NC Dust or 600 NC Tinker Kit) on them. Each of those Mystery Negg items will reward five wearables with an additional item if you redeem all five wearables within them.

The only time a bonus item was rewarded by fully redeeming all three Mystery Neggs was in 2020's event. Despite the three Mystery Neggs being given out for free, the NC portion is completely optional and does not affect the main event in any way.

Fansite Festival of Neggs Articles and Guides
jellyneo.net/?go=festival_of_neggs
thedailyneopets.com/customization-wearables/neggs-20/
sunnyneo.com/neggfestival.php


▸ So, I got a bunch of NC Neggs from the past Festival of Negg Events and I don't have the retired items to open them. Am I just stuck with them forever?
You don't have to be stuck with them! You can do any of the following:

- Discard them by going through their item page in the Inventory.
- Upcycle them with NC Upcycle Fortune Cookies.
- Discard them with Charity Corner packs (when the event is active).
- Gift / Trade them away to other players with Gift Boxes.


▸ I heard GBCs are sometimes discounted. When would that be?
Gift Box Capsules/Cubes (GBCs) are discounted on two different events, the Black Friday Sale and the Spring Cleaning Sale.

The Black Friday GBC Sale happens around the week of Black Friday in November and usually lasts about one day (aside from 2020's sale lasting longer than that). For the first 12 hours of Black Friday NST, the new monthly GBC is released, and it is discounted by 50% off (100 NC). For the remaining 12 hours, they are discounted by 25% off (125 NC) the original GBC price.

The Spring Cleaning GBC Sale usually happens around April and is a day longer than the Black Friday GBC Sale. Instead of a new GBC, five GBCs released within the last year will be rereleased during the sale. For the first day of the sale, GBCs are 50% off (100 NC) and for the next day, they are 25% off (125 NC) their original price.


▸ Are discounted GBCs valued less/more than regular GBCs?
Unless the discounted GBCs are a couple of years old from their latest release, then no, they are neither valued less nor more than a regular monthly GBC.

The only current controversial instance where values might be discussed more thoroughly is with the Kaleidoscope Dreams Gift Box Mystery Capsules released on November 27, 2020. Those GBCs give out 4-7 Gift Boxes instead of the average 2-5 amount, but those GBCs can be a little tricky, since TNT released two different versions of the item with the same name, image, and description. Their Item IDs can be used identify them; the 11/27 GBCs (4-7 Gift Boxes) Item ID is 81979, and the 11/28-30 GBCs (2-5 Gift Boxes) Item ID is 81816. There is no way to identify which Item ID you'll receive upon accepting them.

People do have the right to value their items lower or higher than others, but no one is obliged to make a trade if one side feels the trade might be unfair without informed consent. If you ever feel unsure about a trade, then it is best to make a Value Check (VC) Thread on the NC Mall NeoBoard Chat.


▸ Does TNT discount Fortune Cookies?
TNT does discount Faerie Quest Fortune Cookies during the Faerie Quest Event which is in the Springtime. There has also been one instance where TNT discounted Training and NC Archives cookies by 50% off during the 2020's Black Friday Sale. It is unknown if they will ever discount those again.


▸ How do I get Crafting Faerie Quests?
Crafting Faerie (or Delina) Quests are only available during the Faerie Quest Event. You receive them after completing any Faerie Quest during the Faerie Quest Event. She cannot be summoned by Faerie Quest Fortune Cookies.

Fansite Delina Quests Articles and Guides
jellyneo.net/?go=faeriequests
thedailyneopets.com/customization-wearables/craft
sunnyneo.com/customisation/ncmall/craftingfaerie/index.php


▸ Is completing Crafting Faerie Quests a requirement if I want the end bonus reward of the Faerie Quest Event?
Faerie Quest Event? No, you do not have to complete Crafting Faerie Quests or Kaia Quests in order to get the end bonus reward. You just have to visit the Main Quest Page every day of the event to get the bonus reward.


▸ Can I use the Quest Refresh Boon on Crafting Faerie Quests?
Yes, you can use the Quest Refresh Boon on Crafting Faerie Quests although be warned that there is a significant chance that you may not receive any more of Delina's quests for the rest of the event after refreshing her.


▸ How long can I hold onto a Crafting Faerie Quest?
As Faerie Quests do not expire, you may hold onto a Crafting Faerie Quest for as long as you like although do know you cannot use the Shop Wizard (and Super Shop Wizard) while the quest is active.

We're not exactly sure why older Crafting Faerie Quest ingredients are still being sold when the later ingredients were retired, so you might want to purchase/trade for the items before they retire or just reject the quest if the item's not too special.


▸ Isn't there an NC portion to the Altador Cup event?
Yes, there is an NC portion to the Altador Cup event! The style of the NC portion has changed a couple of times throughout the years, but we are now following a more consistent style of having an item pack system with a bonus item at the end if you redeemed every one of each item. The characters that host the NC portion to the Altador Cup change every year, and the NC wearables are usually themed after the environment of Altador and the Altador Cup itself.

For this event, you are allowed to wait until the last day of the event to see if you like any of the items before trading/purchasing a pack. You are also allowed to redeem up to five multiples of the same item although multiples will not count towards the bonus item.

SunnyNeo's Past Altador Cup NC pages
sunnyneo.com/altadorcup/NCchallenge/


▸ Am I allowed to participate in the NC portion of the Altador Cup event on a side account?
Yes, you are allowed to participate in the NC portion of the Altador Cup event on a side account despite having to join a team to enter the page. Just keep in mind that your side accounts should not participate in any other AC activities that can give you NP/NP items (games, Staff Tournament, etc.) and you should discard the item prizes you get when signing up on a side.


▸ Isn't there an NC portion to the Daily Dare/Games Master Challenge event?
Yes, there is an NC portion to the Daily Dare event! Most, if not all, of the Daily Dare NC events, are hosted by AAA and Abigail's cousin, Lulu.

In terms of the Daily Dare event, the type of NC wearables Lulu gives out is related to the theme of the event (i.e. saving Roo Island, exploring space, etc.). DD sells a variety of event passes ranging anywhere from single packs, five packs, ten packs, and twenty packs.

In terms of the Games Master Challenge event, the type of NC wearables Lulu gives out is related to the games she asks you to play (i.e. submitting a score in Bruno's Backwoods Breakaway and Chemistry for Beginners rewards you the NC wearable, Tree of Potions). GMC only sells a single event pass which is usually at 700 NC.

Jellyneo's Past DD/GMC pages
jellyneo.net/?go=past_aaa_challenges


▸ Am I allowed to participate in the NC portion to the Daily Dare/Games Master Challenge event on my side accounts?
For the Daily Dare event, you are allowed to participate in the NC portion of the event on your side accounts. This does not mean you are allowed to participate in any activities that can reward NP/NP items (i.e. submit game score).

For the Games Master Challenge event, you are NOT allowed to participate in the NC portion of the event on your side accounts. Lulu requires you to actually play and submit game scores in order to get the NC wearables.


▸ Does anything notable happen on the NC Mall's birthday?
In celebration of the NC Mall's birthday in July, TNT releases three free No-Trade stat-boosting cupcakes/cakes with an NC wearable inside each one. You are allowed to collect these on your side accounts.

Aside from that, TNT also releases the Wish Candles and Birthday Rerelease Mystery Capsules.


▸ What are Wish Candles?
Wish Candles are essentially specialty capsules in a different shape. They usually contain 5 regular NC wearables and 1 Limited Edition Bonus NC wearable. Three Candles are released every year with the release date usually being within the month of the NC Mall's birthday. They cost 150 NC each.

Jellyneo's and SunnyNeo's Wish Candle Pages
items.jellyneo.net/openable-items/wish-candles/
sunnyneo.com/customisation/NCWishcandles.php


▸ What is the Haunted Mansion/Hijinks?
The Haunted Mansion (formally Haunted Hijinks) is an NC event during the month of October where players can purchase Mallet/Candle packs and get Halloween themed NC wearables. If you redeem a certain number of packs, you will receive additional Halloween themed Gift Boxes with the NC wearables. A bonus item is included if you have redeemed all the NC wearables, so there's that for an incentive.

For this event, you are allowed to wait until the last day of the event to see if you like any of the items before trading/purchasing a pack.

You can only redeem one of each item per account, but you are allowed to participate on your side accounts.

Jellyneo's and SunnyNeo's Haunted Mansion Articles
jellyneo.net/?go=haunted_mansion
sunnyneo.com/customisation/ncmall/hauntedhijinks.php


▸ What is Stocking Stufftacular?
Stocking Stufftacular is an NC event during the month of December where players can purchase Stocking Stufftacular packs and get Christmas/Winter themed NC wearables. If you redeem a certain number of packs, you will receive additional Winter themed NC wearables with the normal NC wearables. A bonus item is included if you have redeemed all the NC wearables, so there's that for an incentive.

There's also the incentive of participating in the event (whether that be a single pack or the largest pack) to get the Community Reward which is just an extra Christmas/Winter themed NC wearable.

For this event, you have to redeem your Stocking Stufftacular packs before the day the NC items are given out. Once the day has arrived, the item is officially retired.

You can only redeem five of each item per account, and you are allowed to participate on your side accounts.

Jellyneo's and SunnyNeo's Stocking Stufftacular Articles
jellyneo.net/?go=stocking_stufftacular
sunnyneo.com/customisation/ncmall/stockingstufftacular.php


▸ Is the Stocking Stufftacular worth it?
If you like Christmas/Winter themed NC wearables and liked the NC wearables from the previous years, then that's up to you. Full redemption bonuses can be or hit or miss, and it is a gamble to redeem multiple packs for an item you've never seen before.


▸ How does the NC portion to the Charity Corner event work?
Essentially, the event is quite similar to how NC Upcycle Fortune Cookies work with a prize shop system attached. You buy these Charity Corner donation packs to donate (discard) unwanted NC items for Donation Badges which can be redeemed for NC wearables.


▸ Does the NC Donations count toward the main Charity Corner event donation count?
NC donations do NOT count towards totals for final prizes.


▸ What are Dyeworks?
Dyeworks are certain existing NC wearables that come in different color variations! At Loic's Dyeworks Studio, players can use Dyeworks Hue Brew Potions to dye their items into different colors (and get their original back of course). You can read more about Dyeworks over at these guides:

Dyeworks Guides
jellyneo.net/?go=dyeworks
thedailyneopets.com/customization-wearables/dyeworks
sunnyneo.com/customisation/ncmall/NCdyeworks.php


▸ How do I dye an item?
You will first want to check if the item is available to dye at Loic's Dyeworks Studio. There are permanently dyeable items and there are items that have been retired from the Dyeworks Studio. If the item is available to dye, then you will have to obtain the original item and a Dyeworks Hue Brew Potion. Go visit Loic's Dyeworks Studio and select the original item in the wearables section below to dye said item.

NOTE: The item you receive will be randomly selected for you. You cannot choose which color item you'll receive.


▸ Why can't I dye X item?
Here's a quick list of reasons why you cannot dye X item:
- The item is retired.
- You do not have the original item and/or a Dyeworks Hue Brew Potion.
- You do not have JS enabled.


▸ How does Dyeworks Lending work?
Dyeworks Lending is when someone lends you the original item to dye in exchange for a GBC (if two items), Fortune Cookie, or small wishlist item.


▸ When are new Dyeworks items released?
New Dyeworks items are usually released seasonally and are available for a limited time only.


▸ If I purchase a Dyeworks Bundle, does it activate automatically or not?
Dyeworks Bundles activate immediately upon purchase.


▸ Is there anything special about the Advent Calendar Dyeworks Hue Brew Potions?
Advent Calendar Dyeworks Hue Brew Potions function the same as the regular Dyeworks Hue Brew Potion.


▸ What are Mysterious Morphing Experiments?
Mysterious Morphing Experiments (or MMEs) are NC wearables that periodically transform into different wearables. They are typically only available to be purchased for a week or two before their retirement, after which they begin morphing into other items! These items will transform into multiple wearables (and all transformations will be in your inventory at the end).


▸ What is an Item ID and how is that related to MMEs? How does one find item IDs?
MMEs are divided into two Item IDs (MiniMMEs are one Item ID) that associate with their thematic transformation. You can find out what the MME's ID is by following the instructions from these two JN pages:

Finding (MME) Item IDs
jellyneo.net/?go=mmexperiments
items.jellyneo.net/contribute/item-ids/


▸ My MME just changed into a different wearable. Why is that?
That is the magic of Mysterious Morphing Experiments! They will transform anywhere from your SDB, Closet (and pets), Gallery, and Inventory. They will stop morphing once their stages have been completed and you will get all the items in your inventory.


▸ Why is the MME on DTI/JN's Wardrobe weird?
Mysterious Morphing Experiments don't register quickly or easily into these customization fansites. The transformation has to be completed before they can be fully modeled.


▸ I heard MMEs have an additional Bonus item. How does one get that?
MME bonuses are randomly awarded with each initial MME. If you have multiple MMEs, then you have a better chance of getting a bonus (or multiple).


▸ When are new Mysterious Morphing Experiments released?
Nowadays, we only get one new MME per year. TNT has stopped doing MiniMMEs.


▸ What are Rerelease Capsules?
Rerelease Capsules (or RR Caps) are Mystery Capsules that are filled with items that have been retired. Usually they have lots of different items so getting a specific one can be almost impossible. Most let you pick either by year, or by item type e.g. Accessories, Backgrounds and Trinkets, Clothing.

There are many types of Rerelease Capsules, most common are the Seasonal ones such as: Fall (which contain items released during Fall), Winter, Summer, Spring and sometimes holiday ones like Christmas or Halloween. They are not released every year though, TNT may go long periods before releasing these.

Jellyneo's Mystery Capsule Article
jellyneo.net/?go=mystery_capsules


▸ What is Shenanigifts?
Shenanigifts is an NC Mall Game where players can join a party full of costumed Elephantes, and receive gifts from the attending guests. To play, you must purchase a Shenanigifts Invitation Pack and enter in one of the three available parties. You can speak to three different guests to see what NC wearables they have to gift, but once you speak to a guest you must reject their offer if you wish to see what the next guest is offering. If you reach the third guest without accepting anything, you are forced to accept the third guest's item unless you have the Second Look Power-Up.

Fansite Shenanigifts Articles and Guides
jellyneo.net/?go=shenanigifts
thedailyneopets.com/customization-wearables/shenanigifts
sunnyneo.com/customisation/ncmall/shenanigifts.php


▸ Are the Shenanigifts Power-Ups worth it?
Not really, and the power-ups are No-Trade. If you were planning to purchase a 10-pack for yourself, you can save 25 NC when you purchase a 5-pack and five Gift Party Power-Ups.


▸ What is Patapult?
Patapult is an NC Mall bowling game with a prize shop system for NC wearables. How the game works is that you click on the Patamoose and slowly drag your mouse towards the lower "lip" of the holes. You'll have three tries and whatever totem you get for your third attempt is the one you'll be taking home if you didn't claim a totem prior.

At the prize shop, you can redeem these tiered totems for the NC wearables available. The totems remain in the prize shop and are No-Trade, but they don't expire.

Fansite Patapult Articles and Guides
jellyneo.net/?go=patapult
sunnyneo.com/customisation/ncmall/patapult.php
thedailyneopets.com/customization-wearables/patapult


▸ What is Wonderclaw?
Bigsby Shadington's Wonderclaw is an NC Mall claw game where players can scoop out a random NC wearable from a specially themed claw machine. To play, you must purchase a Wonderclaw Widget pack and select one of the three available claw machines.

You'll be prompted to enter your Wonderclaw Widget into the machine and be shown an interactive animation to get your reward. It is unknown if the placement or time affects the tier of the award, but it has been proven that the color of the ball capsule does not affect the item's prize tier.

Fansite Wonderclaw Articles and Guides
jellyneo.net/?go=wonderclaw
thedailyneopets.com/customization-wearables/wonderclaw
sunnyneo.com/customisation/ncmall/wonderclaw.php


▸ Are the Wonderclaw Power-Ups worth it?
Not really and the power-ups are No-Trade. If you were planning to purchase a 10-pack for yourself, you can save 25 NC when you purchase a 5-pack and five Large Claw Power-Ups. The Tier Boost Power-Up isn't really too helpful considering most if not all Wonderclaw items are easily obtainable at a low value when they are currently available.


▸ Can I still play the retired NC Mall games?
No, you cannot play Blumaroll, JubJub Power Bounce, and Secret Meepit 'Stache as they are officially retired. If you had any tokens/packs leftover, they're essentially collectors items now.


▸ What are Monthly Collectible Collections?
Monthly Collectible items are essentially just a limited time NC wearable released every month for a themed 6-month trend. They can be stored in the NC Collectible Collector's Album, located in your User Lookup, and there's a bonus item if you happen to purchase (not trade) all the NC Collectibles within a given trend. They cost 250 NC and they retire on the first day of the next month.

Jellyneo's and SunnyNeo's Monthly Collectible Collections Articles
jellyneo.net/?go=nc_mall&page=collectibles
sunnyneo.com/customisation/ncmall/NCcollectibles.php


▸ My Monthly Collectible is stuck in my Collector's Album. What can I do?
You'll first need to have Flash enabled and disable your ad-blocker. Once you do that, head over to your NC Album, click the NC item's image and click "Remove from Album" a bunch of times. If that doesn't work, send a ticket at the official FAQ for assistance.


▸ Does anything cool happen if I fill out my Collector's Album?
There won't be any blanks, but nah, nothing else happens. Those NC items will just be there for show.

Special thanks and FAQ contributions here from _sissiy_sis_369 (Rerelease Capsules).

Neopian Pound FAQs

Pound Basics Related

▸ What is the Neopian Pound?
The Neopian Pound is a section of the site where you can adopt, transfer, or abandon a pet. When you visit the main page of the pound, you'll see an image of three doors for the three functions of the pound. The main page requires Flash, but you can go directly to these links if you can't enable Flash:

The Neopian Pound Links
Adopt a Pet Link
Transfer a Pet Link (+ Transfer Status Link)
Abandon a Pet Link


▸ How do I adopt a pet?
To start, you'll need to find the pet you want to adopt. You can do this by browsing or refreshing the Adopt section of the Pound. When you see a pet you want to adopt, click on it so it appears in a green box, then click the green and white "ADOPT" button and click "Yes" when asked to confirm.

If you know the name of the pet you want to adopt, you can type it into the box that says "Search Abandoned Neopets by Name.

You can also use the link below and replace X with the name of the pet you want to adopt:
//www.neopets.com/pound/adopt.phtml?search=X


▸ Why am I unable to adopt a pet?
There are a few reasons you might be unable to adopt a pet:

- You've reached the maximum number of pets. Currently, premium accounts are allowed to have 10 pets and non-premium accounts are allowed to have 6.

- Your account is too young. New accounts (under 4 months) are subject to some adoption restrictions (jellyneo.net/?go=pound#restrictions); they can only adopt pets up to level 2, of certain colors, and of non-restricted, non-limited species. New accounts won't even be able to see these pets in the pound, so there's little chance of accidentally trying to adopt.

- You don't have enough Nepoints (NP) on hand. Pet adoption fees are calculated based on the pet's level, strength, defence, and movement, so a pet with a high level and/or BD stats will be more expensive to adopt than a low-level pet with no stats.

- The pet is in "Waiting" status. This is a bizarre glitch in which a pet's petpage will show its owner as "none," but its petlookup will show its status as "Waiting..." If you try to adopt the pet, it will not be available in the pound.

- Someone else adopted the pet first.


▸ How do I transfer a pet?
To start, visit the Transfer section of the Pound. You'll see your pets in a row with the Transfer button under each one. Click the button and fill in the UN of the friend you want to transfer the pet to. If you want to trade your pet for one of your friend's pets, you can do that on the next screen. Transferring a pet will cost you 1,000 Neopoints, and your friend will have to pay an adoption fee of the same amount that they'd have to pay if they adopted the pet from the pound.


▸ Why am I unable to transfer a pet?
There are a few reasons you might be unable to transfer a pet:

- The pet has a no-trade petpet attached, such as a Pile of Soot. You'll get a pop-up reminding you to detach the petpet before trying again.

- Your friend's UN was entered incorrectly. Reenter the UN all in lowercase.

- You and/or your friend don't have enough NP to complete the transfer. Make sure you have at least 1,000 NP out and your friend has enough out to cover the adoption fee.

- You're out of transfers for the month. You only get so many depending on the age of your account; you can check how many here (jellyneo.net/?go=pound#transfer). You won't be able to transfer the pet until your transfers reset on the first day of the next calendar month.

- The pet was already transferred once today. You'll get a message saying "X does not want to be User-to-User Transfered right now. Perhaps tomorrow it will be okay." Pets can only be used to initiate a transfer once per day*, according to the Neopets clock.

* There is a workaround here; a pet can be transferred multiple times per day as long as another pet is used to initiate the transfer. For example, let's say that Anna sends the pet Sven to Elsa. Elsa wants to send Sven to Kristoff, but she can't initiate the transfer because Sven has already been transferred once. Kristoff will need to initiate the transfer by offering one of his pets to Elsa in exchange for Sven. (He can adopt a pet from the pound if he doesn't want to give up one of his own pets. Once Kristoff has Sven and Elsa has the pound pet, she can repound it if she doesn't want to keep it.)


▸ How do I abandon a pet?
To abandon or "pound" a pet, visit the Abandon section of the Pound. You'll see your pets in a row with a button under each one. If you have a PIN enabled for this section of the site, enter it in the box. Then click the button under the pet you want to abandon. You will have to click it five times, and each time the text will change to dire pleas and heart-wrenching entreaties such as "Give me up?" or "Leave me to die." You need to callously ignore this begging until you've clicked for the fifth time, when the pet will go into the pound and be available for others to adopt.


▸ Why am I unable to abandon a pet?
There are a few reasons you might be unable to pound a pet:

- The pet has a no-trade petpet attached, such as a Pile of Soot. You'll get a pop-up reminding you to detach the petpet before trying again.

- You don't have enough NP to abandon the pet. Take out at least 250 NP before trying again.

- You've already abandoned a pet today; the limit for abandoning or pounding a pet is one per day per account. You'll get a pop-up saying "Error: Sorry, you can only leave one Neopet at the pound every day. It is quite full in here already!" You'll need to wait until it's a new day by the Neopets clock to abandon the pet. If you have transfers for the month remaining, you can also transfer the pet to a side account and abandon it from there, assuming you haven't already abandoned a pet from that side account today.


▸ Why are there items in my inventory and/or closet after abandoning a pet?
When you abandon a pet, the following items will be left in your account:

- Any paint brush clothes the pet was wearing, regardless of whether they match its current species/color or not.
- Any NP wearables the pet was wearing.
- Any NC wearables the pet was wearing.
- Any Battledome equipment that was attached to the pet.


▸ What is a Glitched Pet?
Any pet that is quite literally glitched. These pets are considered rare and sometimes valuable in trading. Many glitched pets will display as an incorrect pet image or a broken image. Some examples include pets that have names with spaces in them (i.e. I am cool the Plushie Draik), Unknown Grundos, and pets with a mismatched color/species (i.e. Lemon Hissi).

The Glitch Index (Glitched Pets Guide)
/~Actuality


▸ What is a Grandfathered Pet?
Often at times, this is another name for an unconverted pet. On the PC this may also refer to UC pets with semi-questionable names that have been 'grandfathered' in and allowed to stay on the site. TNT staff determines this on a case by case basis, but has acknowledged that the cutoff date was in 2007.

- Neopets Editorial - Issue 928 | Question 3 [link] (General Info)


▸ Is there anything else I need to know about the basic of the Pound Chat?
The Pound Chat is home to a wide variety of players and the best way to approach this community is by practicing good netiquette. There will be people who have varying opinions on pet names, pet appearances, and so on, but it's best to be kind and respectful through and through.

Pound Surfing Related

▸ What is a Stuck Pet?
A stuck pet is a pet that cannot be found by browsing or refreshing the pound. You need to know the pet's name and search for it in to order to see the pet in the pound and adopt it.

Pets get stuck based on the first few letters of their names. For more information on stuck pets and which letters get stuck, see the following petpage:

Mega's Stuck Pet Searching Guide
/~Megablade


▸ Do colored pets in the pound come with clothes?
No. When a pet is pounded, its clothes will stay in the owner's closet. This includes paint brush clothes, NP wearables, and NC wearables.

If you find an unclothed pet in the pound and want the paint brush clothes for that species and color, you can find someone with the clothes, send them the pet, and ask them to transfer it back to you. Transferring the pet will bring the clothes of the matching paint brush color along with it. To find people with spare clothes available, see the following links:

Dress to Impress
impress.openneo.net/

Extra Paint Brush Clothing Petpages
/~Kyynator
/~ExtraPBClothes
/~Uniks


▸ I just saw a pet with clothes in the pound. Why is that?
This is usually a visual glitch, and can happen for one of two reasons:

- Pets that have been in the pound for years, pre-conversion, will sometimes display with their paint brush clothes on, such as Bruces and Usuls with bows or Elephantes with headdresses. After you adopt the pet and customize it for the first time, it will no longer show up with the clothes on.

- There are also a few types of pets that show up as fully customized and the wrong species in the pound. For example, in the image below, is an example of a Blue Uni that appears as a fully customized Red Acara. In these cases, the written information on the adopt page is correct and the pet will not have clothes (nor will it be a Red Acara) when adopted:

Blue Uni OR Red Acara???

▸ What happens when you abandon a Lutari?
When you abandon or transfer a Lutari, the Lutari runs off to pound limbo. The pet cannot be readopted nor can the name can be recreated. Only in specific situations, will TNT Support let you readopt your abandoned Lutari.


▸ I just saw a Magma pet/Ice Bori in the pound, but it turned out to be colored Red/Blue. Why is that?
Presumably to maintain the exclusivity of the colors, all Magma pets will turn Red upon being pounded and Ice Boris will turn Blue. (Ice pets of other species will retain the ice color.) If you see a pet in the pound that appears to be Magma or an Ice Bori, it's a visual glitch akin to the pets-with-clothes issues described above. After you adopt the pet and customize it for the first time, it will no longer show up as a Magma pet or an Ice Bori.


▸ Am I allowed to remove a Petpet from a Pound Pet then toss the Pet back into the Pound?
While this is distasteful behavior, you are allowed to adopt and repound a pet from the Pound for the sole purpose of taking its Petpet. TNT has stated that the adopted Pet's Petpet is essentially yours to keep and they have no interest in investigating pounded Pets that had their Petpets removed.

Neopets Editorial - Issue 753 | Question 5 [link]

I'd like a clarification of something from two weeks ago's editorial. "I recently created a new side account and adopted several neopets out of the pound. One of these neopets had a petpet attached. At first I thought I'd just leave it be, but then I looked the petpet up and found out it was valuable. Can I sell the petpet if I tranfer it to my main first, or is this considered using a side account to cheat? P.S. Please remove my UN. ~ UN removed Hi! You adopted the petpet, it's yours to do what you want with! If you transfer it to your main, you can sell it if you want to." This makes it sound like it's okay to use the pound for financial gain. This text "Note: The Neopian Pound is not to be abused for financial gain. Selling Neopets, or profiting from abandoned Neopets is a freezable offence." is found on the first page of the pound. This makes it sound like adopting a pet to sell it's petpet is not okay but your past editorial makes it sound okay. Please advice. ~ johnnydeppluver1222

Hi! So the notice on the Pound page refers to trading Neopets for neopoints (or neopoint items) via the Pound. You can trade Neopet for other Neopets, but not anything else, and doing so is a freezable offense. However, adopting a pet and realizing it has a petpet is a different issue - that's an item we cannot force you to keep (and we have no interest in doing so).


▸ What is pound_release?
To answer this question, we need to go into a little bit of Neopets history. In 2007, TNT took the pound down for maintenance. People could still pound pets during that time, but the pets could not be adopted. TNT created the pound_release account to hold the pets that had been pounded so they wouldn't all dumped into the pound right away when it reopened.

Between 2008 and 2019, pets in pound_release were slowly released into the pound and were able to be adopted. On petpages, the owner was listed as "pound_release." However, TNT changed that in 2019; these pets are no longer being released and the petpage lists the owner as "none." Until TNT fixes this, you will not be able to adopt any pet that is currently in pound_release, and it can be hard to tell if a pet is in pound_release, on breik_u5 (see the next question), or stuck in the pound (see the above question on "What is a Stuck Pet?").

For more information about pound_release and the pets that are currently in it, see the following petpage:

pound_release Pet List
/~Poundal


▸ What is breik_u5?
breik_u5 is an account similar to pound_release. The majority of pets on breik_u5 are Grundos and/or badly named pets. Pets on breik_u5 have never been released, and their petpages also list the owner as "none" now. You will not be able to adopt any pet that is currently on breik_u5.

For more information about breik_u5 and the pets that are currently on it, see the following petpage:

breik_u5 (PR-like) Pet List
/~Brekt

Pet Trading Related

▸ Is my pet rare or worth anything?
The short answer: It depends.

The long answer: It depends on a lot of things. The "value" of a pet varies wildly depending on its converted/unconverted status, name, Battledome stats, and species and color. In rarer cases, some people who trade or seek pets may also be looking for specific attributes, such as a certain age (year created), a certain birthday/birthdate, or achievements such as trophies. As of October 2020, the following pets tend to be sought on the Pound Chat (PC) board:

- Unconverted (UC) pets, particularly rarer species and colors.

- Pets with names that are real words (RW), particularly common words in English.

- Pets with names that are real names (RN), particularly first/given names with the most common spelling in English.

- Pets with names that are 3-4 letters long (3L/4L). These are often expressed as a "CVC," "VCV," etc., where C stands for "consonant" and V stands for "vowel." Thus, a pet named rsr would be a CCC 3L; a pet named Nimo would be a CVCV 4L.

- Pets with Battledome stats, which are expressed in HSD (health/hit points + strength + defence).

- Pets created in 1999, the first year that the site existed, and occasionally pets created in 2000, the second year.

However, it's impossible to give a definitive answer to this question. You may have the most desirable pet in the world, but it's only "worth" something if you find a person who wants it and they have something you want. If you have a pet that you'd like to trade, your best bet is to do some research on past trades, ask friends who are experienced traders, or make a board on the PC asking for opinions.


▸ What does this acronym/phrase mean in the Pound Chat?
The Pound Chat board (PC) has a lingo all its own. Some common phrases and terms used there include:

General Terms
Meaning
UC
Unconverted pet. When customization was introduced, pets of certain species/color combinations were given the opportunity to remain "unconverted," meaning they display on the site using the old-style artwork.

Many of these pets are considered desirable since they can no longer be created. UC pets can wear most backgrounds and some foreground items, but few other NP or NC wearables.
Tiers
Most UC trading guides separate pets into tiers of some kind, to reflect the fact that some UC pets are numerous and/or common, while others are rare. The three best-known UC trading guides are:

- /~Danpo, which divides pets into 10 tiers
- /~Heat, which divides pets into 11 indexes
- /~Za, which divides pets into 6 levels.
Converted
Converted pet. Any pet created after customization was introduced is a converted pet. In addition, not all UC pets were given the option to remain UC (for example, there is no UC Red Kougra), so older pets of certain colors/species now appear as converted pets. Converted pets can wear clothes and other NP and NC wearables.
Clothed/Unclothed
A pet that has its paint brush clothes is considered "clothed." A pet that does not have its clothes is "unclothed." Most people prefer to spell out these terms so they aren't confused with "UC" for "unconverted.
UFT/UFQT
Up for Trade/Up for Quick Trade. People who are trading a pet will usually use the term UFT, but may use UFQT to convey that they're looking for a fast trade.
UFA/UFQA
Up for Adoption/Up for Quick Adoption. Generally, pets that are UFA/UFQA are available to the first person who expresses interest and the current owner does not expect lengthy applications for them, but people may use UFQA to convey that they hope to rehome the pet quickly.
Custom
When trading a pet, you can offer or inquire about a custom, meaning that the current owner will morph/paint/dip the pet into a certain species or color before trading. For more information, see the question "What does it mean to do Custom on a pet?" below.
Y1, Y2, Y3, etc.
The year the pet was created. Y1 pets were created in 1999, Y2 pets in 2000, Y3 pets in 2001, and so on. One or more of these descriptors are often used together, e.g. "I have a converted Y3 Kougra + 1m custom UFQT.

Name Terms
Meaning
RW
A name that is a correctly-spelled real word, usually in English; RWs in other languages are often specified as "Language RW," such as "Spanish RW" or "Japanese RW.
RN
A name that is a real name, usually in English; RNs in other languages are often specified as "Language RN," such as "Spanish RN" or "Japanese RN." This generally refers to first or given names, not surnames/last names/family names or place names.

The most common spelling(s) of a name is generally preferred over unusual or less recognizable spellings.
Misspell/MS
A RW or RN that has been misspelled. There is a great deal of latitude given for use of this term, with some misspells being very close to the correct spelling and others being very different.

Some people prioritize pronunciation in a misspell, meaning that they might consider Cricut a desirable misspell of Cricket, but not Kryckhette.

Another common misspell is the use of a capital I, lowercase l, or number 1 to create a name that looks visually close to the real one; for example, the name "CaroIyn" includes a capital I instead of a lowercase l, making it appear as "Carolyn" in certain fonts.
VWN
Very Well Named
WN
Well Named
DN
Decent Named/Decent Name
BN
Badly Named/Bad Name
VBN
Very Badly Named/Very Bad Name
2L, 3L, 4L, etc.
The number of letters in the pet's name; for example, Judi would be a 4L.

This term can be used for names of any length, but is more commonly seen with shorter names up to ~6L.
2C, 3C, 4C, etc.
The number of characters, including both letters and numbers, in the pet's name; for example, C3PO would be a 4C.

This term can be used for names of any length, but is more commonly seen with shorter names up to ~4C
CVC, CVCV, etc.
The name format, where C stands for "consonant" and V stands for "vowel."

For example, Judi would be a CVCV. Xxxx, Xxxx###, Xxxx_###, etc.: For privacy reasons, some people will mask pet names in this way, where X is a capital letter, x is a lowercase letter, # is a number, and _ is an underscore.

This is never done when advertising, offering, or bidding your own pet, as your trader needs to know its real name. It's more commonly used when looking for advice or opinions, such as, "I was just offered XxxxxxxXxxxx_##_### the UC Royalgirl Kyrii for my UC Grey Tonu; is that a good trade?
Capitalized/uppercase/capped
Name starts with a capital letter, i.e. Judianne. This has nothing to do with capped BD stats, discussed below.
Lowercase/uncapped
Name starts with a lowercase letter, i.e. judianne. This has nothing to do with uncapped BD stats, discussed below.
Compound
Name includes two or more distinct words. The capitalization format can vary; both KrazyKarma and Krazykarma would be considered compounds.

The term is generally applied to words that are not usually used together, such as ElementalDream or Nightsinging; names like Campfire or Pancake would not usually be considered compounds, since they have a long history of being used as one word.

One or more of these descriptors are often used together, e.g. "I have a VWN 4L Cvcv pet UFT.

The majority of pet names on the site are neither RWs nor RNs, so these terms were created to refer to the quality of the pet's name based on the format and style (length of name, capitalized vs. uncapitalized, containing numbers and/or underscores). This is where things start getting mushy, as one person's VWN pet may be WN to another. These terms should not take personal preference into account; e.g., "I have a bad association with the name Daphne so she is VBN" is not relevant. Many trading guides, such as /~Danpo and /~Ofu, specify how many capital/lowercase letters, numbers, and/or underscores are acceptable for each type of name. In addition, specific games, trading databases, or petpages may have their own standards for what qualifies as a VWN vs. WN pet.

Battledome Terms
Meaning
BD
A pet with stats that make it suited to fight in the Battledome.
Level / LVL
The pet's level. You can find this information on your quickref page, the pet's lookup, or on the status page at any of the training schools.
HSD/stats
BD stats are calculated as HSD, which stands for health/hit points, strength, and defence.

You can find this information on your quickref page or the pet's lookup, if the numbers are high enough, or on the status page at any of the training schools. To get the HSD, add the three numbers together.

Movement/agility is not taken into account. Generally speaking, pets with higher HSD are considered more desirable, except...
Capped/uncapped
In the Battledome, strength and defence are capped at 750. A pet with 750 strength will do more damage than a pet with 700 strength. However, because of the cap, a pet with 800 strength will do the same damage as a pet with 750 strength.

There's no benefit to training strength and defence past 750. Health, on the other hand, is not capped and can be trained infinitely. As a result, traders will refer to the stats of a high-HSD pet as "capped.

For example, a pet with strength 750, defence 750, and health/hit points 750 equals 2250 HSD. A pet with strength 800, defence 800, and health/hit points 800 equals 2300 capped HSD because the extra 50 strength and defence points are not taken into account.

This pet could conceivably be advertised as 2400 uncapped HSD, but most people don't bother if they're dealing with a pet with such high stats.
Even/uneven
When the health, strength, and defence are close in number, a pet is said to be even.

A pet with strength 120, defence 118, and health/hit points 122 would be considered even.

A pet with strength 120, defence 8, and health/hit points 165 would be considered uneven.

Unevenly-statted pets are often a product of using the Lab Ray. Pets with even stats are generally considered more desirable.
Trainable/untrainable
At the training schools, a pet's level must be at least half its highest stat to train (the exception is the Mystery Island Training School, where you can train health/hit points to 3 times your pet's level, but you still need to raise the level to train strength or defence, so we'll mostly ignore that).

For example, a pet at level 60 with strength 105, defence 100, and health/hit points 110 is trainable because 60 is more than half of 110. You could train any of the stats for this pet without needing to raise its level. A pet at level 60 with strength 120, defence 8, and health/hit points 165 is not trainable because you would not be able to train defence until you raise its level to 83, which is half of 165.

Untrainable pets with a low level and high strength and health are often a product of using the Lab Ray. Pets that are trainable are generally considered more desirable. One or more these descriptors are often used together, e.g. "I have a 600 HSD e/t pet UFT.

For information on Pound Chat games, such as the Pet Auction House, Pet Roulette, and Shuffle, see the Pound Chat Games Related section.


▸ What does it mean to do Custom on a pet?
When a person offers to trade or adopt out a pet with a custom, it means they're offering to make the pet into your desired species and/or color before adopting it out to you. Pets are only allowed to be traded as pet for pet (not items for pet or pet-plus-items for pet), so the custom must be done before they send you the pet. This has nothing to do with customizing, which refers to adding wearables (backgrounds, foregrounds, or clothing) to a pet.

Most customs are offered as a value in Neopoints; for example, if someone offers you a "4m custom," that means you could ask for any species/color that can be done for 4 million NP or less. Some people will also offer a Fountain Faerie dip (FFQ), a premium perk, or a Color It Wild/Charity Corner perk as part of a trade, but would specify that since different species/colors are available with each of those special options.


▸ What is a UL Custom? Is that even allowed?
Yes, sort of. An unlimited custom means that the person offering the custom is willing to spend any amount of NP on changing the pet's species and/or color. Currently the most expensive species/color that can be attained with NP is a Mutant Draik, which runs about 15 million for a Transmogrification Potion.

However, certain things CANNOT be requested under the umbrella of an unlimited custom, such as:

- "Can you open a Faerie Quest Fortune Cookie to get an FFQ and dip the pet into an Alien Aisha?
- "Can you buy premium and use your premium perk to turn the pet into an Ice Bori?
- "Can you buy 100 Armoured Neggs and increase the pet's defence?
- "Can you buy a petpet and/or a petpetpet and attach it to the pet?
- "Can you buy the Stargazing Background and put it on the pet?
- "Can you enter the pet in the Beauty Contest and have it win in its species?
- "Can you feed the pet 700 gourmet foods/read the pet 1500 books and get a trophy?
- "Can you use the pet to get to the end of Neoquest so I can get the avatar?

Also, this term has nothing to do with one's userlookup, which is sometimes also referred to as a "UL".


▸ Am I allowed to purposely trade a Pet with Petpets, Petpetpets (P3s), Wearables, etc. added?
As mentioned above, pets are only allowed to be traded as one pet for one pet, and you are not allowed to profit from trading. Petpets, P3s, and wearables cannot be considered as part of the trade. When you're looking at a pet you're interested in, make sure you base your decision on the pet itself (name, converted/unconverted, color/species, stats, etc.).

It is generally not suggested to send expensive NP wearables with a pet that is being traded; if the other person removes and sells them, it might look like they're profiting from the trade. Many people do leave petpets and P3s attached (especially since removing the petpet would remove the P3) when trading; however, if they remove an expensive petpet, you should not NM them to ask for the petpet or complain about it not being attached.

If you trade for a pet that has wearables, a petpet, and/or P3 attached, it's usually a good idea to ask if the other person wants them back. If they aren't very expensive, most people will say no, and you are free to detach them and put them in your closet/inventory/safety deposit box.


▸ How does one actually break into UC Trading?
The short answer: Find someone with a UC that you want and offer them a pet that they want. Trade. Everyone's happy.

The long answer: Converted to UC trading is intensely subjective, since people seek and value all sorts of different things in pets. However, if you are trying to break into UC trading, here are some very general suggestions:

- Offer a RW/RN pet

- Offer a pet with a short, pronounceable name (3-4 letters)

- Offer a pet with BD stats, preferably even/trainable. The higher the HSD the better, and some people prefer pets at level 250+ so they can avoid the long training courses at the Mystery Island Training School.

- Offer an NP custom, FFQ, premium perk, or Color It Wild perk on your converted pet.

- Offer your pet in shuffles where people with UC pets are accepting converted bids (see the PC Games Related section below)

- Look for people on the PC who are offering UC pets in exchange for very specific converted pets, such as a certain birthday/birthdate, personality attributes, or name.

- Any combination of these suggestions is also helpful; for example, a 4L RW pet with BD stats and a custom has a better chance of finding a trade than a 4L pet or BD pet by itself.

If you have a BD pet and are hoping to trade it for a UC, see /~Trelm for a general guide on values or /~Ofu for past trades.


▸ Are pet trades through Neomail safe?
Yes, as long as the trade is one pet for one pet. Some pet traders prefer to discuss trades via neomail for various reasons (chatting about the details without spamming a board, keeping track of future trades if they are out of transfers this month, etc.).


▸ Is there anything else I need to know about Pet Trading?
If you are ever unsure if something is allowed/disallowed in terms of Pet Trading, then it doesn't hurt to ask the Pound Chat NeoBoard Chat, Help NeoBoard Chat, or Charter NeoBoard Chat (Premium Only). Pet Trading can be pretty complicated at times, so it's understandable if you get lost on the subject.

PC Games Related

▸ What are the different types of Pound Chat games?
A Pound Auction/Shuffle is a Pound Chat game in where members list their pets up for random offers by anyone for fun! Just do know that there's a risk to the listers on the inevitable aspect of accepting trades and those trades won't always go well (unless there's specified reasons depending on the type).

Pound Auction & Shuffle
Themes, Types, and Clauses
Summary / Description
Pass
Listers are allowed to pass on all the bids received on their listings.
No Pass
Listers must accept a bid if any were received on their listings.
Half & Half (H&H)
Listers offer two pets, and must accept at least one offer only if both pets receive bids.
Spicy H&H
Listers offer two pets, and must accept at least one bid.
Pound Auction House (PAH)
Usually Converted Pets only.
Pet Roulette
Converted pets, but you must accept the first VWN offer you get, or use your pass and take your second offer.
Shuffles
Usually Unconverted Pets (UCs) only.
Safety Net Shuffles
Listers have to accept a UC a Tier under or above.
Same Tier Shuffles
Listers have to accept a UC the same Tier or above.
Goal Pet Shuffles
Listers choose 1-3 Dream Pets (host will specify and you have to choose that exact amount, from the same tier or lower) and you are allowed to pass if you do not receive a Dream Pet bid.
Name Swap Clause
Usually, only in a Same Tier Shuffle, Listers are allowed to pass if the only valid bid they receive would essentially be a same colored species name swap.
Exception Clause
Usually, only in a Same Tier Shuffle, Listers are allowed to pick ONE pet from that tier to be able to pass on if it is their only same tier bid.
WN/VWN Clause
WN/VWN Pet Listers are allowed to pass if they do not receive a WN/VWN offer.
Color Clause
Listers can choose color or colors that confer a pass.


▸ Are these Pound Chat games even allowed?
Yes, any game that ends in a one pet for one pet trade is allowed. Generally, these games are designed for quicker trading than traditional advertising boards.


▸ How do I host a Pound Chat game? Is difficult to host one?
Not at all! There are a few main guides with instructions on how to host. Be sure to check how active the PC boards are first and if there are other games already being hosted! If you're not sure, post an interest check board before hosting a new game.

Another note, most PC games will have titles with a series of clapping smilies to make them easier to spot.

Pound Chat Game Guides & More
- /~Medicare (UC Shuffle)
- /~Cheesy (Pet House Auction)
- /~Dawg (Pet Roulette)
- /~Hickups (PAH/Shuffle Petpage Premades)


▸ What happens if I participate in a Pound Chat game, but I don't want to trade my pet?
If the game was Free Pass themed, then you are allowed to pass all offers. If it wasn't a Free Pass, then you were obliged to do so. No one can force you to trade your pet, but you shouldn't have listed/bidded a pet, because you are essentially wasting other people's time.

If you think you'll have regrets or might feel bad about trading your pet, then please don't list/bid your pet.


▸ In a Pound Chat game, what happens if my chosen lister/bidder disappears?
The host will reach out to the lister/bidder via Neomail to let them know that they received a bid or had their bid accepted, and hopefully, the Neomail will remind them or alert them of the trade. No one can force another player to trade, so at the end of the day, it's up to an honor system. Individual hosts can choose not to allow that person to list/bid in their auctions anymore if they make a habit of disappearing, but oftentimes the reason is innocuous (the lister/bidder fell asleep/had to leave unexpectedly), and the trade is completed at a later time.

If your lister/bidder disappeared, you can also choose to accept another offer on your pet.


▸ Am I allowed to list/bid with a pet from the pound/creatable pet name?
You cannot offer an unaltered pet in the pound or a name without some sort of modification (because then anyone could adopt/create the pet), but you absolutely can offer a custom/FFQ/Premium Perk on an undetermined pet (usually the lister/bidder will determine the name/pound pet).

Typical listings will include:
- Pound Pet + (NP Amount) Custom
- Untaken Name + FFQ
Or the name of a pet you already own plus those values.


▸ Why did the host disallow my bidded/listed pet?
It could be for a variety of reasons. Certain PAHs/Shuffles have "types" such as 4L/RW/RN, and your pet may not fall into those categories. Another possibility is the pet name; most PAHs require pets to be V/WN in listing to be considered a "valid" bid.

In shuffles, you can typically only list UC pets, and only pets in the "Quiggle pot" (called this because they have a Quiggle emoji added when listing) are accepting converted bids. So, any converted bid on a pet outside of the Quiggle pot would not be considered.

In PAHs, it depends on the host, but some only allow converted listings, as UCs tend to draw too much of the bidding pool and can deter others from listing as they will likely receive fewer bids and thus fewer options to choose from in a No Pass where they are expected to trade.


▸ Are Neomails okay in these Pound Chat games?
Typically, the only Neomails that occur are from the host to a lister/bidder if they ghosted (abandoned) a board where a trade is expected to be made. There isn't anything outright forbidding them, but the spirit of the game is to bid/trade/communicate on the board. If you missed the bidding and want to trade for a listed pet after the PAH, Neomailing is fine.


▸ Is there anything else I need to know about Pound Chat games?
So many things could go here! My two cents:

- Don't be afraid to give it a try and to ask questions! Speaking as an avid PAH lister/bidder/host, we're always excited to see new faces, and we want to make it an enjoyable experience where all parties come out happy.
- If you decide to host one, consider a No Pass the first time just so you can get the flow down. Half & Half and No Pass tend to have a lot more listers and thus a lot more to keep track of.
- Don't be a spooky ghost. If you choose to play, commit and make the trades you said you would. Never list if you aren't certain you'll be willing to trade for a VWN basic pet (PAH/Roulette tied).
- Don't be disheartened if your pet doesn't receive bids or get accepted. Trading can be competitive, but the goal of the game is always to have fun and find a trade both parties are happy with, and sometimes that takes time and patience.

Purge Info Related

▸ What is a Purge?
A purge is when TNT deletes inactive/abandoned accounts from their server. When an account is purged, the account name and pet names on that account will become available for anyone to recreate.

THE PURGE FAQ
/~John


▸ How can I prevent my account from being purged?
You would want to log into your account once in the past 48 months (2 years) to prevent a purge. Putting wearables and/or purchasing Neocash on your side account might help, but are not thought to be necessary to prevent a potential purging of your inactive account.

NOTE: "Last Spotted: A long, long time ago" is not a definitive mark that your account will be purged. That only means you haven't logged in a year.


▸ How often does Neopets do these purges?
Viacom TNT has historically performed a purge once every three years. JumpStart TNT has yet to perform any purge, but they have mentioned that they plan to do one in the future.


▸ When was the last purge?
The last purge was on November 2012.


▸ Should I prepare for a purge?
If you're looking for Real Word/Names from inactive accounts, then this might be worth considering. If not, then you should probably save some of your sanity.


▸ Is there anything else I need to know about The Purge?
For more answers and information, I would check out /~John. If you did not find what you were looking for, or would like to discuss purge related conversation, then I'd head over to the Neopian Pound NeoBoard Chat.

Unconverted Pets Related

▸ What is an Unconverted Pet?
An unconverted pet is a pet that still has the old, pre-"conversion" art. Conversion happened in 2007 to introduce pet customization and the NC mall. While the majority of pets were automatically converted, there were some color/pet combinations that were not - for example, Coconut JubJub or Plushie Kacheek. If you have one of these pets, it's recommended you don't convert them - they're very prized as they can't be created anymore! Unconverted pets cannot wear clothes other than their paintbrush clothes, but can wear customization items like backgrounds.

NOTE: There is currently a bug with Flash conversion, but there are some workarounds similar to those used for Flash Games.


▸ Are there any major differences between a converted pet and an unconverted pet?
Aside from the artwork and ability to wear bodily wearables, then nope! Unconverted pets can still wear Backgrounds, Foregrounds, etc. but they can't wear Static and Biology Effect zoned clothing.


▸ Will TNT ever bring back UCs?
On May 31st, 2021, TNT has announced that they are reintroducing unconverted pets (UCs) through the NC Mall (price, and exact details not mentioned).

On March 13th, 2021, TNT has announced that they are open to the possibility of implementing unconverted pets (UCs) back into the game.

jellyneo.net/?comments=13722

No, TNT will not bring back unconverted (UC) pets and has officially considered them retired. It is known that TNT do have the power to unconvert pets into their UC formes (only existing post-conversion UCs), but that is usually only done in specific, often direful, situations.

- Neopets Editorial - Issue 896 | Question 5 [link] (A further explanation and repeated message from Issue 733 Question 5)
- Neopets Editorial - Issue 733 | Question 5 [link] (As for why we won't make it work in the system, if we even could do it, it would take a LOT of time and resources, for something that we no longer support. That decision was made a long time ago, and it hasn't changed - officially, UC pets are retired.)
- Neopets Editorial - Issue 722 | Question 2 [link] (- nope, no such plans)
- Neopets Editorial - Issue 649 | Question 5 [link] (Unconverted Neopets are only available "as is" and are not supported in current or future site development.)
- Neopets Editorial - Issue 565 | Question 10 [link] (No. Non. Nicht. 没有. Geen. iie. Nej. Nu. Não)
- Neopets Editorial - Issue 511 | Question 6 [link] (There are no plans for unconverted Neopets. They are relics left over from the past, and not something we are giving any consideration to in the future.)


▸ Will TNT ever mass convert all the UCs this time?
Nope! TNT will not mass convert all the UCs on the site.

- Neopets Editorial - Issue 511 | Question 7 [link] (General Info)


▸ I recently found a UC in the pound, what should I do?
Congratulations! This is an extremely rare find, but there are a few steps you should take. First, be aware that the pet you found may have been involved in a pound transfer (PT). This is when two users trade their pets through the pound because one party is out of transfers. It's not safe, but it still happens. If someone reaches out to let you know that the pet was the result of a failed PT, it's up to you whether you want to give the pet back to them or not. According to TNT, it's now your pet fair and square.

However, you should also put in a support ticket with the name of the pet. Unfortunately, there are cheaters on Neopets who hack accounts and steal or pound pets. Putting in a support ticket allows TNT to check if that pet is from a recently compromised account. If it is from a compromised account, and you haven't let them know you found it in the pound/cleared it with them, you run the risk of being unfairly frozen. Other than that, enjoy your new pet! (And as always, if you're new to pet trading - make sure to do it on a public board and ask advice before going through with it, as some people will try to take advantage of new traders. Sad but true!)


▸ Is there a place I can check out all the active UCs pets?
You can check them all out in the following page:

Jellyneo's Unconverted Pet Preview
drsloth.com/swfs/unconverted-pets/


▸ Is there anything else I need to know about unconverted pets?
A lot of people play Neopets because they want to relive their childhood and unconverted pets might be a large factor in that. The converted variants might not have the same nostalgic feeling. Obtaining their desired unconverted pet might seem like a pipe dream, but you'll see some people who successfully achieved their goal against the odds and who cherish their dream pet to this day.

Special thanks and FAQ contributions here from thelastparticiple (Pound Basics, Pound Surfing, and Pet Trading), solisregina (Unconverted Pets), km042496 (Pound Basics and Pound Chat Games), and edgkid2 (Pound Chat Games).

Trading / Auctions FAQs

▸ Can I trade NP for NC, NC items, Pets, Services, Premium, or any other things than NP items?
You are NOT allowed to trade NP for NC, NC items, Pets, Services, Premium, nor other things than NP items.


▸ Where do I transfer large sums of NP?
Your options would be the Auction House and the Trading Post. You may bid 2 million NP per Trading Post lot. For the Auction House, you can have a 50 million starting price and a 50 million minimum increment.

Selling / Buying Related

▸ How do you sell items and what's the best place to sell them?
First off, let's get down to some basics on the places you can sell items at:

- Your Shop (Shop Wizard): Great for items priced 999,999 NP and lower.
- The Trading Post: Great for selling items in bulk and advertising items worth more than the Shop Wizard's NP limit, but has its own limit of 2m per lot.
- The Auction House: It takes an hour at minimum to process a sale, but has a monumental NP limit of a 50,000,000 (50m) NP Starting Price and 50,000,000 (50m) NP Increment. Auctions can be used for a variety of reasons, but not so much in creating quick sales.

If the item is under 999,999 NP, then you might want to throw it in your shop.

If you're trying to sell things in bulk/sets like Secret Laboratory Map pieces, then hit up the Trading Post.

If you've got a bunch of items over 999,999 NPs (Unbuyable or UB), then advertise that entire stash in a Trading Post Lot and/or toss them in the Auction House. If you don't want to deal with all the Neomails from advertising in the Auction House, then advertising only on the Trading Post is fine too.

If you want to create a sale for an item above 2,000,000 (2m) NP in pure, then the Auction House would be your go-to. Occasionally, the Trading Post will have people requesting/offering Easy-To-Sell items (ETS) such as Nerkmids, Baby Paint Brushes, etc. as NP filler value if the item is only worth slightly more than 2,000,000 (2m) NP.

If you don't want to clutter your Inventory, then making a sales Petpage or Gallery, and advertising that on the Trading / Auctions NeoBoard Chat would be a viable option if you have the energy to maintain it.


▸ How much does X cost?
There are three common methods on how to check the price of an item:

- Check the item on the Shop Wizard (or Super Shop Wizard or SSW) for the lowest or if there are any available sales listed.
- Check Jellyneo's Item Database as a possible price reference while also checking the currently available Trading Post / Auction House listings.
- Create a Price Check (PC) thread on the Trading / Auctions NeoBoard Chat.


▸ How does one buy an item that's not currently found on the Shop Wizard, Trading Post, or Auction House?
You would either want to search for the item on the Trading / Auctions NeoBoard Chat or message possible sellers in Galleries that are looking to make sales.


▸ What are item rarities and are they important?
All items have a Rarity attached to them they can determine how rare and/or valued an item can be.

Items with low rarities tend to be super common (r1-r89), but might be sought out for most Quests of Neopia, the Kadoatery, Faerie Employment Agency, and other miscellaneous activities. Not always but usually, official shops will restock these items in larger batches.

Higher rarity items at r90-r100 tend to be extremely rare and highly sought out for Gourmet Club, Jhudora/Illusen Quests, and by collectors. Official shops will only rarely stock these items (especially some of the highest rarity ones e.g. r97~r99), and usually only one will restock at a time.

The more extremely priced r100 items are really only obtained from the Wheel of Extravagance nowadays. There are also a few specific r100 items that are won as special distributions from the Neopian Times and other Creative Contests.

r101-r180s vary the most in origin and value, and r500 items are Neocash items.

Jellyneo's Item Rarity Article
jellyneo.net/?go=item_rarities_explained


▸ What is reselling and how does one get into it?
Reselling is essentially buying an item for cheap from another Neopian and selling it for a higher price. Some Neopians are willing to discount their wares, because they just want NP now and don't care for the potential profit loss.

You can get into reselling by negotiating deals or sending (hopefully) reasonable underoffers to listers on the Trading Post or Auction House (you wouldn't really want to negotiate with Shop Wizard sellers, because of how flexible selling items is there unless you're seeking bulk purchases) or by creating a "Buying X at Reseller Price" thread on the Trading / Auctions NeoBoard Chat.

NOTE: You don't want to underoffer on a clearly stable buyable (under 1m) listing, because that's pretty much an insult since the person had made the decision to put it up on the Trading Post/Auction House rather than just shove it in their shop.


▸ Am I allowed to artificially inflate an item by buying them all up and reselling them at a higher price?
While this is distasteful behavior, it is fine to do if you're the sole inflator. You are NOT allowed to collaborate with others to inflate and manipulate item prices.

Neopets Editorial - Issue 315 | Question 16 [link]

Quite often in your Editorials and rules, you have said that it is against the rules for a group of people to get together and purposely inflate items to corner a market. You state that it is okay if only one person does this by themselves, but it seems that nowadays the name of the game is "get with the group and buy up all of an item." How are people being allowed to corner markets like this when it has been stated that group inflation is against the rules? ~kalis_coraven

If you strongly believe certain players are grouping to inflate items, please, by all means, send in a detailed report about their shenanigans. Such things are very subtle, and we rely on you honest players to give us a heads up when you think your misbehaving Neo-peers are up to no good.

Also, to reiterate a past Editorial, yes, one person can buy up all the items they want. However, if they make them unbuyable and suddenly the price jumps from 99k to, say, 600k and start getting offered on expensive items, then it's considered scamming.


▸ Am I allowed to sell items on my side accounts?
You are NOT allowed to sell items on your side account. Guild Account Shops are fine as long as the shop is owned bt the Guild Leader (no account sharing), properly labeled as a Guild Account, and all funds go to Guild purposes.

- Neopets Editorial - Issue 844 | Question 4 [link] (Guild Shops Are OK with more clarification)
- Neopets Editorial - Issue 828 | Question 4 [link] (General Everything Most Recent)
- Neopets Editorial - Issue 338 | Question 9 [link] (Using Auctions to puposely bump prices of items is NOT allowed)
- Neopets Editorial - Issue 282 | Question 2 [link] (Using Auctions to puposely bump prices of items is NOT allowed)
- Neopets Editorial - Issue 229 | Question 11 [link] (General Basics Covered + Guild Shops Are OK)

Restocking Related

▸ What is Restocking and how does it work?
Restocking is the act of staking out official Neopets shops to hopefully grab some expensive items for cheap to resell them to other users over at shop, the Trading Post, and/or the Auction House.

It can be pretty intimidating at first, but once you choose a shop of your liking, learn the profitable (and unprofitable aka "bait") items of the shop, and undergo the experience of buying those items quickly, you'll get a hang of Restocking in no time.


▸ How much NP do I need before I start Restocking?
That depends on where you want to start restocking, but having 50k-100k certainly helps for most of the common beginner to intermediate-level shops.

Restocking Articles
jellyneo.net/?go=restocking
jellyneo.net/?go=shopsdirectory
thedailyneopets.com/articles/restocking
sunnyneo.com/games/stock/index.php
/~Sanskrits (Restocking Guide)


▸ What are the Restocking Account Age Restrictions?
There exists an account age limitatation to determine what restockable items you can see.

Age of Account
