▸ What are some good shops to restock at?
That varies on your account and own capabilities. Kayla's Potionery (73), Food Shop (1), Magical Book Shop (7), Spooky Foods (30), Lost Desert Medicine (85), and the Pharmacy (13) are considered to be great beginner shops due to their stocking of profitable items in larger batches. Faerie Quest and Faerie Employment Agency items also tend to be quick-selling small profits.

The most profitable, yet most competitive shops include Kauvara's Magic Shop (2), Neopian Post Office (58), Collectable Coins (68), Collectable Sea Shells (86), and Collectable Cards (8). Morphing Potions and collectibles are extremely sought after, and tend to have the most expensive r99 items around.

Intermediate-level shops include Tyrannian Weaponry (45), Toy Shop (3), Faerie Foods (39), Uni's Clothing (4), and Neopian Gift Shop (17).


▸ What is a Restock Ban?
A Restock Ban is when all the official shops decide that you've had enough of restocking for a specific amount time, during which you won't be able to see any items in any official shop. They're completely normal/generally random and they can last for up to 24 hours if you're really unlucky.


▸ How many shops should I restock at a time?
That's a personal choice. The more shops you restock at a time, the higher the chance you have at being restock banned, but refreshing only one shop can be pretty boring for some people.


▸ Why did all the items in the offical shops just suddenly disappear?
That's what we call a Clear. Shops automatically "clear" out items at random intervals, so that new items can restock!

If you think there's a clear or you're shop banned, you can do the following:
A. Check other shops you wouldn't normally visit for an SWI (Shop With Items).
B. If you had a shop tab open with stock before the clear, then try to buy an item. If it sends you to the haggle screen rather than a sold out screen, then you're restock banned.
C. Ask other RSers for an SWI to verify if you're restock banned or not.
D. Check on a side account for an SWI (DO NOT RESTOCK ON SIDE ACCOUNTS)


▸ Why is there nothing good appearing? How long does it take for X appear?
Restocks and clears are all random.

Restocking is all about having patience for shops to restock, being quick enough to make the haggle, and then having the patience again to sell. It can take minutes to hours for shops to restock/clear and it's completely up to chance if specific items appear at all (the higher the rarity index, the rarer the item). Most of the time shops will stock nothing but junk but that won't stop us from trying.


▸ Am I allowed to Restock on side accounts?
You are NOT allowed to restock on side accounts. Even if you get restock banned on your main account, you are not allowed to go onto a side account to continue restocking.

- Neopets Editorial - Issue 221 | Question 2 [link] (Restocking on sides is NOT allowed)


▸ Am I allowed to block certain junk items/item images from appearing on my screen in order to make it easier to see profitable items?
You are NOT allowed to block items/item images from appearing on your screen, whether through third-party tools or not. That is considered cheating and a freezable offense.

- Neopets Editorial - Issue 275 | Question 10 [link] (blocking images for restocking is NOT allowed)
- Neopets Editorial - Issue 230 | Bottom PSA [link] (AdBlock is OKAY to block Ads only)


▸ Does "Neopian Inflation is currently at X.XX%" mean anything?
It factors into the estimated cost a shop stocks at an item at, but since that never changes it doesn't matter anymore. It's really just flavour text nowadays.


▸ Is there anything else I need to know about Restocking?
If you have any questions about Restocking or want to hang out with other Restockers, don't hesitate to visit the Trading / Auctions NeoBoard Chat or Premium NeoBoard Chat (Premium only) for that.

Shop Wizard Related

▸ What is the Shop Wizard?
The Shop Wizard is a place where Neopians can look up items from Neopian usershops. Searching for items is free of charge, but be aware of its limitations and mechanics.

Shop Wizard Articles
jellyneo.net/?go=shopwiz
thedailyneopets.com/articles/shop-wizard


▸ Why does the Shop Wizard always show me the same people?
The Shop Wizard randomly searches through many groups of shops depending on the first letter of the user's UN, so you might have to resubmit the search request in order to get a different selection of usershops.

The following grouped UNs by the first letter of UN are:

A, N, 0 (zero)
B, O, 1
C, P, 2
D, Q, 3
E, R, 4
F, S, 5
G, T, 6
H, U, 7
I, V, 8
J, W, 9
K, X, _
L, Y
M, Z


▸ What is a Shop Wizard ban?
A Shop Wizard ban is when you hit the limit of 360 searches within the current hour. The search counter resets at the top of the next hour.


▸ Is there a way to search for a specific item that shares the same name as other items (like Treasure Maps)?
Unfortunately, if an item shares the same exact name with another item, you cannot specify which of the multiple variants to search for. The Shop Wizard will select one at random.


▸ I clicked on a Frozen Shop. Why doesn't TNT remove these?
TNT does take notice of Frozen Shops awhile after they've been spotted and will usually remove them within a week or so.


▸ How often should I reprice my usershop?
That is up to you to decide, but updating your shop prices every week or so doesn't hurt. You might have some competition when lowering your prices, but you also need patience when selling your items even if you have the lowest price on the Shop Wizard.


▸ What does Piccy mean?
That's just a cutesy way of TNT saying picture.


▸ Are Neopets Malls still a thing?
Despite the Neopian Marketplace being broken, Neopets Malls are indeed still a thing! Neopets Malls are usually run by Guilds and/or Neopians on the Shop Ads NeoBoard Chat.


▸ Is there anything else I need to know about the Shop Wizard?
When pricing your shop, you would want to avoid leaving your price boxes blank or entering special characters (zeroes are fine). This because there is a bug that can shift the prices of your items to the item next to it. In the event this occurs, you should consider immediately select the Remove All box in the bottom of the page to prevent your items from potentially being sold at the wrong prices.

Trading Post Related

▸ What is the Trading Post?
The Trading Post is a place where Neopians can trade their items and NP with other Neopians. There is no fee for listing items nor placing offers. Additionally, players can create a small description of their desired offers in their listings.


▸ Is there a limit on how many Trading Post Lots I can have?
All Neopians start off with a limit of 10 listings. If your account is 36 months or older, then you are allowed to create 15 listings.

Trading Post Articles
jellyneo.net/?go=trading_post
thedailyneopets.com/articles/trading-post-tips
Trading Post Help

▸ Why can't I post a description in my Trading Post lot?
If you are unable to create a description in your Trading Post lot, then the reason could mean one of the following:
- You're under 13.
- Your account was silenced.


▸ Is there a limit of how many Neopoints I can put in a Trading Post lot?
The Trading Post limit is 2,000,000 (2m) NP per offer.


▸ Is there a limit of how many Trading Post lots I can accept/be accepted for?
Nerkmids (~75k) and Baby Paint Brushes (600k) are often used as item currency to get around the NP limit. You can also ask the lister to place the item in a one-bid Auction (NF Auction is the safest).


▸ Is there a limit on how many individual Trading Post lots I can accept an offer on/have my offers accepted on?
There are no limits, but note that you can only accept one offer per individual lot.


▸ What is a Split Trade and are they allowed?
Split Trades are when a lister requests the bidder to place two offers: one on their main listing and another on a junk item listing in order to effectively bypass the 2m NP limit on a singular lot. They are discouraged due to the high possibility of being scammed, but they also fine if you are trading with a person you trust.


▸ I traded with someone else but somehow, one of us did not get their end of the trade. What can we do?
If for some reason the Trading Posts bugs out and does not provide one side with their end of the trade, then send in a support ticket to TNT at the official FAQ. Make sure to grab the Lot and Offer Number, and mention both recipients of the trade.


▸ Is there a way I can search for a specific item with the same name of another item?
Unfortunately, if an item shares the same exact name with another item, you cannot specify which of the multiple variants to search for.


▸ I see some listers with a bunch of the same high-end themed items. Are they doing something malicious?
Probably not, they are most likely a reseller (Paint Brushes, Secret Lab Maps, random r101-180s) and/or avid restocker (r95-r99 Stamps, Morphing Potions, Gourmets, Collectible Cards, etc.).


▸ Is there anything else I need to know about the Trading Post?
Trading Post lots have an expiration date of two weeks, so it doesn't hurt to manually take them down and repost them every once in awhile to refresh the timer, if your items have been there for long.

It is fairly common for Neopians to forget about their lots and have them expire since you are not sent any notifications when it happens. Items from expired lots are placed back in your Inventory like any other item, where they are vulnerable to various Random Event-related mishaps.

Auction House Related

▸ What is the Auction House?
The Auction House is a place where Neopians can sell items by listing them for a specified amount of time and buy items by openly competing with other Neopians. Auctioned items are usually listed below their usual Trading Post prices and increment with every bid. Placing items up for auction is free of charge.


▸ Is there a limit on how many Auctioned Items I can have?
You can only have 8 auctioned items at a time.

Auction House Articles
jellyneo.net/?go=auctions
thedailyneopets.com/articles/auctions
Auction-Related Help


▸ What's the NP limit for the Auction House?
The maximum starting price is 50,000,000 (50m) NP and the maximum minimum increment is also 50,000,000 (50m) NP.


▸ How long does it take for an Auction House listing to go through?
It should only take a few minutes for the listing to process, but rarely, the Auction House will become "stuck" in processing and items and NP may be held in limbo for hours or even days. TNT will eventually take notice and fix the issue, so your items and NP will ultimately go through safely, but it can be an annoying wait whenever this happens.


▸ I got outbid, but do I get my Neopoints back?
In the event you lose the Auction, your Neopoints will be returned once the listing is closed and processed.


▸ Is there a way I can cancel my offer in the Auction House?
Auction offers are finalized once the bid has been placed. You are not entitled to a refund unless it was a blatant scam (Paint Brush Plushies for their Non-Plushie prices), in which case it is a reportable offense and you should notify TNT as soon as possible.

- Neopets Editorial - Issue 306 | Question 3 [link] (General Info)


▸ Am I allowed to do Auctions with my side accounts?
You are NOT allowed to create Auction lots on your side accounts for the sole purpose of creating sales or to manipulate the prices of items. Transferring NP on the other hand is fine, but the Trading Post is preferred over the Auction House for that.

- Neopets Editorial - Issue 907 | Question 4 [link] (Profiting on sides is NOT allowed)
- Neopets Editorial - Issue 338 | Question 9 [link] (Bidding on sides to inflate prices is NOT allowed)
- Neopets Editorial - Issue 282 | Question 2 [link] (Bidding on sides to inflate prices is NOT allowed)


▸ Is there some sort indicator to know when an Auction ends exactly?
Nope, you'll have to rely on yourself (or the lister if it was posted on the NeoBoards, Guilds, etc.) to know the exact time on when an auction ends. You could stalk the main Auction House page as it shows the approximate ending time for auctions that are due to end soon, but the processing time isn't always consistent.


▸ I accidentally mispriced my Auctioned item. Am I allowed to ask for help to bump it up and get the person to return it back to me?
You are allowed to ask the NeoBoards to see if there might be people generous to help you out although do know that the winner is not obliged to return the item to you nor at the price they won the item at.


▸ What's a Fun Auction?
A Fun Auction is when a Neopian creates a listing of an expensive item at an extremely low price (i.e. 1 NP Starting Bid & 1 NP Increment Nerkmid, Paint Brushes, etc.). The Neopian is not expecting to make a profit, because they want to have a fun competition on who can who outbid the other person.


▸ What are Dr. Sloth Auctions?
Dr. Sloth Auctions were an old method of reintroducing rare and retired items back to the site. TNT would create a fake staff account based off a popular Neopian character (i.e. Dr_Sloth) and auction rare items such as Wock Til You Drop Stamp, Coltzan Stamp, etc.


▸ Is there anything else I need to know about the Auction House?
If you're unsure about or don't remember how to put up an Auction listing, it doesn't hurt to put up a junk item to test run your actual item in question. Also, you can use commas when creating your Auction House listing, if you're afraid that you'll miss out a zero. Note that the first bid on your auction is the Starting Price + Minimum Increment, so if your Starting Price is set at 100,000 NP and your Minimum Increment is 50,000 NP, the first bid is required to be at least 150,000 NP.

Faerieland Employment Agency Related

▸ What is the Faerieland Employment Agency?
The Faerieland Employment Agency (or FEA) is a place where you are able to complete jobs in exchange for Neopoints, and is located on the left fringe of Faerie City in Faerieland.

JN's Faerieland Employment Agency Article
jellyneo.net/?go=employment


▸ What is a Faerieland Employment Agency job?
There are listings in the Faerieland Employment Agency that you can apply for asking you to find between 2 to 6 of a certain r2-r69 item within a specified time and given a Neopoints reward.


▸ Why apply for a Faerieland Employment Agency job?
Some reasons include making Neopoints, beating others in getting the good jobs or personal satisfaction seeing the job counter increase on your pet's lookup. There is also a rankings leaderboard for the top 100 pets to recognise those who have put in the most effort.


▸ Can you lose Neopoints from Faerieland Employment Agency jobs?
Not all jobs are profitable. There will be instances where the items will cost more than you will gain from the job reward. It is therefore beneficial to have an estimate of how much the items will cost and what the payout will be before you apply if you want to make Neopoints. However, you can always decline the job for a penalty of 200 NP within the allotted time if you do not want to finish the job and want to avoid it being counted as a failure on your pet's lookup.


▸ How can you apply for a Faerieland Employment Agency job?
There are 2 types of listings: basic jobs which do not require a job coupon and super jobs which will ask for a minimum coupon type. Each time you get accepted for a super job, your job coupon will get downgraded to a lower level. You can go through the listings of both types at the top of the page. The newer listing will appear at the end and oldest ones at the front. The best jobs will appear near the back as they will only be up for a short time before being taken by someone. There is no set time (similar to restocking) for when new listing will appear so you will need to refresh periodically to find the best jobs. Once you find one to your liking, then click on the "Apply for this Job" link.


▸ How do you complete a Faerieland Employment Agency job?
Once you apply for a job, there will be a confirmation whether you have gotten it or if it has been taken up by someone else. If you get the job then you can search for your items yourself using either the Shop Wizard or Super Shop Wizard, unlike faerie quests. The confirmation page will have a link for you to turn your items in so you should try to buy your items in a different tab or window for convenience. You can also return your items through visiting the status page and clicking on your current job if you don't have the page open.


▸ How many Faerieland Employment Agency jobs can you do a day?
5 jobs. You can get locked out before this by being told to come back tomorrow if you do them in quick succession or after completing your 4th of the day. This can last for up to 10 minutes, but you will eventually be able to apply again until you have completed 5 in total for that day.


▸ How much can you earn from Faerieland Employment Agency jobs?
How much you will earn is dependent on the base reward and how fast you complete the job in relation to the allotted time. As long as you complete the job in time then you will get the base reward amount as a minimum. There is an additional 25% bonus of the base reward on top if you complete the job within a quarter of the time. The extra amount given is dependent on the time taken. For example, if you take 0 seconds (by getting all the items before being accepted for the job) then you will always get the full bonus (1.25x of the base reward) whereas taking exactly 1/4 of the time will net you just the base reward. This is on a sliding scale so it is better to complete the job as quickly as possible to get a higher bonus even if you have a lot of time.


▸ What are the base payouts for Faerieland Employment Agency jobs?
Basic Jobs: less than 10k NP

Super Jobs
Green Job: 3-3.5k NP (lowest ranked job)
Blue Job: 4.5-5k NP
Red Job: 9-10k NP
Silver Job: 28-30k NP
Gold Job: 50-60k NP
Purple Job: 75-80k NP
Pink Job: 99-100k NP
Green Brightvale Job: 20-25k NP
Bronze Brightvale Job: 40-45k NP
Silver Brightvale Job: 60-70k NP
Gold Brightvale Job: 80-100k NP (highest ranked job)

NOTE: Higher-leveled job coupons can be used to apply for lower-leveled jobs, and there is a cap of 100,000 NP (after bonus) per job.


▸ Are job coupons worth it?
Not if you are doing the 3 lowest job tiers as the base payouts of those overlap with basic jobs, so you can receive similar rewards without using a coupon at all. As for the rest, the prices of job coupons fluctuate back and forth so you will need to decide whether the Neopoints gained is greater than the cost of the job coupon being downgraded one level. You do not have to apply for the same job type as your job coupon so you need to take into consideration if you can get a higher return with a lower ranked job. Be sure when using them because your job coupon will still be downgraded if you decline or do not finish the job.


▸ Where does one obtain Job Coupons?
Job Coupons can be obtained from the following:
- Wheel of Knowledge (Brighvale Coupons only)
- Wheel of Extravagance (All)
- Shop Wizard / Trading Post / Auction House (All)


▸ Where are all the Pink jobs?
Pink jobs are extremely rare. Most people with Pink Job Coupons would sell them directly.

Special thanks and FAQ contributions here from d0du0 (FEA).

Rare Item Code / Onsite Related

▸ What Neopets Merchandise gives out the Space Faerie challenger? I just want the avatar.
A broad listing of Neopets Merchandise can be found here, but not all of those will provide a code.

For other products that can reward the Space Faerie challenger are: old Neocash Mystery Capsules Codes, Fun Pak Codes, Comic-Con Codes, What's Your Passion Jewelry codes, Geekify Inc. codes (not all of their merchandise have codes), Overpowered Codes, etc.

TCG Codes, Neocash Codes, and Promotional Rare Item Codes do not reward the Space Faerie challenger.

You could try the Avatars/NeoSignatures NeoBoard to ask other Neopians for a Space Faerie Code for free. Some people do genuinely give out codes on the Neoboards to other users who can't purchase one for themselves (usually because the merchandise isn't sold in their country). However, these people won't ask you to pay them for the code, mainly because asking for such payment is against Neopets' rules. Although, it is courtesy to send the rewarded items to the gifter.


▸ Where do I redeem Virtual Prize Codes?
If you are redeeming TCG Codes, then you would visit Neopets TCG Prize Code Redemption.
If you are redeeming Neocash Codes, then you would visit the Redeem NC Page.
If you are redeeming anything else, then refer to the Grundo Warehouse.

As of 2020, you can no longer redeem Keyquest Codes, Puzzle Adventure Codes, Quizara's Curse Codes, and Pocket Neopets Codes.

As of 2021, you need to enable Flash to redeem certain codes.


▸ What can I get from redeeming Virtual Prize Codes?
That varies on type of code.
- Neocash Codes rewards Neocash to purchase items from the NC Mall. Extra items can be found here:
jellyneo.net/?go=nc_mall&page=obtaining_neocash
- TCG Codes can award items from here (/~Ravenorneo).
- While these items varies on its origin, Grundo Warehouse items are found here:
https://items.jellyneo.net/search/?scat[]=5
- Keyquest Codes (obsolete) awarded items from here:
items.jellyneo.net/search/?scat[]=46
- Puzzle Adventure Codes (obsolete) awarded a site theme and items from here:
items.jellyneo.net/search/?description=Puzzle+Adventure
- Quizara's Curse Codes (obsolete) awarded a site theme and items from here:
items.jellyneo.net/search/?description=Quizaras+Curse


▸ Are Neocash Cards and Rare Item Codes considered Merchandise?
Short answer, yes. Official real-world Neopets products, such as Neocash Cards and Rare Item Codes, are fine to be resold. Here's TNT's response:

Neopets Editorial - Issue 610 | Question 3 [link]

Hi, TNT! I have an odd question for you.... about commissions. Now, I know taking them in exchange for anything on Neopets is against the rules, as is doing commissions with Neopets characters. However... what about real-life merchandise? I'm the sort that's willing to take trades, and I was wondering: could someone pay me in Neopets plushies? What about rare item codes, or Neocash? (the cards, not actual on-site NC items) I mean, people sell the item codes on ebay all the time, so wouldn't that be okay? As far as NC cards go, if I'm just going to buy them anyway, why not save a step? Would these be against the Terms & Conditions because they give things on the site itself? I mean, obviously, it still wouldn't be okay to do a commission OF Neopets, but in exchange for merchandise, where do you guys stand? (please remove my UN) ~UN removed

As you said, as long as you aren't taking commissions of Neopets intellectual property, you're welcome to trade or sell your real-world merchandise however you'd like. According to Lawyerbot: "Trading plushies, rare item codes, NC cards, etc. for real life merchandise is fine. I once traded my brother's turtle to a friend for a Shadow Uni Plushie".

Overpowered Related

▸ So what is Overpowered and what happened to them?
On April 19th, 2018, Overpowered was a revival of Neopets merchandise for a short period of time. They sold keychains which provided Space Faerie Codes and onsite rewards such as toys, wearables, and other fun goodies. Although some can say that the company was painted with Scritchy Sketchy Paint Brush.

- Pre-orders were delayed or for the most part, never delivered.
- An E-Mail was sent with them begging users to purchase more pre-orders with the promise of new merchandise.
- After a year, Overpowered had gone out of business. Their website has been decommissioned, and the domain name was sold to a third party that is now displaying not family-friendly content. We highly recommend not seeking out the current website.

On November 13th, 2019, TNT had announced to split from Overpowered:

We have an announcement to make. We'd like to let everyone know that we are no longer affiliated with Overpowered. We are genuinely sorry many of you did not receive your items and are doing our best to compensate you. However, we are honoring codes and you will be able to redeem them on our website if you have any. We will take this as a learning experience for any future endeavors. Thank you!


▸ I'm late, but can I still get compensated for not getting my Overpowered merch?
From July 30th, 2019 to August 20th, 2019, TNT provided onsite compensation for the unfulfilled Overpowered merchandise orders through their social media. While they have closed this sort of support submissions through their social medias, it would probably be best to submit a ticket through the official FAQ if you still wish to be compensated. Do keep in mind to have the necessary information while requesting support.


▸ Will TNT ever rerelease Overpowered on-site item prizes?
Fortunately, TNT has rereleased some of the Overpowered on-site item prizes through their 20th Anniversary Merchandise Test! It is a rare occasion where TNT rereleases Rare Item Code prizes.

Special thanks and FAQ contributions here from Josh (RICs).

Other FAQs

Flash Related

▸ Why isn't anything loading? It's not lag, but I just cannot see the maps nor play the games? IS THIS THE FLASH DYING I HAVE HEARD SO MUCH OF???
You most likely will need to Allow Flash if you still have Adobe Flash and a browser that allows it. This can be done by clicking the "i" next to your address bar and changing the settings to "Allow." If that doesn't work, try clearing your cache and cookies.

As for the future of Flash Support, TNT has announced that they are working it and you can see their progress over at the Release Notes.

Neopets Editorial - Issue 861 | Question 1 [link]

Special serious announcement from Scrappidoodledandy!

Hey Neopians!

Scrappy here to give you a little update on what's going on here in Neopia. There's a lot of rumors and speculations going around, so I want to be very upfront with you guys on what our plans are at the moment for moving our lovely home to mobile.

As we are all aware, all this flash has got to go. The largest part of that being the customization that allows us to make our Neopets look all spiffy. We're currently working on moving all the art over and are hoping to get a beta version out to you guys early this summer. Once that is up and running you will be able to customize your lovely pets on any browser at any time!

Another topic of discussion here is all our games. The plan right now is to move these over in batches, starting with about 10 games and moving more from there. We want to be able to bring over all of them with time but starting small will be quicker and let us take your guys feedback moving forward!

Of course, there have been other parts moving as I'm sure you all have noticed, such as the maps and other events using flash. We are hoping to get all these converted as soon as we can, focusing around the maps first and foremost then moving onto the other pieces from there.

I am also aware there have been many mentions of an app and while that is not out of the picture, we have decided to focus on moving away from flash and make that our top priority first. Along with moving away from flash, we are making a mobile-friendly browser version to improve the user experience when on a mobile device. This is another area we will want to release test versions as soon as we can and get all your feedback to improve moving forward.

Those are most of the updates for right now! I wanted to be very upfront with you guys here because since this is all to improve your experience, we want to make sure we can get your feedback and let that guide us each step of the way! I will be setting up a time soon to jump on the boards, so we can have a more open discussion about this as well but wanted to start with an update here!

As always, stay cool Neopians!

-Scrappy

This is a quick list of site features that are confirmed to be currently down, broken, or not available anymore:

- Almost Abandoned Attic (not restocking)
- Invasion of Meridell
- Defenders of Neopia (and DoN avatars)
- Punchbag Sid (and the avatar)
- Game High Scores Table not resetting (semi-irregular resets)
- Password Reset (CAPTCHA image can be glitchy)
- Shockwave game issues
- AdverVideo
- Neovision
- World Challenges
- Bilge Dice


▸ The textbox to reply to a NeoMail has vanished! What do I do?
You would want to refresh the page until the textbox comes back. If that does not work, then you can switch to Plain Text Neomail over at your Preferences to prevent the issue from happening frequently.


▸ How can I get TNT's attention on _____?
If it's a content suggestion, request, or inquiry, then I'd check out the Editorial or Ideas / Suggestions NeoBoards Chat.

If it's a Beauty Contest or Art Gallery related inquiry, then I would first check out if there's a TNT thread in Art NeoBoard Chat, then the Editorial.

If it's about a type of abuse, then I would send an Abuse Report.

For all and all else, submit a ticket through the official FAQ and also post your ticket number on the Highway to Help thread in the Help NeoBoard Chat.


▸ Why does my account say I was last active _____? I never leave the site.
Log out and log back in to fix this issue.


▸ Why am I always logged out of the NC Mall when I'm logged in everywhere else?
Log out and then log in through the NC Mall to fix this issue.

Account Safety

▸ Do I really need a PIN?
Pins are absolutely necessary. You don't need to put a pin on everything. They are not only used for account safety, but pins can play a key role as vital information for account retrieval if you happen to need to access your account through ticket support.


▸ How often should I change my password/pin?
You should change your password/pin every 4-6 months or so.

NOTE: If you haven't changed your password/pin prior 2016, I would advise you would immediately do so.


▸ What are the elements of a strong/weak password?
The characteristics of a STRONG password include:
- Having over 14 characters
- Having uppercase and lowercase letters
- Having numbers
- Having special characters (!, #, $, %, etc. though do not use less/greater than signs, as that can be problematic)

The characteristics of a WEAK password include:
- Using common personal identifiable information (Name, BDay, etc.)
- Short passwords
- Keyboard series and repeats (qwerty, 12345, aaaaa, etc.)
- Using common and lazy phrases like the word "password".


▸ Is sharing accounts and/or passwords really that bad or against the rules?
YES, IT IS BAD. This is not only a danger to your account, but it is also a freezable offense.

Neopets Terms of Use
10. Do Not Share Your Account


▸ I just saw someone link off-site. Is it safe to follow the link?
Aside from offical fan-sites (which are okay), do NOT go to those unofficial sites. Linking (or even partly mentioning) off-site links is a warnable/freezable offense, and you would want to protect yourself from phishing attacks.

Community - Fan-Site Directory
Fan-Site Directory Link


▸ What is this images50 pop-up and why is asking for my information?
That is Neopets's back image server and do NOT enter your information in it. There have been reports of people's accounts getting frozen for doing so.


▸ Are there any dangers of using a public or different computer/Wi-Fi location to play Neopets?
It should be safe to play Neopets at a different computer/Wi-Fi location. Just remember to log out afterwards if it is a public device.


▸ Am I in any danger if my family also plays Neopets with the same computer/Wi-Fi location?
You should be fine. TNT can tell and understand that families play Neopets too.

Neopets Editorial - Issue 908 | Question 2 [link]

Hi TNT!! My younger sister plays Neopets and enjoys your site! I recently moved in with her and was wondering if I'm still able to play my games and dailies when using her laptop? I wasn't sure what your rules are for this. ~~kristytempy

Of course you can both continue playing! We know a lot of our members do share an IP or even a computer with family members who also play. Just continue to play the same way you always have. :)


▸ Someone just randomly gifted me some items / wanted to adopt me a really cool pet. Do I take it?
You do NOT want to accept random gifts from shady/shell-looking accounts. If the goods happen to be from an illegitimate source, you might be frozen for being complicit in rulebreaking. If it's too good to be true, then it probably is risky.


▸ Someone just told me to check out their userlookup/petlookup/petpage, but their account looks pretty empty. Am I in any danger?
In most cases, probably not, but you do NOT want to visit user/pet lookups or petpages from shady/shell-looking accounts. When in doubt, you can always just log out and clear your cookies to prevent hidden malicious activity.


▸ Do you have any other tips about keeping my account secure?
There are topics that we cannot discuss in this petpage due to filters, but I would read over the following guides for more information on protecting your account:

Jellyneo's Account Safety Articles
jellyneo.net/?go=safety (Neopets Account Safety)
jellyneo.net/?go=scams (Neopets Scams)

TDN's Account Safety Articles
thedailyneopets.com/articles/neopets-scams (Protect Yourself from Scams)
thedailyneopets.com/articles/security (Password Security)
thedailyneopets.com/articles/freezing-help (Prevent Getting Frozen)

Bot Prevention Related

▸ What are all these CAPTCHAs I'm seeing on Userlookups and Pet Userlookups?
CAPTCHAs are a security feature and bot prevention system. You have to complete a CAPTCHA every time you want to view a Userlookup or Pet Userlookup, and they will also appear in various Altador Cup games.


▸ Is there a way to bypass Userlookup and Pet Userlookup CAPTCHAs?
No, and that would defeat the purpose of having CAPTCHAs in the first place.


▸ What is this StackPath?
StackPath is another security feature and bot prevention system that was implemented to prevent malicious activity on the site. However, it will inadvertently block casual players from their usual activities from time to time. Thankfully, this is not as frequent as you'd think (probably a few days every month or so).


▸ I got hit by StackPath out of nowhere and it won't allow me to return to the site. What can I do to fix this?
You would want to clear your cookies on the site. Don't be alarmed if you happen to be logged out afterwards, but if this doesn't work, then I would suggest sending a ticket to the official FAQ for support.


▸ Why doesn't Neopets have a 2FA in this day and age?
TNT is planning to add additional account security measures in the near future (such as 2FA).

Neopets Editorial - Issue 873 | Question 1 [link]

Are you guys still working on 2-factor authentication? We're all desperate for it! ~~welikedots

The first step is to switch over to HTTPS. We're working on that. 2-factor authentication is something we'd like to take up after that, so no, we aren't working on it at the moment.


▸ Is there anything else I need to know about Bot Prevention?
As annoying CAPTCHAs and StackPath can be, it's important to have patience with these things. Neopets has implemented them for the protection of its members, and in the future we'll have 2-factor authentication to strengthen our account security.

Special thanks and FAQ contributions here from riparu (Account Safety).
